greately aggreue encrease payne dampnacyon hys fayth proued playne false faythlesse worlde se ryally runneth forth prayse though proued trew tyndale thys fayth knowlege euerlastynge lyfe thys borne newe made sonnes god obteyne forgyuenesse synnes translated deth lyfe wrath god vnto hys loue fauour thys fayth mother trouth bryngeth wy h spyryte truth whyche spyryte purgeth v sy e euyn lye errour noysome hurt ull thys f yth fundacyon layde apostle prophetes whereon paull sayth ephe bylte therby howseholde god thys fayth rocke wheron cryste bylte hys congregacyon lo prayse hath made thys fayth feleth folke sholde nede good workes calleth euerlastyng lyfe come bare knowlege fayth shall take away v respecte regarde deseruynge rewarde thanke rather good wurkes yf men myght haue suche respecte greate parell leste men wolde fall greate parell se none consyderynge well taught put proude confydence referre thanke god whose helpe grace wote ye well good man deny lacke suche wurkes men shall dampned cryst sayth hym selfe gospell matt harde good nature god beynge redy rewarde punysshe wolde punysshe v lackynge rewarde v hauynge namely syth hym selfe sayth gospell matt shall gyue men heuen theyr almoyse ded tyndale denyeth tone denyeth tother wyth fonde glose wyll auoyde gospell goo boldely forth wyth hys fayth boste saye thys fayth knowlege euerlastynge lyfe faythfull folke wyll saye agayne thys fayth knowlege y euerlastynge deth thys fayth hath luther frere huskyn bothe yet farre euerlastynge lyfe bysyde abomynable heresye selfe agaynste regarde good wurkes agreed bylyefe concernynge sacrament awter tone byleuynge brede tother thyng loweth ellys brede false bothe twayne tyndale foloweth falser bothe thys fayth delyuereth fro lye besydes yt bothe tyndale wyth byleue yf lye lawfull monkes freres breke theyr vowed chastyte runne wedde nonnes whyche poynt false fayth y parte fundacyon apostle byelded vppon saynt poule preched contrary sayeng vowed wydowes wyllynge wedde shold haue dampnacyon cause frustrated broken theyr forma fayth timoth wytte theyr fayth gyuen god theyr vowe abstynence carnall knowlege man agaynste whyche fayth wolde wedde geue seconde fayth vnto man maryage goth tindale forth wyth hys tale wolde seme proue trew scrypture tyndale cryste asked hys apostle matth toke hym peter wered sayenge say thou arte cryste sonne lyuynge god arte come thys worlde byleue thou arte promysed vnto abraham shulde come blesse v delyuer v peter yet wyste meanes opened thorow world thorow offeryng body blo e necessary euery wyse reder marke well consyder cause purpose tyndale bryngyng thys confessyon saynt peter fayth sayde thou arte cryste sonne lyuynge god arte comen thys worlde ye shall vnderstande tyndale hys mayster marten hys felowys myche fallen ryght bylyef many great artycles fayth consyderynge wyth slender prouys tyndale bryngeth hys parte therto playnely reproueth euery good crysten man yt care hath hys owne soule wylbe sore afrayed put iuperdye dampnacyon fallynge poynt fayth crystes hole catholyke chyrche worde fonde wedded frere fonde felow hys deuyseth take waye fere make n byleue leste wyse man byleue thynge peter confessed suffyseth ynough saluacyon though byleue forther artycles besyde thus farre suffyseth hym make folke lesse aferde draw towarde hym bryngynge v onys farre forward wyll forther purpose say onely man bounden vppon damnacyon byleue forther dampnable thynges byleue thynges neyther auayleth hurteth byleue therfore wysdome stay well selfe begynnynge tyndale sayth haue fyrste boke shewed many thynges agaynst dyuerse sacramentes whych sayth dedely synne byleue putteth fayth inough fayth saynt peter cofessed hys chapyter answered thy boke thys worke whyther apostle lefte thynge vnwryten necessary saluacyon sayth byleue byleue assumpcyon lady perpetuall virginyte many suche mo bylyefe hystory nothynge doth perteyne vnto saluacyon hereafter chapyter crysten man erre maye yet erre chapyter sayth crysten men erre thynge sholde agaynst promyses whyche cryste thynges theyr errours vnto dampnacyon though neuer greate wherof putteth ensample perpetuall vyrginyte lady bylyefe wherof sayth man beynge ledde ignoraunce wordes gospell byleue perpetuall vyrgyne myght case lacke contrary techynge dye mysse bylyefe yet take none harme therby bycause hurteth redemcyon crystes bloude though none cryste sayth tyndale therfore ne er saued n yther yet lesse though suche lyke hundreth p keth mannes fayth cryste myghte erre yet neuer lesse saued though contrary wryten gospell lo haue welbeloued reader thynge letted partely repete agayne hys wordes wryten hys chapyter partely anticypate hys wordes wryten hys othe chapyter whyche wordes hys haue bothe place taken thys entent partely haue partely shall touch theyr owne proper place yet ye sholde se hole somme effecte thys tale concernynge fayth byfore face layed gether whyche draweth peces pulleth sondry partes bycause wolde hys wyll fayne stele awaye v darke leue v wythout playne perceyuynge hys vngracyous mynde haue layed effecte hys hole opynyon together towchynge fayth sauyng hys onely dyfference dyuysyon hystorycall fayth felynge fayth shall reserue vnto hys proper place shall lytell examyne thys fayth ye may loke theron lyght se whyther suffycyent saluacyon fyrste thys fayth saynt peter confessed neuer worde purgatory dowte tyndale redeth thys worde wyll well merely laugh therat saye nedeth fayth wyll saye wyll put quenche fyre purgatory clene wyll aske hym wyll laugh fyre hell fyre thynge spoken co fessyon neyther myghte confessyon wene well inough none hell tyndale wyll saye nay muste nedes byleue thynge whyche cryste sonne lyuynge god comen worlde redeme mankynde muste nedes hell therfore peter confessyon includeth necessyte bylyefe hell answere tyndale agayne therin necessyte peter myghte byleue tyme worde hys confessyon crystes comynge onely redeme v hell losse heuyn whyche myght thynke peraduenture mankynde bannysshed vnto suche place limbus patrum though payne yet suspyrynge syghynge syghte god ioy heuen suche estate chyldren lyue dye vnbaptysed whyche though entre heuyn bycause dye chyldren wrath vnreconcyled yet mercyfull anger god dreueth downe sensyble payne felynge infernall fyre thys fayth myghte perad enture ynte peter haue thynge spoken confessed fayth ye myghte haue therwyth also bylyefe actuall synnes men punysshed thys lyfe lesse whyle lenger yet none euerlastyngly euery man length brought vnto peace reste though neuer man blesse heuen onely crystes commyng thus myghte saynte peter haue rather bylyefe purgatory hell worde mencyoned hys confessyon wherin confesseth bylyefe eyther saynte peter also nothynge confessed crystes passyon descencyon hell resurreccyon hys ascensyon whyche thynges onely pryncypall poyntes fayth also goddes promyse specyally dependeth vppon unto whyche promyses tyndale restrayneth necessary fayth trouth tyndale restrayneth therin sore bounden byleue holy goste equale ye father sonne yt promyse made vnto v yet bounden byleue trewth wherof also nothynge spoken peter confessed fayth therfore yt wyll harde yf impossyble hard tyndale sustayne fayth whyche saynte peter confessed suffycyent serue euery cryst n man therfore lette man take boldenesse vppon tyndale tale thynke wolde haue hym onely thynge peter confessed inough byleue thynges chyrch byleueth whyche cryste hys holy spyryte haue taught hys chyrch synnes thynges indyfferent thyng forced whyther byleued tyndale shall constrayned come thys euyn hys owne wordes affermeth faste sure somewhat maye make good sayth peter ment wordes byleue thou arte promysed vnto abraam sholde come blesse v delyuer v yet sayth peter wyste meanes cryste sholde delyuer v nowe open sayth thorow worlde thorow offerynge hys body bloude yf peter tyme knewe thynge muste nedes byleued vppon payne damnacion ye maye therby se fayth whyche peter confessed inough euery man saued bounden bylyefe also thynges god hath reueled made open byleued vnto hys chyrche tyme synnes ellys muste tyndale tell v tyme god bade ho gaue v leue byleue hym ferther euer wolde ferther saye v consyder yet also tyndale agreeth trew crysten hys electe vnknowen chyrche byleue artycle perpetuall vyrginyte lady soon taught knowledge theyr formar errour wherby graunteth whyche doth e electes saye theruppon foloweth hys owne wordes artycle perpetuall virginyte lady necessary artycle fayth thus alwaye muste tyndale vppon hys owne wordes confesse artycles reueled ferther cryste vnto hys chyrche muste byleued fermely fayth taat peter confessed ellys onely dyscharged bylyefe ladyes perpetuall vyrginyte whyche tyndale yet broughte vnware graunte artycle necessary syth taught knowen also bylyefe crystes deth descencyon resurreccyon ascencyon godhed holy goste wyth dyuerse necessary poyntes mo consydered saynte peter co fessynge cryste sonne lyuynge god dyd co fesse poynte wheruppon hole fayth hangeth poynte alone confesseth hys doctryne muste nedes byleued trew hys co maundementes fulfylled theruppon foloweth ferther syth tyndale wyll byleue hys doctryne fynde wryten scrypture ioha vltimo scrypture selfe sayth neuer wryten wyll also byleue obaye crystes chyrch accordyng crystes commaundement wyll myche knowe matth lucae fondely frameth vnknowen lacke knowledge neyther byleue obaye yt foloweth saye tyndale byleueth pece fayth saynte peter confessed doth pratle prate felynge fayth wythout felynge fayth trewe bylyefe hystorycall yet goth forth boste artycle fayth whiche hym selfe confesseth peter confessyon sayth saynt peter ware crystes passyon made confessyon tyndale offerynge crystes body bloude satisfaccyon synne repente purchasynge euer aske kepe fauour synne treuth passyon cryste offerynge vp hym selfe vnto hys father vppon crosse satysfaccyon synne repente repente ryght effectually confessyon contrycyon penytencyall dedes reuengynge synnes vppon selfe wyth good workes cheryte ye largely encreaced towarde neyghbours doynge frutefull penaunce bryngynge forth frutes penaunce accordynge cousayle saynt iohn baptyst matthei sleyght frutes symple syngle frutes good greate worthy yet selfe worthy suche satysfaccyon cryste maketh worthy wythout whyche coude thynge satysfye wyth whyche maye syth hys pleasure sholde take deth full satysfaccyon gether sholde therfore carelesse slouthfull penaunce selfe owne synne tyndale wyll saye thys content sholde good dedes waye penaunce synne sholde somtyme fast otherwyse afflycte fleshe entent tame fleshe agaynst synne come nothynge punyshe synne paste thys teachynge tyndale myche lyke thoughe wolde aduyse v neuer better bycause thou haste noughte neuer better bycause thou haste done euyll runne neuer faster forth vertue bycause thou haste longe sytten styll synne saynt poule agaynst tyndals doctrine ran forth faster bycause began later toke payne fayth bycause ben persecutour fayth though neuer thought thus yf hadde ben soner conuerted wolde haue done lesse good yet thys mynde bycause began late wold bycause ben bad rom wolde better hym self counsayleth ye haue exhybyted gyuen membres serue vncl ne iniquyte iniquite iniquite agayne exhibyte gyue membres serue ryghteousnes ye maye sanctyfyed tyndale cryste answered vppon thys rocke wyll byelde congregacyon vppon thys fayth agaynst rocke fayth synne hell deuyll lye none errour preuayle euer man hath commytted yf repente come thys rocke safe thys fayth onely waye whyche chyrche goeth vnto god vnto enherytaunce hys rychesse testyfye apostle prophetes scrypture wyth sygnes myracles bloud martyr euer go god forgyuenesse synnes saluacyon way thys heretyke ryghte waye crystes chyrche lo wordes tyndale seme gaye gloryouse ye shall well examyne gaye hed glytereth wyth pretexte crystes owne holy wordes yet shall ye fynde tayle hys tale poysened serpent bosteth sayth agaynst rocke fayth synne hell deuyll lye none errour preuayle euer synne man hath commytted yf repent come thys rocke safe ye maye forgete meaneth way whyche repenteth cometh rocke thys fayth safe hys synnes wythout confessyon endeuour thorow good workes towarde satysfaccyon hys hole tale false heresye ye shall also consyder hys tale hangeth euyll gether wordes whyche proueth agaynste rocke thys fayth synne deuyll none errour preuayle proue poynte thynge though trewe sayth euer synne man haue commytted yf repente come rocke thys fayth saufe yet myght deuyll preuayle agaynst rocke fayth syth myght deuyll myght brynge man hauyng fayth dedely synne sholde happely neuer repente therfore yf tyndale wyll bost deuyll person preuayle agaynste rocke fayth rocke fayth shall saue man yt onys geteth vp theron maye set therunto must tell v eyther stande vppon rocke shall synne ellys shall sure repente hys synne fynally synne neuer faste shall saufe inough whether repente ellys may deuyll preuayle agaynst rocke fayth bryngynge man standeth mortall synne whyche shall neuer repent lyke wyse sayth none errour preuayle agaynst rocke fayth saynt peter confessed wolde fayne wyt whyther meane euer onys byleue neuer fall fro bylyefe errour byleue contrary el man maye fall fro errour yf repente returne agayne therto shall saufe meane fyrst maner muste put away saye yf repente hys errour retourne agayne rocke fayth shall saufe mych meanyng shall neuer fall errour therfore shall neuer nede repente mu e proue v scrypture pryuylege gyuen god euery man hath onys goten fayth whych poynt shall neuer proue whyle lyueth man hath maye hys owne defaut malyce neclygence eyther instygacyon deuyll suche heretykes warse deuyll fall agayne therfro many hath done ere thys onys byleued full ryght tyll spyryte pryde enuy malyce blowen theyr harte deuyll deuyls instrumentes haue brought wronge yf meane secunde maner saye man whyche hath fayth may fall therfro gatys hell preuayle agaynst man onys hath bycause falleth shall saufe yf repente hys errour retourne agayn yf meane thus sayth nothynge purpose excepte saye whyche shall neuer proue haue fall shall sure shall repente retourne agayne ellys gate hell may preuayle agaynste hym lacke repentynge retournynge yet forther yf saye whyche shall neuer proue euer onys haue fayth yf fall fro shall sure repente retourne agayne shall saufe repentynge muste sayde put awaye hys say yf repente muste saye boldely surely shall repente retourne repentynge fayth saued thus good reders ye se thys man fareth one walked barefote vppon felde full thornys woteth trede wolde loth myssetake hym wyllyngly lette passe dyssymule sense myghte meane hys owne wordes whyche hys sayenge myght saued borne good fayth se ferther thyng myght po syble meane hys wordes hell gate shall preuayle agaynst roche fayth haue redy shewed syth meneth euery man hell gate shall preuayle agaynst ye rocke fayth man excepte wolde meane man may fall fayth neuer repente turne agayne yet gate hell preuayle agaynste rocke fayth bycause man synne whyle kepeth fayth yf meane yet sayth false thyng false saynt poule sayth playnely cor maye kepe fayth yet fall cheryte whyche thyng yf tyndale glose say hys fayth dede dede fayth fayth therfore whyle kepeth fayth synne bycause synneth kylleth hys fayth answere though fayth synne wax dede waxeth dede nature fayth bylyefe soule dyeth dedely synne waxeth dede nature soule quycke soule styll though oute grace dede fayth lyuely workes cheryte timoth saynt poule sayed wanto wydowes wydow lyueth delyces dede euen whyle lyueth yf meane fayth stronge selfe saluacyon synne errour preuayle agaynste bycause fayth wyll alwaye preuayle agaynste tyll entre kyll thys goodly boste hym saye chyrch non electes electes haue ryght bylyefe whyche saynt peter confessed maye bolde sure whyche haue fayth goddes electes hys fauour euer shalbe reason fayth cryste sayed vppon rocke wyt vppon fayth wolde byelde hys chyrch agaynst rocke fayth gate hell shall preuayle saye agaynste fayth synne hell deuyll lye errour preuayle shall synne errour preuayle agaynste thys fayth yf kyll thys fayth tyndale put man uerty heuen strength fayth thys facyon none errour shall preuayle agaynste fayth longe fayth preuayleth agaynste tyll fayth febler ouercome kylled doth myche lyke though wolde saye bolde warraunt fere deth haue lyfe longe lyfe lasteth neuer dede lyke wyse longe ye kepe trew fayth ye neuer false heretykes longe ye stande styll state saluacyon ye neuer dampned goodly tale syth neyther thys may serue hym haue towched vtterly diuine myghte mene ellys takynge waye yt taketh swaruyng fro knowe catholyke chyrche vnto hys vnknowen chyrche electes calleth repentaunt synners byleue fayth saynt peter confessed perceyue trowe man ellys hys wordes wyll euyll stande gether yet hath thus wysely handeled though mater well suffycyently proued goth forth wyth boste sayth tyndale thys fayth onely waye whyche chyrche cryste goth vnto god vnto enherytaunce rychesse testyfye apostle prophetes scrypture wyth sygnes myracles bloude martyr euer goth vnto god forgyuenesse synnes saluacyon way thys heretyke ryght waye crystes chyrche lo lusty hyghe wordes eyther false ellys lytell effecte yf meane man may go saluacyon thynge wythout thys fayth aynte peter professed trew purpose spoken haue place thys mater reproueth knowen chyrch go matrymony baptysme also sacrament aulter none dyd saynt peter make mencion cofessyon myche crystes deth neyther wherof tyndale sayth tyme knowlege tyndale affermynge onely fayth peter confessed suffycyent onely waye heuyn shall haue tyndale hym selfe testyfye tyndale hym selfe sayth vntrewe yet wolde fayne good fayth fynde brynge forth yf coulde thyng ymagine myght seme mene ryght neuer wyll wyttyngly preferment part costrue myne aduersaryes wordes wrog therfore yf myghte vnderstande tyndale thus though ment fayth confessed peter euery man suffycient bycause byleue cryste sonne lyuynge god shall byleue also trewe hys wordes therfore byleueth fayle byleue therwyth euer cryst shall teche hym thys wyll fully serue hym also hym selfe speketh thynge yet helpe god best glose deuyse hym doth hym selfe caste awaye thys defence sayth seconde chapyter folowynge none errour noysome yf agaynste promyses thynges graunteth affermeth playnely expresse wordes yt man may erre wythout parell euyn though trouth contrary hys errour wryten holy scrypture w che meruelouse worde myne ere thys ye may se agreeth man may byleue yt cryst goddes sonne yet byleue contrary thynges cryste shall tell hym though tell hym scrypture therfore wyll ye se well none glose bycause wyll stande daynger dede hym selfe shall hym selfe neuer fynde better yet myne wyll suffycyently serue hym neyther man myght byleue cryste goddes sonne therby byleue also cryste wolde teche hym yet myghte wolde byleue thynges onely cryste wolde teche hym personally present wyth hym owne mouth though byleued cryste goddes sonne wolde byleue therfore wolde tell hym yet myghte mystruste byleue men wolde eyther word wrytyng tell hym tale tolde crystes owne mouth ye myght though preued wyth myracles yf tyndals stomake iewys coulde paragraph ascrybe goddes myracles belzabub call goddes hygh meruelouse workes illusyons wonder deuyll calleth myracles wrought god hys chyrche synnes apostle dayes thys myghte one byleued cryste goddes sonne haue redemed v also bloud doth dede tyndale marten hys mayster byleue crystes wordes wryten wryten wordes lyste remanaunt lyste syth draw sense lyste agaynste olde holy doctours chyrche cryst thus appereth yt neyther glose glose ellys saue tyndals tale playne pestylent heresye bothe sayth nedeth byleued also sayth bylyefe alone suffycyente saluacyon yt heresye saye bysyde bylyefe man vnto saluacyon shold nede thynge ellys though put shame repentaunce therunto wyth iffes ye se yet shall ye perceyue well hys chapyters folowynge thys chapyter putteth fayth alone suffycyent repentaunce shadowe neuer folowe yet hys thynges euer darkely wolde fayne leue hym selfe startynge hole surely yt y harde hym starte fro playne wordes hys owne euer go god waye thys fayth saynte peter confessed heretyke ryght waye crystes chyrche thys saye euer bysyde bare bylyefe wyth bare repentynge adde confessyon synne punysshe hym selfe penaunce doth better bycause hath done euyll byfore hopeth god shall eyther rewarde hym haue mercy hym purgatory punysshe hym lesse starke heretyke trouth dede yf thys false tale trewe trewe men holy sayntes holy scrypture false gothe forthe profe prayse sayth tyndale thys knowlege maketh man chyrche whyche knowledge knowledge man nedeth mo artycles hys fayth saynt peter confesseth maye bysyde repentaunce bylyefe vse waye heuen wytte maye therwythall vse waye heuen remyssyon sacramentall shryfte penytencyall workes dedes cheryte towarde satysfaccyon knowledge thys fayth maketh tyndale man chyrche sayth whyche chyrche trowe ye truely chyrch cryste whych bysyde fayth hath instytuted ye fayth blessed sacramentes dyuers artycles besyde hath playnely declared yt ye knowlege hym hys pleasure fayth way toward heuen yt without ca come thyther yet ioyne knowlege good dedes purpose good workes neyther knowlege repentaunce neyther serue v suffycyent waye heuen therfore tyndale thys knowlege made man crystes trewe chyrche syth content wyth bare knowledge setteth good workes short made therby man false chyrch deuyll lyar hymselfe father suche lyars tyndale chyrche crystes body collos euery person chyrche member cryste ephe member cryste hath crystes spyryte parte member body wherin soule present quyckeneth yf man none crystes chyrche tyndale runneth iuglynge equyuocacyon thys worde chyrche hym selfe hath byfore thys tyme confessed wrytyng thys boke whiche answere chyrch many place holy scrypture hole multytude professe fayth cryste whyther good badde fareth though man chyrche onely good folke alone spyryte cryste wyth ensample put body hauyng dede parte hangyng theron wherin soule quycken gyue lyfe whyche therfore sayth parte body forgeteth somtyme member astoyned lacketh bothe lyfe felynge whyche yet reason clene cut caste awaye receyueth lyfe felynge agayne many dedely synner doth body crystes chyrche take lyfe agayne hath synne lyen full longe dede yet thys mynde fayth whych hym selfe hath descrybed thynge onys goten hadde man kepeth spyryte god fast hys harte y surely quycke member chyrche y crystes body lese fayth spyryte tyme hath onys goten haue sayth another chapyter felyngly onely hystorycally euer haue fayth descrybeth hym rekeneth heretyke onely hys fayth trew byleuers therof trew chyrche hys fayth haue ye herde often inough onely fayth suffyseth leste wyse wyth repentynge shryfte penaunce toward heuen remyssyon synnes heresye wurshyppe blessed sacrament aulter dyshonour god purgatory frerys maye well laufully wedde nonnes greate rable suche deuelysshe heresyes mo maner suit sort sauyour sayed vnto saynt peter confessyon hys fayth matth thou arte blessed symon sonne ionas flesshe bloude hath reueled thys vnto father heuyn wyll saye tyndale confessynge thys false fayth thou art accursed tyndale sonne deuyll neyther fleshe bloude hath taught heresyes thyn owne father deuyll hell thus well hath quytte hym thys chapyter endeth confutacyon thys chapyter tyndale whyther chyrche erre foloweth next chapyter tyndale sayth trew member crystes chyrche synneth y yet synner tyndale trewe member cry e chyrche synneth y yet synner nowe come specyall poynte wherin tindale gyueth v glorious demonstracyon hys excellent hygh wytte lernynge farre surmountyng capacyte pore popyshe men perceyue myghte possyble man synneth yet synneth waye styll entent tyndale shall haue cause saye yt deface hys gay goodly tale manglynge hys mater rehersynge hym patchys pecys ye shall fyrst concernynge thys poynt hys hole chapyter gether wythout worde hys eyther omytted chaunged shall consyder examyne partes therfore hys wordes tyndale ferthermore hath thys fayth synne therfore deceyued dampnable errours thys fayth say e borne god borne god synne seed dw e h hym therfore synne cause borne god iohn whyche seed holy goste kepeth man herte consentynge vnto synne therfore fals conclusyo mayster hol eth man maye haue ryght fayth ioyned kynd abomyna yon synne yet uery member crystes congregacyon synner synneth dayly lesse wryten iohn yf saye haue synne deceyue selues trewth v agayne yf saye haue synned make hym lyar worde v paule rom sayth good w e euyll whych wolde sayth synne dwelleth thus synners synners synners yf thou loke vnto professyon harte tow e lawe god repentaunce sorowe haue bothe bycause haue synned also bycause yet full sinne styll vnto p omises mercy dedes frute synne whych remayneth bres breake h notwythstandynge yet spyryte leaueth v rebuketh v bryngeth v home agayne vnto possession neuer caste yoke god neckes neyther ye e vp vnto synne serue fyghte afreshe begynne new batay e lo ye haue herde hys hole holy sermon gether whyche teacheth v trew member crystes chyrche doth euer synne neuer synne tone parte trew membres cryste synne shall mych trouble hym wyth profe sayth euery trewe member synneth euer synneth sayth mo place one yf take synne actuall synne muste take yt ellys speketh lytell purpose men myghte peraduenture lay blocke twayne hys waye wolde breke hys shynnes ere lepte ouer lettynge parte passe lette v se proueth tother trew member cristes chyrch synneth lo thus proueth tyndale forthermore hath fayth synne therfore deceyued wyth damnable errours telleth v member electe chyrche hys fayth deceyued wyth damnable errour proueth none synne dede foloweth synne ergo damnably deceyued syth euery damnable errour synne let v se proueth hys antecedent man hauynge fayth synne proueth thus tyndale thys fayth borne god borne god synne seed dwelleth hym therfore synne bycause borne god chapiter fyrste epystle iohn whyche seed holy goste kepys mannes harte consentynge synne therfore false conclusyon holdeth man maye haue ryght fayth ioyned wyth kyndes abomynacyon synne consyder good reader tyndale telleth v thre thynges proue therby gete onys fayth saynt peter confessed neuer synne fyrste fayth borne god seconde borne god hath seed god hym thyrde haue seed god hym synne uppon thre concludeth gete onys fayth neuer synne let v consyder fyrste sayth fayth borne god therin dare bolde tell hym though trew fayth borne god sayth yet false onely fayth borne god falsely meaneth many place falsely trouth affermeth wolde make v wene bycause borne god become hys chyldren fayth therfore borne god onely fayth wysely yf wolde saye bycause bygotten hys father therfore bygotten hys father onely wythout mother thys hys foly hym selfe well perceyueth many place laboreth couer wyth sophystycacyon vsynge thys worde fayth fayth hope gyther ye somtyme cheryte therwyth also wolde make v wene wyth suche wyse iuglynge fayth alone fayth hope cherite thre geder bycause ellys fayth dede therin vseth hym selfe wysely yf wolde saye body alone eteth drynketh walketh byleueth loueth gether hys foly reproued wolde saye called body alone body wyth soule therin bycause body without ye soule dede body coulde thynge thus ye se ye shall nede deceyued hys fyrste poynt borne god fayth hys seconde poynt euery man beynge borne god hath seed god dwellyng hym wyll contende wyth hym whyther seed god dwelleth chyldern god holy goste fayth grace god wyse god hys holy spyryte dwellen good folke lettynge suche dysputacyons passe thys wyll saye yf seed fayth beynge onely fayth abyde hym thynge shall surely kepe hym fro synne maye synne dedely seed suche fayth stande styll wyth synne man seed suche fayth dwellynge hym may synne chylde deuyll maye dye go deuyll yet y seed fayth alone saye bylyefe alone greate occasyon retournynge god hys callynge agayne offer hys grace therby gete agayne bothe holsome hope cheryte great occasion therof man may kepe styll hys fayth hys bylyefe alone wythout hope cheryte eyther malyce neglygence fyrste fall synne contynue styll synne refuse ye grace god yf wyll well deuyll dyd begynnynge doth euer styll wyll styll hell longe god dwelleth heuen yf seed god crysten man ment hys grace whyche men come fayth hope cheryte good workes wythall wythout consent applyeng theyr owne fre wylles therto folke haue vse reason workynge wyth god theyr pore parte towarde theyr owne saluacyon wyth instrument yt god hys onely goodnesse hath made gyuen therunto yf meane thys seed goddes grace dwelleth styll man kepe hym fallynge synne saye trew longe man wyll cleue therunto let owne wyll worke therwith whe euer wyll withdraw owne wyll therfro folowe world flesshe deuyll lyke wyll departeth grace doth ordinarily ye seed grace depart yf meane seed god spyryte god dwelleth crysten man specyall maner dwellynge aboue dwellyng dwelleth men hys power presence hys godhed onely fauour grace speciall maner yf tyndale meane coceyue syth make selfe sure meaneth suche dwellynge vnyte person seconde person ye godhed dwelleth manhode cryste yet yf deuyse meane maner dwellynge whyche spyryte god dwelleth wyth faythfull man say spyryte dwelleth hym helpeth hym contynue suche longe man wyll applyenge hys owne wyll contynue wyth spyryte saye man may frowardnesse hys fre wyll mocyon flesshe instygacyon deuyll entycement ye worlde hys fayth remaynynge fall cheryte put spyryt hym mat dyd peple gerasens seynge crystes myracle wrought vppon madde man dyd caste deuyll bycause draue deuyll theyr hoggys therby draue theyr hoggys se though well perceyue myghty lord goodnes saw hym delyuer man legyon deuyls therfore loued hym somwhat lykelyhed wolde haue ben glad haue hym dwell styll wyth yet ferynge castynge mo deuyls myghte afterwarde happely lese mo theyr hogges prayed hym courteysely gete hym quykly thense yet god man hath put hym hys dwellyng doth hys great goodnesse alwayes vtterly leue hym hys vnkyndnesse though yf man dye ere god come agayne god shall iustyce hys vnkyndnesse houeth styll ye dore harte alway knockyng vppon hym fre wyll man let grace howse mane harte agayn accordyng ye wordes sauyour apocalipse sayth stande dore knockyng ap calip man may froward obstynate synne hath expelled god hart may dreue hym synne vpon sinne dispyghtfull cyrcustauces farre fro dore heretykes dispyght vertuouse vowes chastyte rune wedde none lyue lechery dispyght lenton faste eate flesh vpon good fryday dyspyght blessed sacrametes ye awter cast precyous body cryst pyx god shall iustely ye hougenes theyr abominacio withdraw hym selfe farre yt shall peraduenture neuer approche nere vnto agayn neuer offer hys grace muste nedes neuer cease fallynge tyll come downe deuyll thus fynally concernyng hys seconde poynt fayth alone may dwell man dedely synne togyther lyuely fayth yt wyt fayth alone coupled hope cheryte wyll good workes dwell dedely synne neyther wyth manslaughter aduowtry suche lyke tone co meth tother goth whyther synne comytted malyce weykenesse frayltye wherof tyndale styffely techeth v vntruly yt cotrary yet say synnes one wayght concernyng dyffycultye returnyg repetauce ye degree payne hell finall impenytence punyshement purgatory lacke penaunce yf dye retourne grace good wyll vnto penauce perpetually dampned hell tone well tother well thys euer haue seed god dwellynge hym synne thys poynt ye remember proueth wordes saynte iohn thyrde chapyter hys fyrste pystle whyche pystle vndowtedly one moste harde darke place new testament wherof sundry great heresyes haue rysen sondry mo may thorow suche malycyouse myndes rede scrypture none entent wreste euery word vnto worse parte playnesse symplicite apostle vsed maner theyr wordes place excepte thou repent penaunce doth playnely appere whyche hath goten fayth lyuynge fayth worketh well therwyth lyght hys faythfull lyuely workes shyne bryght face god maye yet declynynge feruour bothe myght excepte mended shold doth saynte poule saye r thynketh standeth let hym beware fall apereth playne cyrcumstaunces place speketh rekened good men faythfull stand gyueth counsayle beware lyuely fayth worketh wyth loue fynde felynge let hym tell v yet yf felynge fayth byleuyng louyng workyng selfe semeth saynt poule may lefte agayn loste appereth wordes syxte chapyter vnto hebrewys whyche wordes tyndale taketh hys chyefe holde tother parte hys heresyes hebrae wytte synne onys dedely hys baptysme shall neuer forgeuen saynte poules wordes impossyble whyche haue onys ben illumyned haue tasted heuenly gyfte haue ben made part taker holy goste haue tasted good worde god power worlde come thys fallen downe sholde renewed agayne penaunce mych mych lyeth crucyfye agayne sonne god haue hym derysyon lo syrs tyndale speketh felynge fayth saynt poule speketh haue felte taste therof tyndale speketh mych worde god saynt poule speketh haue felt taste good word god tyndale speketh myche beynge borne agayne spyryte saynte poule lyke wyse speketh yt haue receyued spyryte yet haue ben illumyned haue felte taste celestyall gyfte ben part taker holy goste haue felt swete taste good worde god power worlde come yet sayth contrary tyndals techynge may thys fall downe farre dedely synne impossyble renewed agayne penaunce hath tyndale saye saynt poule surely defence thys folysshe heresye thyng hath saye good colour hath shalbe fayne gyue ouer thys wyll comfort hym selfe wyth saynte poule semeth ferther hys heresye euery dedely synne baptysme sholde irremyssyble comfort shall dreue hym shortely sure place holy scrypture wryten one holy spyryte varyeth sentence wordes well appereth olde holy wryters full hardynesse dyffycultye yet sentece may serue tyndals heresye yt shall leuyng theyr exposycyons whyche clene agaynste hym make hym open euydent playne clere wordes holy prophete ezechyell whose wordes lo xviii chapyter synner repet hym synnes yt hath done ezec kepe comaudementes deale iustely ryghteously shall lyue shall dye ye iniquitees hath wrought wyll none remeber ryghteousnes whyche hath done shall lyue wyll sayth lorde god wicked man shold dye rather sholde conuerted hys wayes lyue truely yf ryghtuouse man turne hym selfe awaye hys ryghtuousnesse worke wyckednes abominatios wicked man wont worke shall lyue ryghtuousnes yt hath done shall none remebred offence hath comytted synne hath done shall dye lo syrs promysed heresyes destroyed onys god mouth holy man promiseth without maner excepcion yt euer wycked man wyll turne shalbe take grace lyke wyse euer ye ryghtuous man synne formar ryghtuousnes shall saue hym dampnacyon sentence lorde hath set sure repeteth agayne ye xxxiii chapyter wyse paragraph ryghtuousnes ryghtuous man shall saue hym daye euer synne also euer wycked man turne wyckednes shall hurte hym ryghtuous man lyue thorowe hys ryghtuousnes daye euer synne haue ye good reders hard sentence word god thys one holy prophete dowble cofermed therby tyndals dowble heresye dowble also condempned yet lest tyndale myghte say sholde well expoune glose ezechyel saynte poule saynt poule ezechyel namely syth saynt poule came therfore goddes mynde maye tell v ferther apereth saye lorde wyll wordes ezechiel glosed wordes though spoken god hym selfe wordes yf seme contrary shall rather expouned therof gyueth v open warnynge hys wordes folowynge sayth ezechiel ye though wolde saye ryghteouse man shall lyue trustynge hys ryghteousenes commytte wyckednesse hys ryghteousnes shall forgotte iniquyte whyche hath wrought shall dye yf saye synner thou shalt dye repenteth hym hys synne doth iugement iustyce wycked man restore pledge hath man also make restytucyon stollen goodes walke comaundementes lyfe nothynge vnryght shall lyue shall dye saued none synnes hath commytted shalbe layed charge iugement iustyce hath done therfore shall lyue dye lo good crysten reders se playne farre vnwyse yf wold folowe foly tyndale eyther bolde presumptuose hope folysshe ferefull despayre eyther wenynge felynge fayth onys dede coulde coulde dedely synne dede done baptysme could penaunce neuer saued maye sure saynt poule playnely reproueth tone y harde perceyue meaneth tother meneth tyndale telleth v may well know onely olde holy doctours sayntes expoune saynt poule sayth impossyble renewed penaunce impossyble penaunce renewed vnto state baptysme exposycyon destroye yet thyrde heresye tyndale concernynge hys full remyssyon synne payne forthwyth soone repenteth also well lerned prophete ezechyell though yt maye peraduenture man maye go forth synne farre shall neuer haue grace repentauce offered vnto hym cause ought euery man stande greate fere synne greate fayth euer fele yet yf begynne onys repente may sure god offereth grace wyll perfyt penauns wyth encreace grace wyll perdone deth dew dedely synne yf fayle parte go forwarde wyth hys grace folyshly fall therfro agaynste euydent place scrypture playnely contrary tyndals exposycyon thynge hath tyndale defende exposycyo wythall name men shall name none fewe knowen condempned heretykes agaynst holy doctours sayntes catholyke fayth crysten people pretende place scrypture shall alledge darke hard obscure thyng pertaynynge mater agaynste great many manyfeste playne euydent clerely prouynge hys exposycyon false fynally ye shall fynde hole purpose saynte iohn pystle thynge maketh thys worlde tyndals entent rather clerely contrary saynt iohn entended shew onys good neuer badde tindale sayth ment vtterly gyue world warnyng men one tyme neuer good yet euer noughte nought theyr euyll doyng lese theyr goodnes lyke wyse byfore whyle byleue well worke well whyle borne god goddes chyldren haue seed euer fall fayth heresyes good workes dedely synne lese seed god borne deuyll become hys chyldren saynte iohn thys poynt ment none thus hole processe hys pystle one parte compared wyth doth playnely declare sheweth ye deuyll y father euyll folke hys chyldren folowynge hym theyr synfull workes sauyour sayd ye iewes ye father deuyll hys desyres wyll ye ioh son god sayth saynt iohn came worlde appered dyssolue breke workes ye deuyll euery man borne god saye y goddes chylde doth synne bycause ye seed god abydeth hym synne bycause borne god goddes chylde though wolde say yf fall synne ceaceth borne god goddes chylde begynneth borne deuyll hys chylde therfore foloweth forthwyth texte chyldern god chyldern deuyll open saye thys maye ye se chyldern god chylderne deuyl ryghtuouse chylde god loueth hys brother sayth euery man hateth brother manqueller ye knowe manqueller hath euerlastynge lyfe abydynge hym lo good reder sayd byfore chylde god synne bycause hath seed god abydynge hym sayth euer hate hys brother homicyde therfore hath euerlastynge lyfe abydynge hym whyche thynge called seed god whyther ment therby lyuely fayth grace spyryte god whyche thre fyrste two begynnynge entre euerlastynge lyfe whyche shall perfyted glory thyrde hym selfe euerlastynge lyfe hys owne omnipotent nature thus haue seed lyfe neuer stronge sure one tyme whyle chylde god yet euer falleth hatered hys brother leseth lyfe commyttynge dedely synne becometh chylde deuyll thys wyll tyndale peraduenture say passe ouer dyssymule wayght saynt iohns wordes yt allegeth wynke wyll perceyue playnely proue hys purpose though trewe euer man hateth hys brother homicyde synneth dedely hath euerlastyng lyfe seed god abydynge hym yet foloweth wyll tyndale saye hath onys felynge fayth therby borne god therby hath seed god hym may synne dedely lese seed god lese synne seed god onys beynge hym bycause seed suffered hate hys brother purpose dedely synne lese seed lyfe euer strength vertue seed euerlastynge lyfe preserued fallynge dedely synne proue wyll tyndale saye playne open wordes saynt iohn alledged sayth borne god synne bycause hath seed god abydynge hym sayth longe hath sayth synne bycause hath sygnyfyeng playnely yt neuer synne bycause hath thynge hym wyll neuer suffer dedely synne entre reason made agaynst vppon wordes pystle auoydeth wyll tyndale saye myne exposycyon nothynge lyke wyse made agaynste man onys borne god proue maye borne deuyll may well made angell heuen yf angell heuen wolde fall loue god malyce sholde turned angell deuyll lyke wyse case neuer fall bycause seed god angell whyche kepeth hym euer shall haue euyll wyll doth seed god onys entred wyth felynge fayth soule preserue kepe myghty power seed soule fall malycyouse wyll maye make dede hys dedely synne thys saye yet agayne wordes saynt iohn whyche haue alledged playnely proue sayth borne god synne bycause borne god bycause hath ed god abydyng hym sayth nother place pystle whyche borne god hys generacyo wytte hys beynge borne god seed god wherby y begote borne god doth preserue kepe hym thys wyse wyll tyndale peradueture answere surely selfe deuyse effectuall wordes myghte speke hys parte good fayth yf coulde wolde neuer wyll purposely leue parte fayntely defended myne farre selfe se thynge hym selfe myghte saye thys answere shall tell hym agayn bytwene man angell almoste greate dyfferece thys mater bytwene theyr substauce nature blessed angellys stode styll wyth god deuyls fall forthwyth surely confermed grace neuer fall synne thynge wherof god wyll commaunde contrary thys sure fayth worde god taught vnto hys chyrche sure knowledge hys promyse made vnto wyth hys worde whyche meane v imagynable continually speketh vnto contemplacyon byholdynge hys almyghty godhed man fynde promyse made vnto hym one good neuer waxe nought fynde scrypture co trary haue playn scrypture proued redy se also catholyke fayth crysten people contrary crysten people excepte heretykes byleue thys xv hundred yere euer haue byleued good men chyldren god maye fall dedely synne become chyldern deuyll yet aryse grace thorowe penaunce made chyldern god agayne ezechiel many textes also holy scrypture playnely proue rom good folke maye falle perysshe cor psalmo scrypture full good counsayle aduysynge good men stande faste alway euer lyue fere fallynge yf specyall reuelacyon geuen certayne man bysyde comen ordinary course fynde also playne ensamples scrypture owne eye many vertuouse chyldren god haue fallen estate becomen synne chyldren deuyll lettynge passe ouer iudas chylde god holy apostle torned traytour god chylde deuyll hell haue seen ouer many owne dayes haue experyence ye lyke frere luther frere huskyn otho monke pomerane preste frere lambert swynglius neuer herde good vertue hym good chyldren god onys suche tyme grace deuocyo brought relygyon yet good man dowte breche theyr holy vowys promyse made god runynge apostasye lyuynge lechery vnder pretence matrymony theyr corage boldenesse suche bychery bere better shamelesse wyth vngracyouse company makynge shamefull secte therof abomynable heresye fallen cryste haue expelled seed god theyr harte synne deuylysh dedely yet dare despayre tyndale hym selfe neyther hys owne rule wherby techeth whyche wyllyngly synne purpose malycyousely impugne knowen trouth shall neuer come grace ame dement ought prayed yet dare neyther saye despayre hym selfe neyther hope yet praye god maye amende yf none de dede theyr synne gone deuyll redy ioha peccatum ad mort saynt iohn speketh vayne synne also praye deuyll u inferno null est redemptio wreches lye blasphemynge god hys vnchaungeable enemyes deuyll reason example saye wyth consent olde holy exposytours saynte iohns pystle make v perceyue surely saynt iohn dyd neuer mene wordes maner tyndale expouneth hym bycause seed god y onys hym therfore neuer dedely synne enter saynt iohn hym selfe pyste counsayleth euery good man stande styll hys goodnes beware fall idolatry whyche myghte haue boden goddes chyldre care neuer yf tyndale sayth sure theyr felyng fayth could neuer fall therto bycause seed god onys wyth theym sayd tyndale wordes saynt iohn taketh occasyo symplycyte vsed maner speche holy scrypture make cauyllacyons seke sophysmes vppon euery worde saynte iohn sayth chylde god synne menyng precysely synne dedely maner meane greate occasyon kepe hym synne doth dedely synne goddes chylde deuyls tyndale affermeth hym playnly mene whyche y onys goddes chylde neuer synne dedely though euery man wolde say honorable mannes chylde vertuousely brought vp fall shamefull vycyouse lyuynge hys good educacyon shall brydle hym drede shamynge hym selfe hys frendes muste nedes refrayne hym myghte meane wordes yonge man sholde haue greate occasyon contynue good muste nedes meane impossyble hym good neuer coulde forgete hys bryngynge vp shake shame fall nought yf one wolde saye man taketh hys wyfe loue neuer fall aduowtry loue hath must nedes kepe hym shame begyle hym loue bereth folke speke fasshyo yet though mene thynges great occasyons contayne partyes faythfull matrymony mene neuer happen otherwyse suche maner whyse meaned saynt iohn wordes sayd borne god synneth hath seed good hym therfore synne bycause borne god ment saye impossyble hym synne dedely great helpe occasyon kepe hym dedely synne yet wyll tyndale let stycke styll hys errour saye saynt iohn playnely ment impossyble hym synne hath seed god hym sayth whyche onys hath seed hym synne dedely maner menys bycause hath seed god hym onys thys saye sample dyd put neyther man wyfe come gether great loue fall aduowtry bycause loue whyche eche towarde suffer truth longe lasteth endureth eyther yet may farre fall loue hote loue whych bytwene selfe may cole clene quenched fyre wyth castynge water inough saynt iohn therfore wrytynge wordes vnderstandynge dede doth sophystycall fasshyon yt vtterly impossyble hym tyme synne dedely hath onys ye seed god hym well resonably menyng comon maner spekyng shalbe great occasyo hym abyde good styll long man kepeth seed god whyther saynt iohn toke lyuely fayth grace spyrit god cleueth vnto longe synne dedely saynt iohn say sayeng menynge spake bycame ryght euagelyst cryst tindale telling saynt iohns tale menyng thereby wolde make v wene saynt iohn ment wit euer onys borne god neyther shall synne dedely neuer bycause seed god able preserue man kepe synne speketh wysely yf wolde fyrst make argumet turneth spyt sitteth fyre sitteth fyre colde bycause hath good fire hym ergo turneth spyt colde made v onys argument wolde wene playnly proued euer onys turned spytte coulde neuer colde lyfe surely tyndals vnderstadyng saynt iohns wordes reason mych lyke lykewise man sitteth fyre cold bycause fire hym kepeth hym warm seed god man synne bycause seed god beynge hym doth kepe preserue hym synne lyke wyse broche turner sitteth warme fire may let spitte stande suffre mete burne walke himselfe snow tyll teeth chater hed colde neuer cathe hete agayne fall starke dede grownd yt onys goddes chyld hath seed god hym therfore ca synne dedely longe kepeth cleueth faste vnto may foly frowardnes owne fre expell seed god reiecte grace neclecte holy spyryte fall dedely synne continue therin dye therin go deuyll therin trewe saye hath good fyre hym colde menyng therby long kepeth hym trew say haue ye seed god hym synne dedely menyng thereby longe kepeth thus ment saynt iohn wolde say sitteth fyre neuer cold menyng therby could neuer go fro fyre cathe cold starke fole wold say haue seed god hym synne menyng therby could neuer lese seed foly frowardnesse owne wyll therby synne dedely dapned mych mad syrs thus meneth tyndale wold make v wyse wene saynt iohn ment wherof se playne contrary onely many playne place scrypture also many place saynte iohn selfe pystle wyth olde holy sayntes euer expouned pystle saynt iohn syth tindale styffely stycketh poynt seed god onys mane harte doth kepe hym euer fro euery dedely synne let hym tell v wherfore kepeth hym euer euery dedely synfull dede tyndale sayth hym selfe though seed shall kepe hym dedely synne yet shall kepe hym fro aduowtry manslaughter horryble dedes poore vnlerned people contreys wont call dedely synnes therfore good crysten reders shall poynt ende wyth good holsome counsayle saynt iohn whych selfe pystle agaynst tyndale expressely byddeth v beware suche heretykes wolde make v wene goddes wanton cokneys speciall wyse yt euer thyng could displease hym lytell set farre hys fauour yt repentauce penauce fayth none hope loue god theyr neyghbour coulde brynge fauour agaynst fond frantyke imagynacyo saynt iohn though say euer cofesse yt iesus ye son god dwelleth hym hym yet warneth v well playnely yt wolde man sholde begyle v make v wene wyth confessyon bylyefe alone good man sayth thys shall ye se chyldre god chyldren deuyll yt ryghtuous god sayth also lytle chyldre let man begyle yt doth ryghtuousnesse ryghtuous yt doth synne ye deuyll may clerely perceyue onely wordes saynt iohn vtterly destroye tyndals heresye grouded vppon hys false exposycion saynt iohns wordes saynt iohn sayth hym selfe chyldren god chyldren deuyll manyfest open theyr outward workes stande tyndals exposycyon hys heresye dependynge theruppon whyche sayth trew membres elect chyrch may fall doyng horryble dedes thorowe frute synne remaynyng theyr membres vppon great occasyons brekyng theyr membres yet horryble dedys done chyldren god styll neuer become ye child ye deuyll ye theyr horrible dedes bycause malyce purpose fraylty onely weykenes ye se good reders openly yf tyndale thys hys heresye false exposycyon god specyall maner entred theyr holy brestes yt none theyr abomynable dedes coulde dedely synne bycause yt spyryte sayth dwelleth styll within saynt iohn sayth ende thyrde chapyter kepeth goddes commaudemetes hym god dwelleth marke know sayth saynt iohn dwellynge v spyryt yt hath gyuen v whych wordes declareth clerely yt holy heretykes breke comaudeme te horryble dedes tyndale hym selfe confesseth worlde seeth frere luther weddyng nune wyth brech theyr vowys agaynst comaundemet god hath holy scripture expressely comaunded kepe fulfyll theyr vowys saynt iohn saye declareth agaynste tyndals doctryne clerely se suche dedes maye well perceyue tyme neuer whyt goddes good spyryte man dowteth whyther two better vnderstode saynt iohn whyther tyndale saynt iohn hym selfe therfore good crysten reader whyle ye se holy father authours heresyes prechynge sayntly theyr felynge fayth boste self theyr felowes sure chyldre god bycause spyryte neuer synne purpose therfore neuer synne dedely worlde wax party almayne surely fyxed confermed kynde heresyes yt coulde none errour folys frantyke deuysed man myghte bolde set forth sholde fayle fynde fonde felowes folow hopyng sholde lytell sorow taken theyr synne forgyue deth maner payne dew ye horryble dede comitted therfore dedely bycause goddes remyssyon pardo prouyded shall dye thys answere tyndale slender implyeth cotrary yt sholde well assured shall neuer dede shall spyrytually dye sure feleth well hys felyng fayth yt spyryt wyll call hym home agayn neuer farre gone wyll cause hym repente gete hym hys pardon thys opynio surely wherof ye se well foloweth lytell occasyan bolde settynge forwarde vnto synne yf prynce wolde promyse euery man perdon byfore hand yt wold surely truste vpon promyse euer shold wolde let come aske dowteth suppose plenty thys promyse wold make kynde vnthryftes god though haue made trew faythfull myse pardo trew repetautes penitetes minde purpose euer byfore truth promyse tyndale yet mystrusteth ye synne willyngly purpose playnely sayth yt shall neuer haue pardon yet hath lorde godnes wysdome left one brydle boude menes heddes refrayne fro boldenes synne yt wyt yt theyr synfull dedes repente agayne selfe without specyall grace though doth goodnes comely offer yet put surty byfore yt shalbe offred vnto yt yf boldely make self sure therof byfore yt corage therof gyue occasyo synne may ye cause yt god shall clerely withdraw fro neuer offer thys vncertaynty grace folow ye brydle yt refrayneth boldenes tyndale holy felowes trewe mebres crystes chyrch feling theyr feling fayth theyr horrible dedes done shall vndowtedly take repetauce gete theyr pardon haue brydle drede cast theyr hed therfore redy lyke vnbrydled coltes rune rouers horrible dedes whyther euer ye occasyos theyr wyld affeccyos synne tindale sayth brekyng theyr mebres lyst cary theym whe caryed vpo occasyos ye deuyll ye flesh tyndale calleth frayltye infyrmyte wyll wise malycyous purpose therfore heresy without defede theyr ye se good frute must folow yet suppose yt tyndals false heresy trew yt certayn sure repetauce therby remissyo pardon say wold yet mayntayne mater though traytoure well acquaynted condycyon hys kynge veryly knewe hadde wrought coude traytorouse purpose agaynst hym sholde yet obtayne pardon therupon boldely dyd vpon occasion hope hygh promocyon afterwarde deceyued obtayned hys pardon dede yet ben stark traytour meane whyle hadde dedely trespassed though deth folowed faute fully forgyuen mych traytorouse wretche mych prynce hys nature benyng marcyfull thus ye se playnely tyndale proue rydle trewe though synne synneth neuer dedeli muste seke better shyfte thys tyndale wyll saye hys felowys synne dedely tyme doynge suche horryble dedes bycause say purpose wyllyngly cosent vnto synne serue whyle go aboute whyle also whyche doynge resyste theyr wylles haue styll theyr harte theyr professyon loue lawe sory shall breke fynally breke agaynst theyr wyll greate occasyons gyuen whyche cary forth doynge horryble dedes rage synne brekynge theyr membres whyche horryble dedes rage one passed repente waye forthwyth clene forgyuen good reder goodly defence godly vndowtedly thys theyr defence defendynge selfe dedely synne tyndals awne wordes well thys chapyter folowynge playne clerely shew seeth euery good chrysten man well inowgh wyckedly occupyed psalmo sekyng holy dauid saith excuse theyr synne man doth suche dede agaynste hys wyll resyste ye mocyon deuyll flesh fyrste cleuynge contrary styrynge god hys good angell repugneth stryueth agaynste synne peraduenture loth brought therto whych doyng godd therby good folke fynally caste ouercome temptacions thorow grace god wurkyng yet suche conclusyon fall doynge horryble dedes whyche tempted though fully euyll resyste deuyll nothynge rather runne apace towarde hell selfe tary tyll deuyll come cary yet vndowtedly thorow theyr owne defaute fall grace wyllyngly holpe whyle resysted cowarde fought whyle wolde sodaynly caste awaye bothe bukler swerde fall downe hys enemyes fete yelde hym selfe hys enemyes handes folke comytte horryble dedes whyle resystynge whyche goddes helpe sholde haue victory yf wolde haue perseuered fyght chaunge theyr mynde ye faute theyr owne fre wyll thorow delectacyon synfull dede consent vnto seke selfe waye come therto deuyll helpeth fynde breke wyllyngly goddes commaundement fulfyll pleasure deuyll luste fleshe whyche wylfull fallynge god hys grace vnto deuyll flesh god man dowteth dampnable dedely synne therfore whan tyndale telleth v luther suche trewe membres theyr chyrche wha commytte ony suche horryble dedes comytte theym wyllyngly bycause commytte theym vpon great occasyons caryed awaye spyte theyr tethe rage synne breketh theyr membres sauynge charyte syr beshrewe theyr knauysshe membres whiche theyr synne breketh forthe suche rage let theym cast colde water sorow quenche rage without defawte theyr owne fre wyll deuyls hell neuer caste vpon theym suche hete shalbe able brynge theym vyolent inuyncyble rage compell theym vnwyllyngly suche horryble dedes god hathe promysed playne scrypture appereth wyll neuer suffre theym corint god faythfull sayth saynt poule whiche shall suffre tepted aboue ye may bere teptacyon shall also make way get ye may well welde whan saynt poule hym selfe corint leste greatnes hyghe reuelacyons myght haue set hym vp hygh pryde thorow goddes great mercyfull goodnes angell sathan prycke flesshe gyue vnto hym bete hym suche wyse fayne thryes cry god take away lord agayne shewed hym good hym lacke soone haue sodenly taken away hym shewed hym grace suffycyent whose strengthe mannes feblenes worketh fre wyll hym purposeth contynue good deuyls hell shall neuer able put hym suche rage may cary hym towarde horryble dedes one bredth forwarde agaynst wyll thus ye se tyndale towchynge ryall rydle synnynge synnynge brought poynt rede owne rydle hym self excepte wyll peraduenture saye neuer dedely synne though doone wyllyngly yf man consent synne wyll vnderstande therby co senteth synne consenteth dede yf consent dede shulde synne agreeth auoutry doth synne bycause doth consent aduoutry shulde synne rather wolde none excepte tyndale mene suche farre fette wyse inuencyon elles good faythe perceyue helpe luther hym selfe holy heretyques trewe membres theyr electe chyrche consentynge synne whan confesseth horryble dedes vpon great occasyons thorow rage synne buddyge bryngynge forthe fruyte bredeth theyr vngracious membres yf lake helpe wordes sayth yelde theym selues vnto syn serue though folke whan synne entende serue synne holynesse theyr felynge faythe doynge theyr synnes entende serue synne make synne serue theym theym pleasure theyr owne luste lykynge let hym answere loke saynt austayne mocketh lyke case olde fylosopher whiche beynge asked ashamed haue harlot rybaudes answered defence great dyfferece bytwene dede theyrs theym harlot harlot theym hym harlot harlot hym ther saynt sym propre reason trym fayre bost phylosofer haue harlot wyll lay euery man bysyde wyll tyndale maketh lyke boste excuse hym felowes sayenge fall whan occasyons great horryble dedes fruyte synne whiche remayneth membres breketh yet neuer yelde selues vnto synne serue menyng lykelyhed synne shall serue harlot dyd folyshe phylosofer sauyour hym selfe wypeth way clene worshyp tyndale worde whan sayth playnly euer synne doynge bycome bonde thrall synne trewe tale chryst tyndale false tale auoyded whan euer yeldeth hym selfe horryble dedes whiche sayth fall vpon great occasyons whan fruyte synne remaynynge theyr myscheuous membres breketh large forthwith theyr felynge fayth theyr foule fleshly felynge doynge theyr fylthy deuelyshe dede yelde selues serue synne synne serue deuyll deuyll serue agayne fyrste lytell whyl lytell fylthy pleasure hell euer blowynge fyre aboute towchyng tyndale wordes folowynge sayth wyll ryse fyght freshe begynne new batayle wordes make nothynge purpose neuer able ryse agayne alone yf god lyfte vp many tymes dothe yet sure wolde dothe euer euery man sorte hym selfe neuer tell e er bable also yf dyd alway also sure byfore wold allway yet serue tyndale poynt speke dedely synne tyme fall seruitude thraldom lyeth whyle lyeth prostrate vnder deuyls fote god hath goten hym vp agayne therfore wordes wyll helpe trouthe tyndale wordes wryten lytell yf trewe wolde make profe purpose saythe thoughe fall horryble dedes vpon great occasyons whan rute synne remaynynge theyr flesshe breketh theyr membres yet neuer caste yoke god fro theyr neckes wordes yf trewe wolde make dede somwhat theyr purpose yf doynge theyr horryble dedes dyd neuer cast yoke god fro theyr neckes myght seme tyme doynge dyd yet synne dedely syth theyr neckes yet styll bouden within yoke obedyence loue god shaken yoke truthe wordes vntrew whan horryble dedes whiche god hathe vpon peyne eternall dethe precysely forboden whiche temptacyon cause agaynst theyr wyll myghte goddes helpe leue yt vndone yf wolde syth god neuer vseth deny helpe grace tyll man leue holde slouth frowardnes owne fre wyll therfore say whan horryble dedes thorough frute theyr synne brekynge theyr bestely membres dysobeyng precepte shake yoke god whyle euyll ta ched horse shake somtyme brydle runneth large agayne yf happen goddes callynge repent penaunce purpose amende better yoke put agayne vnbrydled horse somtyme whan folowed standeth styll stayeth mayster whystelyng suffreth brydle put agayne yf tyndale say styll bycause felynge fayth whiche whan hathe one goten sayth neuer lese therfore neuer dedely synne euen whyle doynge suche horryble dedes consenteth may fall thorow frute synne breketh mebres wolde aske hym yet one agayne thynge rage passed h sore shuld repent sorowe hym selfe sayth thorow suche repentaunce may haue remyssyon shuld sory dede entent sorowfull rep ntaunce made partener pardon mercy restored lyfe yf comytted doyng maner dedely synne say sorowe hathe offended god whiche greueth hym loue reuerence bereth hym fere hell whiche fere seruyle bonde therfore metely suche holy folke luther hym selfe answere hym yf say tr w consented worke well standeth styll theym whyle doynge horryble dedes fall vpon great occasyons thorow frute synne breketh theyr mebres therfore horryble synfull dedes selfe synne remayneth theyr membres resyst dede whyle doynge consent agre vnto theyr harte onely theyr mebres wylbe wonderous case mynde consyder maner medytacyon maner conflycte haue selfe bytwene theyr harte theyr membres frute synne remayneth theyr flesshe agaynst professyon theyr harte lawe god breketh theyr membres suche horryble dedes take theyr bodyes membres god corint make saynt poule sayth membres stynkynge harlot fyrst deuyll vpon syght wanton woman putteth suggestyon theyr harte make crosse lykelyhed neyther theyr forehed theyr brest wher theyr body fo suche blessynge crossynge tyndale calleth waggynge fyngers ayre dum ceremonyes ymage seruyce lyke holy spy ytuall father borne agayne god spyryte resyste manfully fyrste great whyle whan resorte vnto talke agaynste theyr wyll ye wote well deuyll dryueth thyther must nedes go deuyll dryueth way go say god selfes ywys though go thyther fete yet wyll agre go thyther myne harte lo wold come good lorde sauynge vpon great occasyon saw one lyked well caryed thyder eue rage yet rage wyll cast thy yoke good lord wyll cary thy yoke styll necke bedde put necke yoke v bothe gether yet lo rage paste yt haryeth forth hete thorow frute synne remaynynge flesshe breketh member wyll repent good lorde sory therfore retourne agayne ellys brynge yoked wyll pray pardon thou nedes good lorde forthwith fyrst worde gyue full remyssyon synne payne holy father popys leue shall neuer punysshed therfore neyther hell purgatory world neyther good mynde good lorde wyll kepe styll neuer let fall harte whyle lye bassyng besse doynge horryble dede body yet wyll neuer agre therto wyth harte yf myshappe weykenes fraylte consent vnto dede yet wyll neuer consent synne dede shall neuer synne cosent yf cosent synne yet wyll cosent purpose malyce deuyll doth weykenes fraylty holy folke ferthest wyll consent ferther synne synne shall serue serue synne wyse wyll well ware thanke good lorde seed thy spyryt thorow felyng fayth neuer suffer harte consent seruaunte synne horryble synnys many euer membres therfore euyn whyle doyng yt thanke thyne good lorde neuer synne dedely neuer shall neuer synne thy fauour neuer stande state grace synne neuer many neuer horryble suche one peuyshe popysh papystes shall dampned deuyll yf fyftenth parte suche one faute suche felynge fayth suche good medytacyons haue godly medytacyon trew ye forsothe suppose ye shall fynde suche nother medytacyons saynt barnarde holy man assure tyndale hys felowys yf theyr holy syes trewe muste nedys doynge euery horryble dede tyndale telleth v fall ragyouse occasyos synne brekyng theyr wredched membres must say nedes haue maner medytacyo theyr holy harte yf shall horryble dedys yet tyme doyng neuer consent vnto synne serue cotynually kepe styll theyr myndes professyon purpose towarde law god ye tyme theyr horryble doyng neuer onys shake ye yocke theyr bond toward god abyde bouden styll vnto god yet ronne lose large deuyll twayne bothe onys wythout suche medytacyon neuer stande gyther fynally coclusyon worshypfull chapyter euer synnynge neuer synnynge tyndale though clerely proued thyng wherof proueth nothyng cocludeth agaynst thys wyse therfore afals coclusion holdeth man may haue ryghte fayth ioyned withall kyn e abommacyon synne conclude agaynst tindale cocludeth clerely ye yet co clude farther ye cocluded trew co cludeth false thus bycause yt chapiter tindale semeth euer synnynge neuer synnynge set vpon redyng rydles recreacyon put hym rydle agreed yet agreed sayth say yet say sayth sayd trew sayde ryghte fayth may stande abyde abomynacyo menyng therby trew ryght bylyefe artycles ye catholyke fayth maye man yet may bylyefe styll stadyng fall many dedely synnes without wrong opyn taken agayst ryght bylyefe cometh tyndale agreeth vnto therin agreed wolde fayne saue worshyp sayeng nay therfore denyeth agreed sayth yt thyng call ryght fayth ryghte fayth though man byleue ayth neuer ryght without wronge opynio artycle fayth yet yf haue trewe trust full vndowted hope god cheryte therwith also sayth must nedes ensew therupon el hath ryghte fayth tyndale auoydeth prouynge abomynacyon synne stande wyth thynge dede ryghte fayth abomynable synne stande thynge whych hym selfe calleth ryght fayth bycause pleaseth hym call ryght fayth bylyefe right inough hath none artycle wronge therin farforth perteyneth nature onely fayth yf fayth hope cheryte wherin amonge lerned men v bothe se hys sotle shyfte wynneth mych worshyp therby maye surely mych ashamed therof often thynketh therof marke well good reder cometh forth sayth hym selfe suche hys holy companyons trewe membres theyr electe chyrch haue ryght fayth felynge fayth wytte hys owne doctryne full fayth full hope cheryte bothe surely neuer fall theym maye yet theyr ryght fayth fall abomynable synfull dedes vpo great occasyons brekyng frute synne remayneth theyr synfull membres maye space perseuer horryble synfull dedes yet whyle theyr ryght fayth doth contynue theyr abomynable synfull dedes gyder tindale hym selfe abomynacyon synne maye stande gyther wyth ryght fayth onely wyth ryght bylyefe alone affermed wyth ryght bylyefe wyth good hope cheryte tyndale sayth whyche say playnely false surely thynne sotelty therof groce wytte wyse perceyue thus good chrysten reders conclusyon ye clerely se folysshe conclusyon hath brought hym selfe conclusyon thys chapyter royall rydle synnynge synnynge royally ronne ryghte nought chrysten man erre may yet erre tyndale synne erre tother syde synne erre neuer vnto deth damnacyon neuer synne purpose holde errour malycyously synnynge agaynste holy goost weakenes infyrmitye good obedyent chyldren though loue theyr faders commaundementes yet breke ofte reason theyr weakenes yelde selues bond vnto synne serue euyn erre thynge sholde agaynste promyses whiche chryste thynges theyr errours vnto dampnacyon though neuer greate bycause holde malycyously shall good chrysten reader make longe worke aboute thys chapyter syth hole somme therof ye se thynge ellys effecte trew membres tyndals electe chyrche ofte erre yet neuer erre euyn lyke maner often rather alwaye synne yet neuer synne whyche hys manyfolde folyshe heresyes euer synnynge neuer synnynge haue many maner wyse playnely refelled confuted chapyter nexte maye therfore wyll ake great dele lesse laboure busynesse thys wyll therfore put remembraunce hys mater standeth onely thys hys trewe membres hys electe chyrche haue onys goten trewe fayth saynt peter confessed vnderstandyng suche erronyous wyse luther tyndale teche wyth many playne pestylent heresyes therin haue openly clerely declared haue onys attayned fayth wyth hystorycall maner man maye beleue story wyth felyng fasshyon chyld byleueth fyre hote bycause hath burned hys fynger tyndale wyll tell nother chapyter sayth hath onys suche fasshyon attayned goten fayth wytte euer one enfect hose heresyes fast felyng fashyon neuer erre dapnably two cause sayth tyndale one bycause lyke synne purpose weykenesse infyrmyte neuer erre thynge yt shuld agaynst promyses chryste nother cause bycause errour euer trew faythfull electe meber electe chyrch happen falle agaynst promyses chryst dapnable neuer grete though trueth contrary errour wryten sayth tyndale euyn gospell selfe dedely synne bycause sayth tindale elected men ber holde malycyously ye maye clerely se tyndale affermeth techeth treuth thinges bysyde promyses trewe member hys electe chyrche maye somtyme erre neuer malycyously wytte neuer weykenesse furmentye hym selfe hath often redy declared therfore suche thynge synne dedely dampnably thynge neuer greate also wryten gospell sayth thys also ye may clerely se concernyng promyses chryst sayth trew member erre neyther malycyously fraylte syth graunteth errour infyrmyte thynges onely towch promyses ye may clerely perceyue concernynge promyses holdeth trew meber electe chyrch erre maner wyse neyther malyce purpose fraylte weykenes infyrimte yt putteth poyntes onely malycyouse errour dedely synne dapnable putteth concernyng promyses euery maner errour dedely synne dapnable purpose malice infyrmyte fraylte weykenes cause trew member electe chyrche neuer fall therin yf ment thus wolde deuyde two kyndes errour one agaynst promyses agaynst thinges ye se hym yf teche v tone dedely synne dapnable euery waye tother neuer dampnable yf holden malice therfore trew member electe chyrch maye erre tone kynde malycyously bycause ellys dampnable dedely synne tother concernyng promyses neuer erre bycause euery errour therin dedely synne dampnable one heresyes ye haue herd byfore trew member elected chyrche neuer synne dedely thys ye se therfore hys playne doctryne whych treuth hath shall nowe playnely shew let v fyrst begynne errours agaynst promyses chryst therin let tyndale tell v fyrste wherfore trew meber electe chyrch erre thynge agaynst promyses chryst suche wyse may great artycles fayth promyses hath say bycause euery maner errour though holden malycyously yet dedely synne dapnable yf towch promyse none errour dedely synne dampnable whyche towcheth promyse yf holden malycyously must forther aske hym wherby woteth wherby proueth yt euery maner errour euery artycle promyse yt chryst dedely synne dapnable though come weykenes fraylty none rrour artycle neuer great dampnable dedely yf holden malyce must aske hym wherby knoweth inowg saluacyo byleue promyse god chryst tha thorow chryste shalbe saued byleue chryste holy goste one equale god wyth father thre person one god shalbe saued ye chryst one god equale father promise made vnto v yt holy goste neyther thyng god tolde vnto v maruayle mych menys tindale proue v lesse parell byleuynge goddes wordes wordes hys promyses syth byndeth v byleue lyke cause saluacyo bylyefe promyse truste therin neyther proper nature bylyefe promyse nature good workes able selfe saluacyon ordynaunce god pleaseth hym saue v obedyence hys commaundement bothe bylyefe worke coulde yf pleased hym brynge v vnto blysse heuen wythout good worke coulde yf lyste brynge v thyther wythout fayth coulde brynge v thyther wythout knowledge gyuen v therof tyll came thyther appereth clerely cause saluacyon standeth obedyence goddes co maundement wherby byddeth v hys byddyng byndeth v captyue vnderstandynge obedyence fayth byleue hys promyses yf thys thus trouth dowte vpon lyke rewarde vpon lyke parell payne bounden byleue thynges yt god telleth v well thynges whych promyseth v therfore yf tyndale wyll contrary loke byleued man thys poynt muste accordynge hys owne rule brynge forth playne open scrypture whyche god hath tolde v wrytynge yf byleue onys hys promyses care thynges promyses wyll lyberty byleue lyste malyce v lybertye byleuynge god hys wordes hys promyses perceyue cause tyndale imagyne yf madde thynke god wyll hys tale hym lyste tell v though wryten gospell tyndale sayth haue v yet lybertye beleuynge hym bycause hym selfe wolde lybertye tell v hys pleasure somtyme trew talys somtyme suche tyndale telleth wytte vntrewth lye surely maruelouse tale tyndale mynde maruelouse dyfference putteth bytwene bylyefe promyses bylyefe artycles fayth though bylyefe promyses onely farre aboue bylyefe artycle euery man wytte hath maye well clerely se bylyefe promyses depende vpon artycles bylyefe artycles gone bylyefe promyses gyther gone many haue ben madde byleue god wyth hym goddes promyses quyte gone hys synne greate erred byleuynge god hys byleuynge god erred yet byleued euer made promyse man yet goddes promyses tyndale meneth onely promyses god made vnto mankynde farre go saynt peter wordes matth qui hunc mundum venisti tyndals exposycyon therfore tyndale ye se well byleue hys electe chyrche mankynde shalbe saued maye wythout parell chese whyther wyll byleue euer angell eternally saued notwythstandyng chryst sayd saynt iohn baptyst lest heuen greter lucae yet bycause tale tolde mouth chryst promyse made specyally syth promyse gyfte gyuen man thynges promyses artycles besyde shalbe saued thorow chryst chrystes passyon promyse yet chryst hym selfe person dede shold done properly tale promyse maye man byleuyng promyse mankynde shall saued thorow chryst may yet erre byleuynge iesus sonne mary chryste trouth eyther errour nere errour hole secte iewes great parell byleue god hys tale whe sayed thys welbeloued sonne myche delyte byleue hym hys promyse made vnto habraam matth hys seed sholde sauyour come genesis one promyse hym sholde one come worlde sholde saued tell hym thys man promyse spake promise tale one thynge though euery promyse dede tale syth man make promyse yf tell yet euery tale promyse euery chylde perceyueth therfore saynte peter toke sure waye sayed thou arte chryst arte come thys worlde takyng pryncypall poynt byleue goddes tale tale thys whyc sauyour sayde father heuen hym selfe tolde vnto peter tale peter confessed iesus chryste whyche comen worlde promyse whyche sauynge worlde sholde wrought hym thyng iewes lyke many byleue thorow chryste world shall saued yet lese frute bylyefe bycause wyll knowe chryste euyn tyndale sayth matth byleueth chrystes promyse made vnto hys chyrche erth hys holy spyryte
