catholyke chyrche euyn clene contrary also chryst turned brede precyouse body wyne blessed blode comauded done euer chyrch remebrauce passyo lucae dyd comaudyng make faythfull promyse yt hym selfe wolde euer hys chyrch holy sacramet perpetuall memory hys bytter passyon suffered v wolde gyue hys owne flessh suffered passyon hys owne blode shedde hys passyon abyde perpetually v accordynge hys owne wordes spoken vnto hys chyrche sayed matth dayes vnto ende worlde tyndale wyll byleue promyse haue fyrst boke hys owne wordes proued maketh mockes mowes blessed sacrament calleth cake brede reasoneth rather starche full lyke starke heretyke god wote sayth neyther body bloude thus hyghly magnifyeth bylyefe goddes promyses onely settynge artycles fayth thynges seconde sorte hym selfe byleueth ye se promyses lytell tother let v go ferther hys wordes se cause sayth none errour thynge saue promyses dampnable neuer greate lo thus sayth tyndale thynges promyses theyr errours vnto dampnacyon though neuer greate byca se holde malycyously yf rede new testament chrystes bretherne wolde thynke ladyes chyldren byrth chryst bycause knowe vse spekynge scrypture hebrues nygh kynnesmen called bretherne happely myghte iosephes chyldren fyrste wyfe neyther haue teache hym tyranny greate yet coude hurte hym thowgh dyed therin bycause hurteth redempcyon chrystes blood though none chryst therfore neuer saued neyther yet lesse though suche lyke hundred plucke man fayth chryste myghte erre yet neuer lesse saued though cotrary wryte gospell synnes soone rebuked repent euen soone better tawght sholde immedyately knowledge theyr errour resyste haue ye good reders reason ye cause wherfore trew membres tyndals chyrch neuer synne dedely though erre artycle promyse article neuer great cause sayth bycause lyke wyse synnes soone rebuked repente euyn soone better taught repet theyr errour byleue trouth resyste cause dedely synne mene season rebuked taught better though dyed errours artycles neuer great contrary trouth wryten gospell none promyses thys hole somme effecte thys hole chapyter though tryfle thynges bytwene therfore wyll fyrste aske hym scrypture reason proueth euery person whych elected saued shall repent soone euer rebuked synne doth wyll shew peraduenture dauid dyd happely wyll bare argumente dauid electe person dyd ergo euery elected person doth thys argument wyll lyke forme arguynge yonge chyldren vse grammer scholes asinus meus habet aures tu habes aures ergo tu e asinus meus myne asse hath eares thou hast eares ergo thou arte se fyrste suppose tyndale wyll hym selfe agre euer sayth suche rebukynge whyche hys electe persone shall alwaye soone repente retourne hadde nede come rage passed hym self sayth rage paste shall repente yf suche rebuker come whyle rage hym whyle man forwarde vppon hys vyage tyndale sayth vpon hys greate occasyons caryed forth wyth concupyscence thorow frute synne breketh hys membres rebuker may fortune tyme speke twyse ere go backe agayne wyth hym ye euer tyndale say great ge passed yet many man heuen hath baptysme fallen full often synne repented alway fyrst rebuke withstandyng many rebukynges mych callynge vppon bothe theyr frendes good gostely father ha e yet lyen l nge th haue ter ame ded pro ed full tuou e men elles g forbede thys poynt open euydent onely scrypture lso euery ne eye nothynge fere euery wyse man wyll thys poynte take tyndals al false inuented foly syth mak th thys poynt gro de tother wytte euery electe pers shall lyke wyse fyrste techyng soone better taught repente euery errour holdeth shall well folowe seconde false folysshe fyrst dede maye full well ryght good man maye mysse ledde suche tyndale thorow folkes false perswasyons maye fall errours heresyes mo one onely besyde promyses also promyses extendynge farre cuttynge shorte luther huyskyn tyndale theyr vntrewe doctryne maye depe entred roted good symple soule better men better taught shall repent hys errours fyrste seconde tyme neyther defende many tyme ofte yet shall length wyth helpe goddes grace applye hys wyll rather indyfferetly perceyue treuth frowardly stycke styll heresye shall fall ye ryght way agayn clerely se blynde heretykes ledde hym darkenes ellys yf tyndale sayd trew euery elect person wolde reformed fyrste muste folow euer dyd better taught retourne reformed fyrste w fynall reprobate sholde neuer saued vayne talke wyth hym ofter onys yf wold tourne fyrst soone onys well taught tyndals tale electe shall sent vnto trouth soone tolde hym forthwyth repent hys errour olde holy doctours sayntes ben tyndals mynde sholde haue lefte heresye many man coulde conue te fyrste yet conuerted well truely yf saynt ambrose taken vndowted token inuyncyble malyce heresye euer hym selfe fyrst techynge byleued obayed lykely neuer sholde haue c uerted saynt stayne treuth mo erro one th ugh saynt poule counsayle titus ad titum ye man che er retyke sholde one warnynge twayn e ment forbyd hym oftener callynge vp n hym wyth good holsome cousayle aynt chrysosth sayth yf deuyll dyspayre turne man last god vnto hym selfe though myste hys purpose oftentymes farforth letted say iob agayne agayne pacyence founde hym prayse also god gaue hym hym selfe great shame yf good man sholde dyspayre conuerte synner deuill god bycause bringe passe onys yet tyndals doctryne yf synner dyd repente fyrste rebukynge errour leue errour fyrst trewe techyng muste nedes perceyue therby none electe consequently playne reprobate fynally sholde dampned euer sayd done vnto hym therfore vayne go aboute tourne hym agayne god l ue hym styll deuyll thys wene good reders godly wyse waye dare boldely saye tyndale hym selfe yf shold mete wyth man trewe catholyke fayth sholde fynde hym fa e therin wolde teche hym hys heresyes though coulde fyrste techynge seconde neyther brynge hym trouth yet wolde leue hym hys wyll wolde assaye hym ofter prece vpon hym styll without hope wynne hym begyle hym laste saye tyndale hys hope mannes chaunge hys secte eyther bycause hym selfe shall laborynge hym drawe hym playe deuyls parte thynke though electe shall turne euyll good alway fyrste mocyon therfore yf turne fyrste vayn go hym yet reprobate though turne hys present good state vnto synne fyrste shall turne well inough therfore wyll laboure hym styll secte thynkyng thus tyndale taketh catholyke fayth good owne secte nought elles yf take catholyke fayth false whyche g th gete man hys owne secte good whyche lab reth brynge hym saye syth wyll leue hys doctryne resysted fyrste condem neth play ely hole tale telleth yf euery pe son electe shall sayth repente hys errour alway fyrst soone taught treuth th man fyrste treuth onys taughte hym tyndale dyd resyste made tyndale surely knowe none electes therfore reprobate god fynylly sholde dampned deuyll shold tyndale lese labour hym thys thus tyndale though mane errour suche artycles promyses yf promyses tyndale shold fynd man baptisme byleue ye chyrch byleueth agaynst heresyes byleueth wytte byleuynge agaynste tyndale goddes promyse saluacyon blode chryste doth quyte put awaye shryfte penytencyall workes towarde satysfaccyon punysshement synne repented sustayned eyther thys worlde purgatory byleue truste goddes promyse dampnable erroure agaynste goddes promyse yf tindale say fynde man shold hys owne tale perceyue man forthwith desperate heretyke bycause yf hym selfe saye trewe none electe person hys baptysme euer fall errour concernynge promyses shold hym selfe knowe founde errour co cernynge goddes promyse fynall reprobate sholde let hym alone lese labour turnyng hym sauyng cheryte beshrewe hym hartely dothe thus good chrysten reders ye maye well perceyue treuth tyndals tale profe hys hole conclusyo thys chapyter none electe fall errour agaynste promyses artycles epente theyr errours soone b taught uth repente theyr synnes oone rebuked hangeth mone shyne neyther hys heresyes towarde profe wherof wolde make thys conclusyon serue h two tone hurteth redempcyon chrystes blood consyder good reder many thynges falle vppon tyndals hedde onys hys owne fond handelyng thys ensample fyrste foly hym put tyranny nowe man sholde lacke techynge destroyeth hys owne solucyon sayth bounden byleue none artycle yf proued playne scrypture though teche trew member hys electe chyrche thynge euery chylde tell redy amonge hebreus nere kynnesmen called bretherne hath taught therby thinge scrypture doth proue yt lady euer mo chyldren chryst doth yet scrypture teche trew membres perceyue yt mo onely scrypture sayth playne contrary doth hys owne rule bysyde teche maye byleue theyr lybertye yf lyst mo chyldren dede ferthermore techeth shold wyse take sure article theyr lyefe perpetuall vyrgyn neuer mo chyldren chryst thys poynt techeth playnely maister luther ye haue herd redy thorow hole tytle wherin laboreth proue ye apostle haue lefte nothyng vnwryten bylyefe wherof necessary saluacyo whych false assercyon haue dyuers place formar bokes clerely cofuted ende thyrd boke haue answered auoyded hole chapyter therof syth thys present place tyndale hym selfe graunteth cause electe person shall saued though happen erre thynke yt lady perpetuall vyrgyn bycause shall repente errour taughte contrary playne man yt hym selfe therin cofesseth yt necessary artycle saluacyon euery man leste wyse opened taught syth cause saluacyon whyche byleued contrary tyndale hym selfe repentyng hys formar errour tyndale doth sundry place confesse agre thys poynt proued playn euydente scrypture ergo confesseth playnely cotrary fastely hath affermed whyle taught thyng byleued suerty yf proued playne euydent scrypture apostle haue lefte thynge vnwryten whyche men bounden byleue vppon payne dampnacyon thys doctryne hys mayster owne hath ye se hys owne handelyng mater vtterly destroyed dampned yf wyll happely shame laboure seke shyfte saye meaneth put thys dyfference bytwene artycles fayth promyses artycles none errour dampnable tyll man mysse byleueth better taughte trouth bounden byleue whyther scrypture bylyefe promyses euery errour ignoraunce also dampnable ere euer taught man shalbe saued yf taught haue faythfull bylyefe thus muste tyndale nedys saye aught se ellys muste cofesse one pece doctryne playnely destroyeth nother cocernyng dyfference bytwene promyses artycles yet abedeth styll agaynste hym syth confesseth perpetuall necessaryly byleued yf euydentely wryten holy scrypture concernynge dyfference bytwene necessyte bylyefe promyses bylyefe artycles shall tell hym wylbe peraduenture hard hym proue sayenge trew specyally takyng promyses hym selfe taketh begynnyng vpon fyrst prechyng saynt peter ac uu many sodaynly chrystened therupon wherby tyndale proue yt fully taught fayth promyses baptysed none dyed ere euer taught ferther yf dyed forthwith vpon theyr baptysme theyr chrystedome stode theym stede lacke ferther instruccyo promyses concernyng dare bolde say neuer taught doctryne tyndale calleth necessary techeth lacke fayth promise dampnable say neuer taught must byleue promyse shold saue gete theyr synnes tyme theyr baptysme comytted theyr bare repentauce alway full remyssyo synne payn purgatory world eyther without regarde good wurke purpose therof bare repentaunce fayth promyses dare well saye dyed th baptysed ere euer herde thynge poynt f fayth promyses whych neuer thought vpon saynt peter hys felowes yet man elles tyll deuysed deuyll put forth heretykes whe cheryte waxed cold many wynter tyndale make v many questyons sodaynly chrystened many onys begynnyng wyll yet bolde infunded theyr soules habytually wyll aske hym wherby proueth hys dyfference bytwen fayth promyses article yf proue v onely fayth promyses infused artycles whych proueth byleue hym meane whyle byleue besydes thys yf wolde graunte hym thynge neuer proue yet neuer nere though trewe wythout bylyefe promyses man myghte saued bare ignoraunce dampnable ignoraunce artycle dampnable contrary bylyefe tyll alwayes sende hys spyryt teche enforme lede euery trowth thys chyrch therfore must tyndale lerne artycles el bounden byleue repente hys forma errours contrary yf say hym selfe haue specyall reuelacyon olde holy doctours sayntes euery tyme thys fyftene hundred yere shall shame saye nay agaynste luther hym holy sayntes fayth ye comon catholyke lay people haue yet vnto thys daye ensample horryble abomynacyon monke frere sholde wedde nonne wherin yf tyndale dare say lye let tyndale haue often sayd brynge forth olde holy sayntes one sayde contrary whyche sure fynally tyndale comen agayn poynt catholyke people clergy lay folke whych euer theyr lyuynge amonge vndowtedly ar bothe sortes many ryght good vertuouse stande gether agre confessyon one trew catholyke fayth wyth olde holy doctours sayntes good chrysten people bysyde redy passed thys fyftene hundred yere byfore agaynste arrius otho lambert luther wyclyffe zuinglius huten hu se tyndale rable erronious heretykes therfore say sauynge wyll go ferther shew som hys ferther foly ellys myghte well euyn bothe ende thys present chapyter also thys hole worke wherin hys owne wyse wordes tyndale hath confounded hym selfe stroyed hys hole mater towchyng hys accustumable raylynge ende hys chapyter wyth whyche wolde seme touche catholyke chyrche clene agaynste hym selfe clerely describeth depeynteth hym selfe felowes yf wolde laboure sore fynde oute euyll myght say coulde fynde better thyng put v remembrauce euery poynt theyr myscheuouse mater tyndals owne wordes wryteth hym selfe lo thus sayth tyndale whyche malicyously mayntayne opynyons agaynste scrypture shold say ensample mayntayne frerys maye wedde nonnes proued byscrypture one thynges ye haue herd perpetuall vyrginite lady hym selfe hath cofessed chapyter trew membres electe chyrch must nedes byleue one taught yf selfe bounden byleue bounden stande therby mayntayne speketh tyndale clere agaynst hym selfe suche maketh mater vnto scripture meneth thynges necessyte requysyte wryte scrypture therfore wryteth lyke hym selfe one article fayth necessyte neded wryte god coulde haue taught kepte without wrytyng hath taughte kepte ensample petuall virginite lady tyndale hath denyed confessed denyed agayne woteth neuer hold deuyl troubleth braynes saluacyon chryste whyther trew chyrche hath none suche make mater saluacyon euery thyng god wyll haue byleued pertayneth saluacyon syth contrary bylyefe dysobedyence god taughte hys chyrch bycause wolde haue byleued perpetuall virginite lady sorte tyndale hath hym selfe openly playnely agreed yet wold secretely stele backe agayn wyttyngly peraduenture yt deuyl pulleth hym backe cote skyrte vnware blynd zele make sectes brekyng vnyte chrystes chyrche whose sake oughte suffer thynges rese agaynste fylthy purpose th wolde neuer breke vnyte fayth ye sle theyr bretherne good reder cosyder make sectes saye sondry partes dyuisios breketh vnite christes chyrch whyther catholyke chyrch yt agreed mynde relykes image kept holy dayes fastyng dayes byleued faste fermely yt abomynable sacrylege frere wedde nonne thynges many good thynges mo good chryste peple agreed one spyryte god without varyauce appereth playnely bothe olde cotynued bokes ruyce vsed chyrches thorow chrystendom bokes old holy doctours saintes euery age tyme sauyng onely heretykes arrius wycliffe luther lambert huyskyn husse tyndale lyke one tyme another wurst tyme haue ben deuyll styred vp stroye trew fayth vary fro catholyke corp christendom make new fond sectes theyr owne folysh braynes speketh kyllyng sleyng theyr bretherne hym selfe tell well inough good chrysten prynces vertuouse people dyd ye begynnynge gretely forbere heretykes tyll fynally fayne auoydyng theyr sedicyous trouble repressyng theyr inemendable malice timoth folow thensample saynte poule betoke deuyll punysshement theyr bodyes helpe theyr soules ceacynge theyr synfull blasphemy teporall lawes bodyly punyshemet fynysh ye infynyte malyce intolerable trouble heretykes sauegarde good people peace traquyllite comon peace quyete yf heretykes perturbed ben self mych esely handeled tyndale knoweth trew knoweth well agayn heretykes haue ben dyd chrystendom begyn fyght kyll sle selfe kylled slayne thyng foughten withall yt began kylled foughte withall theyr owne importune malice wherby catholyke people constrayned copelled kyll necessary defence innocentes trew tindale knoweth well storyes well england place also ye experyece dayes almayn thorow cruell insurreccyo owne felowes heretykes secte rose robbed burned killed one noughty knaue two towne good kynges prynces horryble incorigible heretykes yet somtyme ant one tenne yere good towne onys tenne score yere hole goodly monastery burned vp destroyed chyrches almost thorow hole contrey robbed spoyled bare awaye euer fonde dyspyghted sayntes image relykes crucyfyx blessed sacramet robbed mayhemed murthered many good vertuouse people goddes good sufferaunce ceaced clergye b fely g frute went ferther fell theyr lordes landes wynked cared goddes part fayne wake within whyle care theyr owne part fell vpo heretykes agayn kylled aboue iii score thousand dyuers place one somer synnes tyme swycherlande euyn thys laste yere zuinglius set heretykes rage agayne pyll spoyle trew catholykes owne countre god gaue victory faythfull folke full loth fyghte wyth sauyng force draue felde bare ouer theyr enmyes zuinglius hym selfe tharcheretyke dedely wou ded taken burned vp fayre fortune tindal master toke heresy agaynst blessed sacramet therfore tyndale speketh kyllynge heretykes calleth crysten bretherne knoweth well hym selfe yt owne vnhappy felowes heretykes say self began fyrst guyse bega eue kepe styl surely dowte tyndale hym selfe hath longed long yet euer loketh yt lutheranys zuinglianys haue begon ryse ruffle rebellyon sondry partes almayne myght se disciple assay fete trust goddes grace kinges goodnes theyr harte shall faynt ere come therto yf ye deuyll stronge styre vp wold wyshe tindale among frere barn lytell dowte yf dyd captayns copany zuinglius bushment came shortely myschyefe yf god syt sat sholde haue lyke lucke playn coclusyo bothe trust theyr owne workes lo parell yf frere sholde put truste chastyte kepynge vow yf trust lechery weddyng nonne saufe inough bycause wurke hys owne wurke wurke deuyll synne breketh mebres also put truste theyr owne opinyons falle chryste erre waye fayth chrystes blode therfore none chrystes chyrche bycause buylt vppon rocke fayth thys doth hym selfe hys felowes heretykes artycles hole catholyke chyrche put trust opynyon man sure doctryne god wherof certayntye truth depedeth vpon promyse sauyour hym selfe whyche hath promysed holy goste shall teche hys chyrche trouth lede vnto therfore yf trew dede whych truste theyr owne wurkes make idol theyr owne opynyons breke vnyon chyrche make sondry sectes kyll theyr chrysten bretherne fallen chryst waye fayth christes blode therfore none christes chyrche bycause buylt vpon rocke fayth must nedes folow luther lambert zuinglius huskyn tyndale theyr sondry sectes fallen chryste waye fayth chrystes blode therfore none christes chyrche bycause put trust theyr owne vayne inuencyons make idol theyr owne fals opynyons whyche breke peace vnyte bothe chyrch fayth makynge sectes sownyg sedycyon dyssensyon styrre vp rebellyon insurreccio agaynste theyr neyghbours theyr gouernours therby cause robbery pyllage spoyle murder theyr good catholyke chrysten bretherne put also theyr truste theyr owne workes fastyng prayeng almoyse good wurke destruccyon monasteryes castynge oute relygyon expulsyon chastyte wyth weddynge nonnes lyuyng lechery prophanyng chyrches pollutyng aulters blasphemynge sayntes rasshyng downe theyr image castynge theyr relykes dyspyghtynge lady de ylynge crucyfyxe fynally mockynge mowynge blessed sacrament thus abusynge selfe declare lo clerely buylte vpon rocke fayth wyth breth dampned spyrytes blowen downe deuyll praye god amende set rocke agayn ende chapyter ye se lo pleasaut passe fyrst ryall ridles synne synne erre erre hys ryall raylynge makynge sectes brekynge vnite kyllynge chrys en bretherne trustyng theyr wurkes perceyuyng owne wordes fynally brought nto euery myschyefe layth agaynst knowen catholyke chyrch eche fall owne necke wher fagotte lyeth surely bounden hys sholder longe lyueth wyth shyftes fynde shall neuer well shake faythe euer ted fought withall tyndale moreouer fayth whyche haue chryst er fought agaynste euer assayled bete desperacyon synne onely also temptacyo aduersyte whiche god yngeth v e v shewe v harte ypocrysye fals thoughtes lyehydd almost fayte lytell loue euyn ha pely thowght selues moste perfecte temptacyons come stande haue synned fayth feble wronge done v forgyue sykenesse losse goodes tribulacyons impacyent neyghbour nedeth helpe muste departe hym loue colde thus lerne fele goodnesse yet power good god onely temtacyons fayth preyshed vtterly neyther loue consente vnto l w god weak lykke wounded clene dede thys chapyter hath tyndale put great effecte onely comely florysshe set furnysshe hys heresyes chapyter next wherin techeth trewe membres hys electe chyrch fayth doth neuer fayle euer contynueth therfore neuer synne dedely horryble dedes euer confesseth many yet synne neuer dedely bycause malice purpose fraylte onely wekenes thorough frute synne remayneth theyr flesshe breketh theyr sely weke frayle mebres fe ther ga nysshy ge thys hys horryble heresye hath brought chapyter whych neyther proueth thynge therof thyng go h ab u proue onely falleth prechyng telleth v f holyly fayth euer fought n agaynst though man euer herde euery chyld well woteth faith alway assawted fought agaynst whyther speke hys owne false fayth heresyes trew catholyke yth chryst lyke trew catholyke fayth euer hath ben oppungned assawted deuyll hys dyscyples suche heretykes tyndale begynnyng vnto thys present tyme hath euer hys false fayth heresyes ben impugned assayled condempned god hys prophetes chryste hys apostle hys holy doctours sayntes hole corp chrystedome begynnynge hytherto thys conflycte batayle shall neuer ceace tyll chryste shall fynally refourme worlde fynysshe delyuer kyngdome father corinth euery mannes fayth pryuately knoweth though tyndale tell v deuyll dayly laboreth quenche laboreth destroye hope cheryte vertues thys nede lerne tyndale neyther men temptacyons lerne fynde fele goodnesse ne yet power good god onely yf tyndale mene trouth goodnesse cometh god man hath none none coulde haue neyther man angell god e gyfte coulde haue yet power good yf god wolde wythdrawe hys grace yf mene thys place sayth wyth hys mayster marten many place n hath power ye fredome wyll good wurkynge hym selfe wyth goddes grace resystynge temptacyon wurkynge wyth god ke ynge hym selfe synne muste nedes suche thynges syt styll hym selfe stonyed amased rechele se outh let god wurke alone saye tyndals holy sermon dampnable heresye synnys reherseth sayth fayth peryssheth vtterly loue consent vnto lawe god weke syke wounded clene dede say tale lytell purpose yf fayth mene belyefe nece syte loste dedely synne excepte heresye ryght bylyefe dedely synnes maye stand gyther well inough man may byleue trewly falsely byleue ryght lyue wronge byleue well nought yet maye electe person fall trewe fayth saye trew bylyefe lese vtterly byleuynge lye heresyes fall grace tyme yet wyth helpe gra e fynde fayth fall therto agayne fynally dye therin yf tyndale name fayth vnderstande hope truste god iugleth cotynually worde suche equyuocacyons dyuers vnderstandynges one worde serue hym hys goblettes hys gallys iuglynge stycke proper poyntes hys hole conuayaunce hys lygier de mayne sayde yf fayth meane hope graunte dyeth alwaye wyth synne gothe therwyth away waxeth tyndals doctryne oftetymes ouer grete dredeles truste theyr techyng man falleth boldenesse synne whiche hath ferelesse longe contynued waxeth forcelesse carelesse setteth synne tyll sodeynly deuyll hys hyghe harte hawte corage stryketh hym cowardouse drede vtter desperacyo ye outragyouse encrease theyr hope ryght hope though greater hope sholde hete feuer ryght naturall hete though body hote helth therfore suche affeccyons soule somtyme falleth one contrary qualyte nother ye body agew chaugeth colde hete fro hete tyme colde agayne whiche maner chaunges soule deuyll dryueth one vice contrary may well veryfyed wordes holy scrypture shall fro colde water snowe go farre passynge hete iob yet say synnes trew member may lese hope fall dyspayre grace come vnto hope agayne sayth loue co sen lawe god lost trewe member electe chyrche wote whyther tyndals loue remayne sure synne chrysten cheryte goth away neyther cheryte grace stande gether wyth synne saynt poule sayth corinth felysshyp bytwene lyght darkenes bytwene chryst beliall saye also hys gaye goodly tale telleth v hys electe membres wyth theyr holy felynge fayth wold approper specyall pryuylege kepynge styll fayth hope cheryte wyth theyr heuy hepe horryble deuelysshe dedes saye farforth hys wordes treuth hys pryuylege proper membres hys electe chyrche comon fynall electes fynall reprobatys bothe tone tother may synne repente amend synne agayne amende agayn er tyndale hath fyngers hys handes toos hys feete fynally repenteth hys synnys ryght fasshyon electe foresene god begynnynge finally dyeth impenytet dyuers wedded freres dye theyr lechery tyndals doctryne repenteth without care shryft dyeth fals heresie agaynst hys holy howsell folkes fynally reprobate fore knowen vnto god worlde wrought yt wolde fynally impenytence fall vtterly nought part hys tale whyche veryfyed reprobatys wytte kepynge cheryte styll doynge horryble dedes veryfyed electes neyther tale euery syde folysshe false nought semely settynge forthe wherof make appere fayre lykely bycause neyther bryng reason scripture good authoryte ye shall se ensample bryngeth forth tyndale good chyld father moder h e ght nurtour wisedome loueth father commaundementes perceyueth goodnes shewed hym father loueth hym father preceptes vnto welthe profy e father commaudeth hym nothyng nede father hath therof seketh profyt onely therfore hath good fayth vnto father promyses loueth hys comma mentes dothe wyth good wyll wyth good wyll goeth scole waye happely seeth companye playe wyth syghte taken ra shed hys memory forgetteth hym selfe stondeth byholdeth falleth play also forgettynge father mother theyr kyndnes theyr lawes owne profyte therto knowledge hys father kyndnesse fayth hys pr myses lo e hath agayn vnto father obedyet mynde vtterly quenched lye hydde thynges man slepeth lyeth traunc soone hath played hys lustes warned meane season cometh agayne vnto olde professyon neuer later many temptacyons go ouer harte lawe ryght hangman tormenteth hys conscye ce gothe nye persuade hym father wyll caste hym awaye hange hym yf etche hym lyke greate whyle r ne awaye rather returne vnto father agayne feare drede rebuke los e father loue punysshement wras ell wyth truste whyche hath father goodnes gyue hys fayth afall ryseth agayne soone rage fyrste brunte past mynde quyete goodnes hys father olde kyndnes cometh vnto remembraunce eyther hys owne corage comforte byleueth hys father wyll caste hym awaye destroye hym hopeth wyll vppon getteth hym home dysmayed gyther faythlesse olde kyndnesse wyll lette hym dyspayre worlde set hys harte reste vntyll payne paste vntyll haue herde voyce hys father forgyuen neyther haue yet euer herde neuer loke wyse worde tyndale workes yet herde neuer peuisshe processe holy prechynge therewith pestilently perelouse pretendeth make chapiter faythe iugleth truste hope yet wolde make v bileue neither nother tyme faileth man one hath goten man whiche one hath faythe hym selfe describeth thereby one true mebre electe church euery man dotrine one attaineth faith tyme lese fall awaye cause neuer dedely synne though neuer many danable dedes call hym selfe calleth horryble dedes dampnable happely tyndale wyll saye neuer horryble bycause seed god wytte theyr felynge fayth neuer suffer suche tre e membres hys electe chyrche horryble dedes wyllyngly purpose onely weykenesse frayltye whyche sayth dedely synnes blessed bodyes dedes neuer deuelysshe proue v thys wonderfull straunge paradox thys opynyon inopinable playne open euydent clere furnyssheth wyth sample feble dymme faynt syghte sore eye scant attayne perceyue sample thynge touche mater sholde make v clerely beholde put hys ensemples greate horryble dedes suche hym selfe another chapyter confesseth hys holy membres forgetteth suche horryble dedes wolde make reders abhorre doer speketh fayre easely feble somtyme temptacyon stande haue synned theyr fayth faynte sholde helpe theyr neyghboure theyr loue colde pacyent trybulacyos suffer wronge forgyue lo men take away theyr goodes angry lo lo angry tyndale wyth hys trew membres electe chyrche sore layeth theyr synnes theyr charge yet bycause sholde take theyr fautes myche sleyghter mynyssheth mater maketh myche lesse resemblynge lykenynge good lytell chylde though theyr fawtes chyldyshnes babe wepeth waxeth angry wyth kyghte catchynge awaye hys brede butter wold complayne hys mother byd go take rodde bete kyght syth tyndale goth aboute playe mayster sette catholyke chyrche agayne scole wolde haue v lerne suche harde lesson neuer herde lyke men maye comenly myscheuouse dedes wythout dedely synne bycause wyllyngly body compelleth lette hym leste wyse syth wyll make v yonge chyldren teche v lesson good mayster techeth hys yonge chyldren let hym teche v lesson small ragged hande wherin yonge begynner scante perceyue one letter let hym teche v fayre greate letter texte hande easy lerne vppon therfore shall pray hym lette passe ouer thys onys hys longe chyldysshe ensample hys good chyld nurture hys father hys mother wysedome lerned loue theyr comaundementes trust father promyses whyche goth good wyll scole fyndynge yet waye companyons fall playe ra ysshed remembrauce forgetyng father mother theyr promyses theyr kyndenes theyr lawes wisedomes lerned nurtur turtur taught hym standeth styll loketh falleth wurke wyth suche prety playes lykelyhed chyldre wont playe chyrystone mary bone bokyll pyt spurne poynt cobnutte quaytyng let v leue say thys good chylde hys game tyll fette eyther home wyth hys father scole wyth hys mayster wyth thre strypes hys taryenge trewauntynge waye whyche mete suche chylde hys lustes played tyndals tragycall processe remembraunce hys olde professyon wyth temptacyons ouer hys harte lawe hys ryght hange man turme tynge conscyence fere destruccyon almoste desperate drede hangyng let tyndale therfore stede thys chyld take ensample trew member hys owne electe chyrche hath felynge fayth hys owne false heresyes lytell chylde great slouen slouche hys boyes age twenty wynter stepte hys knauys age let tyndale put hym ensample doth beynge angry wyth doth hym wronge lacke dew loue lyberall helpe hys neyghbours nede wyth whych mynde softe ensample infyrmyte feblenesse imperfeccyon frayltye tyndale couereth kepeth syde hatefull herynge beholdynge theyr abomynable dedes let hym put ensample hys trewe member thys iak slouch speke frayle feble temptacyons thorow frute synne remaynynge hys flesshe tyndale sayth brekynge membres falleth horryble dedes tyndals worde aduoutry wyth hys mother poysenynge hys father murderynge hys brother sacryledge incest frere luther doth wyth hys nonne fall mockynge almyghty god tyndale doth blessed sacrament syth haue ensample taken lytell prety synnes great horryble dedes haue also taken ensample lytell prety boy olde greate knaue fytte mete mater may well co uenyently veryfyed tyndals tragycall termes tempcyons turmentry destruccyon hangeman galowes gether let v thys abomynable beste horryble crymes great text hand loke vpo lesson mayster tyndale techeth v se whyther wryten therin thynge wolde haue v lerne whyther syth haue suche boke wyth great large letter spell vpon gether selfe shall peraduenture appere went aboute byfore wyth smale ragged hande begyle v make v rede false ye remember good reders sayth hys trewe membres vppon greate occasyons vppon syghte suche thynges delyteth rauesshed theyr memory forget selfe hys lytell good chylde doth syghte playe contynueth styll folowynge fulfyllynge hys luste man hys slepe one laye traunce neyther hys fayth loste whyle loue law god though lye hydde yet contynue styll bothe twayne hys hope hys truste god also therfore though iak slouche horryble dedes dyd put ensample yet beynge trewe member tyndals electe chyrche bycause hys felyng fayth lyeth hydde hys harte feleth thynge therof consenteth hys mynde none dedes doth none wyllyngly purpose leste wyse malycyously worde hys olde tale putteth tyndale newe hys false exposycyon vppon fyrste pystle saynt iohn therfore hym none horryble dedes dampnable dedely synne myghte lette iak slouche alone aske tyndale whyther nother slouche hys acquayntaunce hys owne mayster marten luther onely trewe member also one chyefe membres hys electe chyrche hath lyen thys whyle slepe space many yeres gether syth fyrst ranne hys order apostasye wedded hys nonne yet contynueth styll thys frere hys nonne dranke well lykelyhed ere went theyr bryde bedde yf lye styll slepe yet myche tyndale wyll agre frere luther lechery wyth hys nonne euyll dede well done vertuously therfore though nede none ensample agaynste hys frantyke heresye earys good chrysten man yet tyndale hym selfe muste leue luther lyenge styll slepe wyth hys leman retourne agayne iak slouche whose dedes tyndale wyll graunte agre horryble though deny dampnable bycause iakkes felynge fayth whyche though fele bycause lyeth slepe kepeth hym styll yet loue goddes lawe suffereth hym consent vnto synne suche dedes wyllyngly purpose leste wyse malycyously let euery man agaynste tyndals folyshe tale shamelesse inuencyon take testymony wytnesse hys owne wytte whyther deuyls entycement defowleth hys mother poyseneth hys father mordereth hys brother mocketh almyghty god suche horryble abomynable dedes oftentymes doth delyberately wyth longe deuyce studye bystowed thys gere wyllyngly consent vnto ellys doth vnwyllyngly slepe traunce let tyndale tell v wyll shall wene fynde wyse man thys poynt agre bestes theyr detestable dedes vnwyllyngly wythout consent vnto synne towchynge tyndals tother goodly refuge horryble dedes hys trew membres hys elect chyrche neuer dedely synnes bycause neuer malyce thys ye sure comely deuyce whych euery wyse man ye wote well muste nedes alowe commende ensample iak slouche indyfferent iudge wolde holde good man excused abomynable dedes yf myghte appere court defoylyng hys mother dyspyght malyce borne hys father vnnaturall affeccyon bestely luste also poysenynge father grew anger euyll wyll hys person loue longynge hys substaunce suche excusys lyke hys detestable crymes wherupo myghte appere none rose anger euyll wyll pryde couetyce lechery rybaldouse appetyt coulde hys iudge suche case saye hym pytye yf poore man sayde onys sory stroke hys hed byd hym go home good sonne therfore myche iak slouche dothe none detestable dedes pure malyce body kynde affeccyon towarde hym selfe hys loue vtterly quenched therfore one tyndals electes synneth neuer bad euer fynally tyndale techeth v trew membres hys electe chyrche neuer synne dedely bycause luskes haue played theyr lustes repent agayne remember selfe theyr father formar kyndenes sory thys fayre tale tubbe tolde v hys electes euery man well woteth thus fynall reprobate dew repentaunce dyuers tymes theyr lyues restored agayne state grace thys tale tyndale dede dapnable dedely synne man neuer abomynable onely last synnes whiche dyed impenitent tyndals hyghe descrypcyons dyfferences electes reprobate brought thys poynt laste theyr dedes one theyr fasshyons theyr faythes theyr louys lawe god lyke chaungeable thorow remanaunt theyr lyues sauynge tone sorte dye repentaunt tother sorte impenytent thys thynge saye tyndale longe folysh varyaunce laste maugry teth agaynst hys purpose compelled saye haue waye sayed alwaye denyed saye one thynge forther electes hys owne agreement penytentes onely trewe repentauntes neyther hym selfe whyche repenteth abomynable heresyes stuburnly standeth sayth wyll dye mayster marten luther whyche notwythstandynge luske hath often tymes played luste wyll yet leue lechery lye styll nonne defende lawfull matrymony theyr fylthy lyfe afore god good men bestely bychery shew selues clerely trewe penytentes vtterly yf repent better ere dye shall elles none goddes fynall electes wreched reprobate accursed goddes company myserable membres deuyls dampned chyrche hell yet sayth tindale forther ende thys chapiter olde kyndenesse father let good chylde vtterly dyspayre hath played spurne poynt waye goynge scolewarde yet world set harte reste vntyll payne past vntyll haue herde voyce father forgyuen wordes wolde haue tyndale apply well hys gostely purpose turnynge sample hys good chylde olde shrewe playenge spurne poynt detestable dede let tyndale tell v voyce hys trew member elect chyrche shall voyce remyssyon mene worde spoken scrypture redy soone spedde shall hys synfull cryme comytted fall greate conflycte hym selfe bytwene hope dyspayre hys fayth almoste catchyng fall fere last wyth myth worke rysynge agayne thys gere soone done yf voyce hys father grauntynge remyssyon set hys harte reste voyce hys worde wryten scrypture herde worde dyd ye dede worde beynge suche yf vnderstanden tyndale techeth forthwyth bare repentynge without shryft penauce forgyue synne payne bothe eternall temporall bothe hell purgatory worlde worde say redy bifore dede forgyuenes onely synne passed lycence almoste also horryble dedes done meane voyce father afterwarde wrytten muste mouthe goostely father vpon humble shryfte confessyon whiche tyndall calleth crafte inuencion sathan lo conclusion tyndall chapitre false faithe euer assawted whiche ye se nowe taken assawte pece mele euery syde wounded spoyled bounden quycke felyng blayne botche vtterly dede grace sent downe vnto deuyll tyndale maner ordre election evyn goth wyth goddes electes god choseth fyrste god thou redest iohn sendeth forth calleth theym sheweth hys good wyll beareth vnto maketh se theyr owne dampnacion lawe also mercy layed vp christes blode thereto haue se mercy loue agayne chose hym submitte selues vnto lawes wytte hath great good wyll worke goddes grace well tother moch wytte lernyng lacketh wyll worke well reason therefore letteth grace go wylfully foloweth affeccion yf tyndale beleue nat wyde worlde besyde wyll truste leste wyse beleue selfe nowe sayeth mo place boke one se truthe well inoughe se well inoughe shuld nat sayeth wyttingly wylfully wryte agaynste truthe wherin wyll nowe confesse sayeth vntrue lette hym reuoke hys lye call backe agayn god forgyue wyll abyde styll worde said muste go fro worde quyte sayeth nowe yf wote well nat well yet one man leste wyse whose wyll foloweth nat wytte suche one shall nat truste lyue alone shall rather fayle fynde tyndale hym selfe good felowe falcefye owne wordes bere pore man company wordes false dede dothe yet farther appere hys conclusyon concludeth theron conclusyon necessarily folowe hys conclusyon teching onely standeth pythe mannes lyuynge false dede necessarely folowe vpon hys wordes hys wordes must nedes false vpon truth nothyng folowe truthe euery man lerned well knoweth nowe knoweth euery man well pythe mannes lyuynge standeth nat onely techyng many full well taught howe shulde lyue ye well taught able teche full well yet lyue selfe full nought shall nat nede seke longe ensample syth man douteth iudas scariothe good scole mayster longe wyt metely well taught howe shulde lyue nat wytlesse thoughe defaute good wyll e waxed conclusyon gracelesse appereth well wyse mayster oure sauyour sent hym forthe amonge one hys vsshers teche owne tyme matth yet well taught well taught yet hys owne lyuynge nat good whyle bothe e traytour bothe god man yet shall nat nede seke farre fyftene hundred yere ago wene wyll great difficultie fynde folke inoughe euyn nowe owne tyme preche gyue good counsayle theyr neyghbours agaynste vyces whiche lyue selfe thoughe good lyuynge good techynge necessary yet may euery fole se good techynge standeth nat pythe good lyuynge tyndale sayeth dothe sythe many men haue ben well taught yet lyued nought wyse reason amonge many lyke lerned tyndale mayster luther whiche wormes almayne beynge emperour sayd yf gospell well taughte shulde nede none lawe sayd sayeth tyndale bycause theyr felowes wolde fayne take away lawes leaue nothynge sermon theyr vngracious esyes myght frely preched gospell god lawe let many soules sent vnto deuyll theym shulde haue done almayne redy begynne sedicion rebellyon fall ryflynge robbery murdre manslaughter shulde without force punysshement onely teche preche vnto suche vnruly rebelles shulde ye wote well haue deuoute audyence tyndale matter wha hath tolde v tale pythe mannes lyuynge standeth gether techynge addeth thervnto sayeth tyndale howe swyne receyue lernynge defyle dogges rent good lernynge theyr tethe suche swyne suche dogges dede sauyour hym selfe wytnesseth gospell say truthe matth tyndale telleth v nowe false tyndale tolde v afore wytte standeth techynge swyne dogges nought good techyng kepe suche doynge harme must nat onely teche preche vnto suche wyll lyke swyne muste yoke brekynge hedge rynge wrotynge haue bande dogges dryue corne bytynge leade eres yf suche dogges dede rent good lernynge wyth theyr teth standeth pyth good lyuynge good teachynge auayleth tech wyll lerne rent good lernyng wyth theyr teth therfore dogges men may onely preche muste whyppes battes bete well kepe terynge good lernyng theyr dogges tethe ye barkyng chastyce make couch quayle tyll lye styll herken sayde vnto suche meanes bothe swyne kepte doynge harme dogges fall somtyme well lernynge stande vp vppon theyr hynder fete holde theyr handes afore pretely lyke mayde ye lerne daunce theyr maysters pype suche effectuall thynge punysshement bare techynge wyll suffyce proprely suche dogges heretykes barke agaynste blessed sacramentes tere wyth theyr dogges tethe catholyke chryste fayth godly exposycyons olde holy doctours sayntes proprely suche hoggys heretykes dayes fylthy kynde neuer came whyche suche wyse defyle holy vowed chastyte pure scripture god trede vppon wyth theyr foule dyrty fete drawe honest chastyte vnclene shamefull lybertye frerys wedde nonnes therfore vnto hogges dogges ye pyth good lyuyng standeth techyng good thynge wyll lerne wythout bytynge betynge yet goeth tyndale forther sheweth mo kyndes folke wordes ye pyth good lyuynge standeth techynge tyndale popeholy whyche folowynge ryghtuousenes theyr owne faynynge resyste ryghtuones god chryste wordes lo good reder expowne well playne declare techynge tyndale thys whyle bosteth wherin sayeth pyth good lyuynge onely standeth taketh techynge hys abomynable heresyes whyche techeth v onely fayth suffyseth neyther good workes haue reward heuen euyll workes shall haue punysshement eyther thys worlde purgatory hell neyther yf synner bare penytent onely byleue repent well ware wyse go shryfte penaunce hys synne rayleth calleth pope holy sayeth make self ryghtuousnes theyr owne faynynge resyste ryghtuousnes god chryste bycause resyste tyndals vnryghtuouse heresyes whyche vnder pretexte goddes onely mercy taketh awaye goddes ryghtuousnes onely vnder pretexte praysynge settynge forth mercy couertely craftely depraueth dysprayseth trewe mercy selfe god hys godnesse ordynaryly vseth towarde v tindale maketh though mercy lytell penaunce thys worlde done partye many great mortall synnes temporary payne endured purgatory set mery e chrystes passyon remanaunt whyche wolde ellys infynytely tenne hundred thousande thousande tymes longer thys taketh tyndale n mercy whyche dede mercy lorde ordynaryly vseth thys order beste blasphemeth well thys deuelysshe wurke hys dyuerse calleth expresse tyranye yet goeth fynally forther nother kynde suche folke techynge whyle helpe yet doth thus sayth tyndale attende harken vnto truth rage lustes whiche lustes abate come obaye well inough therfore chrysten man muste pacyente suffer longe wynne brother chryst whiche attendeth daye maye morowe se theyr latter ende colde fere deth hath quenched hete theyr appetytes lerne con ente vnto trouth wherunto coulde gyue none wyld rage lustes blynded theyr witt lo good reders ye maye se constaunce thys man sayth sayth trewe men wyll tyme lerne harken trouth though neuer well taught yet nother chapyter sheweth electes soone euer taughte trouth assente forthwyth wyll neuer resyste hath false parte defende neuer woteth holde hym leste wyse thys sayth trewe onely rage passed men harken also rage cometh agayne many fall nought agayne dedely synne waxe good agayne fynally shalbe saued lyke wyse good faythfull folke false shrewys come false heretykes alse doctryne fall fro rewe fayth agayne though hadde ryghte lyuely yet suche turne agayne grace theyr dedely heresyes lyfe fayth sore nowseled fal e heresyes theyr obstynate frowardnesse take suche deuelysshe delyght fynally dye therin dyd bayfeld bayn tewke b ry yet tindale telleth v euen latter ende colde fere deth hath quenched hete theyr appetytes god worketh wyth towarde consent trouth wherunto wolde gyue none eare dyd dede good contryte penytent open confessour hys fayth hys fawte tho bylney whiche beynge onys good faythfull vertu use dyd false delyght luther tyndale bokes fall theyr false heresyes helde thorow delectacyon vayne glory toke prayse secrete sect scatered congregacyo tyll fynally hys deth god hys goodnesse opened hys eye loked vppon selfe considered vayne praysours muste go fyre sawe yf dyed heresyes sholde neuer mete wyth fyre hell shold neuer fro turned trewe fayth agayne exhorted vnto thus good reders ye se hys order eleccyo tyndale hath thys chapyter hytherto sayed thynge purpose shall ye se lytell sayth purpose thys foloweth tyndale though goddes electe fall ryse agayne bycause mercy god euer wayteth vp n delyuer euyll care kyn e father wayteth vppon sonne warne hym kepe hym occasyos call hym backe agayn yf gone farre yet forgette selues oftymes nd synke downe traunces fall slepe lustes season soone awaked repent come agayne without resystaunce maketh tyndale thoughe sayde greate thynge whan wordes well examyned meneth falsely speketh folysshe wylyly sayeth electe nat fall shal ryse agayne meaneth necessyte electe muste nedes ryse agayne thor mercy god euer wayteth vpon whiche false trouthe electe shall aryse agayne meane goddes grace mercy yet myghte wolde lye styll synne whan goddes grace mercye calleth vpon byddeth hym ryse many reprobate vpon whome goddes grace mercye wayteth calleth faste calleth vpon hys electes redy helpe vp agayne tother wolde ryse malyce slouthe theyr owne wylles letted nat take holde goddes grace made nat lye styll synne lyke swyne nowe tyndale thus meneth appereth playne whole processe worke wherin concernynge saluacyon dampnacyon laboreth make v wene wyll man dothe nothynge wyllyngly vtterly forced ineuitably necessytat eternal eleccyon god vnto glory eternall reprobacyon vnto payne whiche moche say wyll man wyll myght saye wyll tre growe brynge forthe frute leaues wyll axe hewe downe tre whan man smyteth tre therwith e thus specially meneth thys chapyter ordre eleccycon appereth well generall hole progresse therof also assigneth thynge onely difference betwene electes reprobate alledgynge electes neuer fall shall ryse reason mercy wayteth euer vpon wherby well appereth tyndale meneth reprobate wytte none finally shalbe dampned hathe goddes mercy whyle elyueth waytynge vpon call vpon styrre ryse synne excepte ment shulde put electes reprobate one case sayde mercy god onely thinge sayeth waytyng vpon electe reyseth hym synne wayted vpon reprobate shulde put dyfference bytwene reason different workyng theyr fre wylles whiche tyndale wyll none wyse menynge falsely thus vseth yet hys speche folysshe wylynes doth cony couereth hed weneth well loynes open sayth electes fall shalbe saued bycause mercy wayteth vppon therin sayth truth yf god foresene wolde fynally turne agayne hym wyth helpe hys grace deserue parte taker mer te chry te passyon saued wolde haue elected saluacyon meneth shall necessaryly saued shall mow repent amend soone god hys mercy calleth vpon repent thys though thus mene yet doth dyssymule sayth bycause mercy wayteth euer vpon therfore muste nedes ryse theyr fall bycause mercy wayteth vpon therfore shall ryse thys poynt layeth open many place worke folysshe wylynes hym wene well couered thus wherfore good speke playnely tell v whyther mene fall mercy wayte vpon reprobate say nay sayth agaynst scryptures playne begynnyng god greate mercy calleth vppon people bothe electes reprobate come hym doth bothe twayne co men receyued gone waye synne agayne call ordynaryly vppon bothe hys lyke mercy styll longe lyue thys worlde wolde yf wolde assente therto selfe obaye gladde fynde agayne euer wynne wordes holy wrytte playne apocalyps stande dore knocke yf tyndale wyll auoyde thys muste saye apoca wordes holy scrypture whyche god called vppon people repentaunce spoken onely electes must tell euery man may know hym selfe electe leste maye wene pertayne hym shall reason saye comaundementes wryten vnto onely electes reprobate reproued obseruynge yf wryten surely tyndale tell v mercye god wayte vpon onely electes onely calleth vpo telleth v vayne folysshe tale dothe dede meneth dede agaynste playne scripture olde interpretours agaynste olde holy doctours chrystes churche agaynste catholyke faythe christen nacyons xv hundreth yere tyme sauyour hym selfe blessyd apo telles euen vnto lowsy luther dayes yet natwithstandinge semeth assygne cause rysynge electes theyr synne mercy god alwaye waytyng vpon yet handeleth mater man may nat well wytte wordes whether meane wha electe sonken downe traunces fallen slepe lustes calleth season whether meane say mercy calleth vpon hym traunce shaketh hym slepe el let slepe styll hys lustes deuyll rocke cradle tyll babe awake selfe surely rather semeth say god nat awaketh hym luste letteth hym slepe luste vntyll luste haue lefte though goddes callyng men glotony nat put mynde call vpon besely inspyre good thoughtes temperaunces whyle theyr mete lette alone traunce slepe tyll wery eatynge grefe gryndyng theyr belyes standynge strutte stuffynge call theym vp awake good easy waye easy entreate faste forbere nat moche lenger tyll waxe hungered agayne fareth traunces slepes folke fall bely fareth lykewyse traunces slepes folke fall partes benethe bely whan rage thereof tyndall sayeth ouer passed haue theyr traunce theyr slepe played theyr luskysshe lustes awake sone awake repent tyndale sayeth ano come agayne chastyte without resystence euer wold tyndale shulde remembre tale whiche telleth v purpose electes tale lytell effecte tale suche slepynge awakynge electes nothing propre electes thynge commune bothe electes reprobate rage traunces slepes synfull flesshely lustes whiche folke fall whiche wake agayne repent thynge tyndale telleth v thynge farre fatte sought serched botome depe diuinite ye thyng maner thus farforthe doctour ouide descrybeth v well plainly pleasaunte poetry entytled remedy loue declareth tyndals fasshyon full clerkely wanton louers theyr rage passed theyr lustes played lye wakyng haue medytacyons amendement leuyng theyr lecherouse loue euyn lyeng theyr lemmans sydes thynke wyll come wolde wyth good wyll hadde come neyther thys chapyter whyche tyndale entytleth order eleccyon loke alwaye sholde reason tell v thynges properly pertayne vnto electes thynges contrary wyse appertayne properly reprobate whyche maner handelyng ye mater myght clerely perceyue vnderstande meneth order goddes wurkyng wurkynge mannes owne wyll putteth course progresse tone sorte tother towarde theyr fynall ende tone euerlastynge lyfe tother eternall dapnacyon alway whyle loke tyndale besyde hys conclusyons false heresyes ende telleth v thynge almoste waye excepte onely peraduenture yt laste repentaunce deth comune well fynall reprobate fynall electes thys also hys chapyter foloweth wryteth thys wyse tyndale god withdraweth hand leueth vnto theyr owne strength make fele power good god onely leste sholde proude whiche none theyrs tyndale maketh wordes grounde great mater concernynge order god vsed towarde electes vpon thys fundacyo specyally rereth hys byeldynge traunces slepes slydinges electes synnes errours whyche synnes yet synne whyche errours yet erre bycause theyr felynge fayth whyche though fall yet fal bycause fele still though fele good reder wordes hys speketh electes veryfyed bothe electes reprobate yf say speketh specyally electes bycause somtyme god wythdraweth hys hand reprobate wythdraweth hande helpe grace alwaye saye thus sayth vntrewe doeth god hys goodnesse calleth theyr comynge receyueth fall awaye false fayth faynte harte flesshely delectacyon calle vppon agayne doeth vppon hys electys wythout accepcyon person parcyall fauour indyfferently tyll eyther tyme theyr immesurable outrage comenly theyr fynall impenytence fynally reiecteth refuseth amonge whych fatherly cure care well hys electes theyr fynall fall vseth wayes wynne saue vseth ye doth somtyme peraduenture gyue hys gracyouse ayde helpe world toward saluacyon heuen vnto reprobate wretche wyll damned hys electes wyll wurke wyth hys grace fynally shall saued dowte two soules haue ben saued syt heuen wyth tone halfe grace iudas caste fynally fell hell therfore thys tyndale telleth v electes god somtyme wythdraweth hys hande leueth theyr owne strength maye well tell v reprobate electes cause god wythdraweth hys hande hys helpe alwaye cause tyndale alledgeth bycause longeth alway make glaunce agaynst meryt mannes fre wyll auoyde pryde mynde farre lesse boldnes presumynge vpon surtye hye holy lyuynge fayth whyche many men maye fall takynge selfe god almyghtys mynyons though gyue thanke hym selfe ascrybe thynge theyr owne strength wene haue fre wyll neyther proude pharysey dyspysed pore publycane lucae though proude hys dedes yet ascrybed vnto hym self sayd thys haue done good lord myne owne strength sayd thanke therof good lorde suche thou haste made better gyue grace lyue holyly thys publycane sayed thanke therof selfe therfore say god wythdraweth hys hande shewe hys electes page page page page dede thynge rekened fyrst laste came onely god hym selfe saynt poule sayeth hast thou thou hast nat receyued gloryeste thou corin h thoughe thou haddest nat receyued sayeth nat thoughe thyne owne whan haue receyued myne may call another false entent wherfore tyndale telleth v thys tale withdrawynge goddes hande somtyme electes bycause wolde haue stande heresye gothe faste wytte electes sinne dedely theyr dedely synnes bycause nat wyllyngly infirmyte lacke power inpursuynge whiche purpose wolde make seme god withdraweth hade without faute leaueth power resyste blame synne thoughe cotent call synne ye maner yt mocyon toward synne rymayne origynall synne called synne tyndalles entent matter whiche excuseth synne electes withdrawynge goddes hande defaute theyr owne synne haue done matt kepe onely synne wolde el another tyme god dothe poynt bothe electes reprobate one wyt neuer withdraweth grace tone tother tyll begynne theym selfe withdrawe hym selfe onely malycyously caste theyr yoke goddes commaundementes necke man good cometh tyme vppon hym fealeth hym selfe fayth loue vnto god syke man tymes feleth taste meate whyche eateth lo good reders ye se tyndale doctryne dauid dyd dedely synne euer faute nat blame worthy neyther impacyence drawynge nere dispayre persecucyon ye purpose moch manslaughter angry worde auoutry conceyued sight another mannes wyfe trayterous destruccyo frendely seruaut recompence truthe amendes mysdede dedely synne hym bycause electe yet tyndale ashamed confesse say boldely electe inoughe may lys e synne pleasure god gyue leaue cause hym repentaunt whan hathe done forgyue hym forthwith whan repenteth forth totiens quotiens pena et culpa beleue well surely truste thereto leste faynte hope feare fall lesse synne tale tyndale saye somwhat ashamed tell v euen well playnely forthe therfore deuyseth another waye wolde make v beleue preserued fayth neuer dedely synne theyr dedes suche men may well se nat blamed neuer bestely babis veniall suche god lesse ryght reason remytte forgyue thre great cause specifyed tyndale fyrste neuer synne vpon greate occasyos farre aboue strength secondely theyr horryble dedes done repent vpon rebukyng without resystence thyrdely whiche mooste whyle doynge poore babe wote nere whyle slepe putteth ensample dauid therfore lette v consydre dauid dedes tyndals wordes examyne thre godly reason fyrste sayeth dauid synnes arose vpon great occasyons aboue dauid strength whiche great occasyons god suffred fall vpon hym cary hym awaye whan wolde haue slayne naball sonnes euen childe cradell fell nat mynde without great occasyon ye wote well rude felowe tyndale well reherseth gyuen hym churlyshe answere man vnreasonable yt wolde thynke kynge great man cause inough kyll twenty paysans vyllayns churlysh answere one fell aduoutry therby manslaughter great occasyon importable bere saw woman loked wyndow therfore euer haue one syght woma excusable yf take catche man greatly blame eyther blynde man taketh one darke neuer saw lyghte must yet remeber lest mystake tyndale great stronge occasyos greate stronge selfe tyndale sayth stro ger dauyd able theyr excuse thys poynt cause whyche tolde layed fundacyon god soche tymes fyrste wythdraweth hys hande hys helpe muste nedes weke feble frayle theyr fall cometh occasyons occasyons myghty reason theyr feblenesse theyr feblenesse cometh wythdrawynge goddes hande wythdraweth wythout desert defawte onely kepe synne takyng good workes theyr owne progresse theyr dede n dedely synne self syth occasyons bryng wythout theyr owne fawte strenger reason theyr fawteleste feblenesse cary clene awaye thys ye se fyrste goodly cause whiche tyndale wyll make v wene abomynable dedes electes dedely synnes bycause greate occasyons agaynste whyche yf mater worth argument wolde prece vppon hym sore wyth synnes reprobate bere hym hande theym haue greate occasyons theyr synnes somtyme churlysshe answere kynge man syght naked woman wynddwe aduowtry wolde aske hym suche questyons forther eyther holdynge goddes hande ouer wythdrawynge hys hande helpe wyth dyuerse dependauntes theruppon whyche euery ler ed man may fynde hym selfe almoste vnlerned whiche tyndale sholde answere sholde soone make euery wyse man se thys chapyter order theyr eleccyon hath elected chosen folysshe order myche foly therof open playne selfe shall let forther dyspycyons thys poynt passe corinth agaynst saynt poule playnely speketh sayth vnto v god faythfull whyche suffereth tempted aboue ye maye bere maketh wyth temptacyon way also ye maye well weild yt whyche wordes thys poynte occasyons aboue power clene caryed awaye clerely determyned god suffereth suche temptacyon come vnto v suche maye bothe reprobate electes able wythstande wyll thorow assystence goddes gracyous hande whiche neuer wythdraweth fawte owne wyll neuer denyeth put forth vnto v yf call therfore wyll take holde vppon therfore syth saye reprofe thys fyrst poynt playne wyll passe ouer se substaunce seconde seconde thynge soone rebuked theyr fawtes tolde repente immedyately turne agayne mekely thys sayd ii iii tymes two thre chapyters confermeth wyth hys ensample dauyd whyche dyd sayth bothe tymes yet thys barely layed forth order electes trouth thus reprobate amoge repente onely rebuked also forgyuen theyr repentaunce penaunce well ye electes longe repente tyll dampned bycause dye laste impenytent also thys proued alwaye trewe euery electe repenteth fyrste rebuke mekely returneth wythout resystence though dauyd dyd twyse truste many man heuen rebuked thryes one fawt defended full styffely repented yet ameded full well ensample nede ferther blessed apostle specyally saynt thomas inde ioh whyche lefte hys dyffydence dystruste neyther fyrste spekynge seconde tyll put hys fynger god almyghty hys syde tyndale excuseth beynge amased doth electes horryble dedes beynge traunces slepes doth dauyd ye thyrd poynt moste specyall excuse electes dedely synne slepe whyle thus sayth dauyd ye haue herde longe slombred rather harde slepe adultery bethsaba murder husbonde vriah dauyd longe slomber depe dede slepe dede yf
