mystruste vnbylyefe se selfe wryte sauyour selfe accused maici rebuked sore theyr incredulyte harde harte byleued hadde sene hym ryse tyndale hath wysely defended cometh partycalarly saynt peter sayth tyndale ye peter soone denyed chryste came hym selfe immedyately went wepte bytterly sorowe thus se peter fayth fayled though oppressed tyme tyndale euer laboreth lede v myle fro mater well ye wote chyrche techeth man euer madde saye chosen electes dye dedely synne somtyme dedely synnes wytte synnes yf dyed wythout repentauce sholde dampned agaynste thys doctryne catholyke chyrch taketh tyndale hande proue v well dyuers tytles thys boke hys exposycyon vppon fyrste pystle saynt iohn processe thys hys present chapyter order theyr eleccyon electes neuer dedely synnes ye wote well myche say suche synnes whych done maner theyr nature dedely saye suche yf person doth dye repent sholde dampned good chrysten reders poynte consydered debate bytwene v ye perceyue well eyther muste tyndale take vnderstande dedely synne thynge maner men otherwyse taken vnderstanden ye catholyke chyrch chryst agaynste dysputeth whych maner hys dysputacyo yf otherwyse toke hys aduersaryes hys parte shamefull folysshe euery man well seeth lernyng hath dysputed vppon worde vppon mater whyche wyll wene shame madde ellys yf take saye thys worde dedely synne dede must nedes tha good reders dowt well clerely se tyndals tale saynte peter hys repentaunce sorowe hys denynyenge chryste nothynge proueth tyndale purpose whyche muste saynt peter hys repentaunce synned dedely tyme forswore chryste tyndale yf wyll proue dyd therin dedely synne tyme nat inoughe hym tell v repented repentaunce restored state saluacyon muste proue v forswerynge sauiour yet shulde nat haue letted hym saluacyon thoughe forthwith vpon dede deceased without repentaunce remembraunce synne shulde proue v ye wote well ye se well dissembleth proue saynte peter synned nat dedely telleth v repented whyche thynge wherby declared holy scrypture synne greuous thinge repented synne denyenge therfore ye sorowfully repented bytterly wepte bewayled payne toke hym selfe sheweth v sore offence heynous dedelynes therof nowe commeth tyndale tother syde selfe sorowe wolde make men wene dedely synne whyche specially dothe appere contrarye thus handelynge matter nat ashamed tell v conclusyon nowe se wyse reason saynt peter faythe fayled nat whereof hathe ye se proued v nothynge hathe hym selfe tolde v playne expresse wordes contrarye whan tolde v thapostles coulde nat ye woman wordes beleue christ rysen well good syght sauyour hym selfe howe thys sayeth faylynge peter faythe oppressynge whyle thoughe man elles tyme sayde peter fayth feyled euer say fayled whyle euer yet sayd ferther dialoge therof liuely faythe fayled ye whyle bycause wrought nat loue belefe stode styll bare belefe barayne frute charyte whiche wroughte nat harte whan brought nat forthe confessyon christe mouthe mary tindale hath sayd yet hath taken away hym boldely bothe quicke fayth dede faith whyle whyche poynt whan tyndale hath done neuer whyle lyueth auoyde sayenge tyme whyche apostels coulde nat byleue christe arysen agayne agreed v matter wordes confesseth tyme theyr faythe fallen stryueth styll v vpon worde wyll wyse haue fall called faylynge amasyng astonyenge vpon great occasyons great burden oppressynge well sythe metely well agreed together tyndale matter wyll thys one lenger debate worde styll dyspute daye whether fallynge may called fayling content gyue ouer lette tyndale haue hys wyll abyde thereby styll thoughe saynt peter dyd fall faythe yet shall nat tyndale bounden call fallyng faylynge amasynge yf lyste estonyenge vpon great occasyons sore burden oppressynge lyke wyse content yf vpon great occasyon longe wery way depe myre great blocke botome tyndals horse happen vnder hym fyrste snappre stumble faynt fall downe myre tumble mayster lye gether iumble tyll good felowe helpe vppe brynge inne tary together tyll horse mete reste better growen hart let tyndall whan rydeth agayne call fall faylynge fallynge neyther yet shall neuer let men call nowe tyndale yet hys fowle falle dissymulyng hys ouerthrowe thoughe man sawe ryally tryumpheth bosteth matter hathe hys chapyter ordre eleccion wel wysely quytte selfe lyke pretye man ioye glorye whereof fynyssheth hys chapyter pleasaunte proper taunt wherin taunteth tyndale therfore nede seke gloses texte chryst sayde peter howe hys faythe shulde nat fayle yes sayeth mayster fayled hym selfe reserued lady lette v se text theyr glose together chrys sayeth luke xxii symon symon sathan seketh sy te men syfte whete haue prayed thy faythe shall nat fayle wherfore whan thou arte come vnto thy selfe agayne strengthe thy bretherne nowe put thys wyse glose therto se howe agre gether symon sathan seketh sy te hete haue praye mother faythe shall nat fay e wherfore whan thou arte come thy selfe agayne accordynge prayour hathe obtayned mother faythe shall nat fayle strength thy bretherne howe say ye nat thys proper texte well framed gether ye nat thynke moche wytte hede madde colyns braynes suche expositours tyndall good reder felynge matter fayn feble reason scrypture good authoryte neyther impugne aduersary defede selfe wolde fayne walke away thus without pece purpose prouyd make men wene wonne mery scoffe howe tyndale rehersed wordes dyaloge suche case wonte reherse wolde sawe well haue made quycke mery scoffe waxe dulle thanne halfe dede ye shall well perceyue truste whan come place replyenge hys seuerall answeres made vnto chapyters sayde worke whervnto shall reserue substaunce myne answere thys wyse cauellacyon hys agaynste myne exposicyon bettre men myne wordes sauiour spoken vnto saynte peter haue prayed thy faythe shall nat fayle wyse beare comen opynyon good chrysten people faythe abode tyme onely lady therfore mocketh maketh gaye game saynt peter faythe shulde preserued lady fayth shulde faythe wene wyll great sotell thynge perceyue faythe whyche saynt peter confessed may bothe owne confessed yet ladyes beleued thynge also beleued one bothe hym sauynge beleueth hys byleueth yet loste belefe therof may called styll vnderstandynge spekynge fyrste confessed therfore good faythe nat well se wherfore may nat saye saynt peter faythe lady well maye say wyclyffes heresyes tyndall therfore saltynge seasonynge vnsauery scoffe chaungeth mysse reherseth wordes wordes chrystes gospell hathe pleasure playe betwene lady saynte peter tosse faythe lyke tenys ball frome tone tother fonde wordes hys owne folisshe framynge nothynge nere matter whan place dyaloge shalbe shall one goddes grace surely sene examyned truste make se propre sportynge wherin playeth pageaunte betwene saynt peter lady may wyt hit hathe serue hym pastyme satte saddely frantycke colyns pyked rysshes betheleem happy tyndale yf well recouered fransyes truste god colyns day hys yet reseruynge say farther answere myne place mater moche aptayneth yet syth tyndale sayeth hym selfe cause suche glose nedeth wordes oure sauyour bycause saynt peter faythe neuer fayled owne persone confesseth thereby euer tyme fayled person le te wyse glose nedeth dare bolde say nede glose tha mocketh let reherse right suche wyll nat thys fyue yere fynde better leauynge glose say tyll come dyaloge yet se meane whyle whether glose neded none syth tyndale agreeth neded faythe tyme fayled saynt peter shall nat lette pleasure one agayne serche whether faythe tyme fayled saynt peter thentent may deale well playnly gether let hym fyrste agre gether thinge whervpon dispute vseth often whan conuycted say toke thys worde worde otherwyse take hym therein let v therfore fyrste bycause speke faythe hym declare hym selfe calleth faythe thys sawe hym selfe shamefully confuted concernynge hys heresye fayth alone suffycyent saluacyon sayth calleth dede fayth fayth meaneth waye fayth chrysten fayth hath loue therwyth reason wherof worke well shall ye se courteysely shall handle tyndale ye se well myghte many meanes many playne authorytees iacobi well saynte iamys saynte poule gospell corinth conuycte hym poynte haue often done redy gala yet shall hys pleasure lette passe thys tyme matth take fayth sayth taketh hym selfe aske tyndale thys tyme whyther tyme whyche peter forsoke forswore chryst dyd byleue wyth suche bylyefe wroughte well wyth loue saye ye syth worke wroughte forsakynge forswerynge chryste muste nedes folowe sayth forsakynge forswerynge chryste good worke wyll theruppon folow syth saynte peter wepte sorowfully therfore vere sory sore repented hym hadde well wroughte wyth loue done good worke se remedy tyndale muste nedes neuer loth confesse graunth v saynt peter tyme dyd byleue wyth loue wrought well thynketh bytwene tyndale lacketh one thynge call faylynge better perceyuynge wherof wyll aske tyndale thys saynt peter holde styll forsakyng periury styll hys lyfe fynally dyed therin yet whyle byleued hys herte artycles ye trew fayth cotrary yt sayd onely rayled thyng ye whyle agaynst chryst also loued hym sauyng well yt wold rather forswere yt euer sawe hym suffer payne sorow hym aske say tyndale yf saynt peter contynued lyfe dyed state tyme lyfe fayth yt tindale calleth fayth yt say bylefe well workyng loue fayled hym yf say wyll folow vpo tindal word yt may many faythfull folke wyth well workynge loue eternally dampned hell excepte false sauyour sayth denyeth worlde wyll denye hym angel god wyll saue hys lyfe lucae thys worlde shall lese ci moste parte suppose chrysten people shall dampned cause theyr dampnacyon shall byleue ryght loue god also farre forth wyll let liue lyst make mery bynde theym nothynge haue lust loue hym yet suffycyentely loue bere hym wyll rather forbere pleasours theyr lyfe also rather dye dedely dysplease hym doynge suche thynge wyll rather shall dye se therfore remedy tyndale muste nedes agre yf saynt peter state lyued dyed hys fayth well workynge loue fayled hym syth hadde sometyme leste wyse fayled hym lette v deuyde tyme state hys hys fyrste denye ge forswerynge vnto minute hys dyenge supposynge contynue styll dye state fyue egall partes yf please hym haue fyue tymes one fasshyon whyche fyue tymes tyndale yf please hym maye gyue name call b c e saye syth tyndale muste nedes agre yt n fyue tymes peter fayth fayled aske whyche wherto syth fyue one fashyo concernynge hys fayth muste nedes graunte fyue fayled hym let v somwhat chaunge case myghte haue ben dede peter fayth fayled thre fyrste tymes saye named abc partes hole tyme wherof abcde partes lette v put fourth parte hyche called peter ented helpe goddes gr ce thorow ye meane chrystes foresayde prayoure th hys l ynge bylyefe came hym agayne yme h lled wolde euer ather suffer tenne tymes dye onys forsake god agayne aske tyndale whether faylynge fayth latter partes hys tyme yt wyt e doth make trewe hys fayth fayleth hym whyle fayled hym dede thre formar tymes abc thre partes hys hole tyme abcde tyndale must nedes answere vnto thys tell well inough warraunt loketh hys carde vpon letter hys crosse rowe muste nedes se though hys fayth fayleth neuer whyle fayled yet whyle fayled ayled de wherof prefe playne vppon hys crosse row muste nedes se yf tyndale wolde wynk letter lyke wanton ladde man coulde make hym loke vp yet shall shew hath redde redy spyed full well peter synned dedely lyke shrewed wyly lad hath scraped hys boke ye wote well wordes sauyoure vnto saynt peter sayth vnto hym thou thou shalt conuerted conferme thou make stronge thy bretherne though myght say haue prayed thy fayth shall fynally fayle though ayle tyme forsakynge tell tru ly thou shalt thryes ere cocke crow yet shall come agayne meane prayour therfore thou shalt conuerted agayn wytte thy lyuely fayth fallen faylynge tyme thou therby turned fro enemy thorow forsakyng forswerynge dedely synfull drede bodyly deth en thou shalt say myne helpe meane prayour wyth applyenge thyne owne wyll therewyth haue gotten grace repented attayned fayth agayne thy sel e conuerted turned myne enemye vnto agayne thou conferme strength thy bretherne se goddes sake tyndale hath scraped altered one worde whyche one worde standeth makynge marrynge hole mater sauyour sayed thou arte onys conuerted strength thou thy bretherne tyndale putteth cuuerted maketh sauyour say thou art come thy self agayn strength thou thy brethern hys translacyon hadde put thys worde conuerted yet bycause sayed thys chapyt r apostle e faylynge theyr fayth dede synne turned wyse tyme god onely sed astonyed paste remembraunce therfore w hath put thys worde conuerted whyche syg yfyeth turny ge god therin doth euer imply turnynge awaye fro god hath putt stede ther f wordes comen agayn thy selfe make agre wyth wordes ama ed astonyed forgettynge selfe whyche hym selfe sayed thys ye good reders well though g aun vnto tyndale man may turned good turned bad turned vertue turned vice turned god turned deuyl yet euer scrypture worde turned standeth alone euer taken turnynge vnto god specyally word conuerted whyche worde yt hath chaunged wher euer scrypture standeth lone neuer taken turnynge man vnto hym lfe vnto god turnynge hym selfe maye turne god vnto deuyll lucyfer turnynge hym selfe turned deuyll ye se tyndale make gospell seme agre wyth hys heresye chaungeth exposycyon chyefe effectuall worde wherupon pyth mater hangeth wyll therfore aske ye question tyndale doth whyther ye thynke myche wytte hed madde colyns bray e suche exposytour oat questyon wene wyse men thynke deuyll mate made colyns madde hath sucked bray thys exposytoure blowen hys empty scalpe full bysy frantyke heresyes elles wolde neuer shame speke folyshe heresye none electe tyme dothe dedely synne whyche thynge seeth playnely reproued scrypture excepte ew heretykes ellys agrement wene hole people worlde chrysten hethen many byleue soule immort yet better sporte se howe point whyche weneth hym selfe deale mooste wylyly therein vttereth hys foly moste folysshely hys purpose thys chapyter ordre eleccyon onely proue none electe tyme synneth dedely euen laste ende weneth leste weneth selfe sytte surest chayre gloryous tryumphe mooste merely mocketh scoffeth hys aduersary euen false exposicyo text scrypture thou beynge one conuerted confirme strength thy bretherne hys vnwyse wyly chaunge worde conuerted comen hym selfe fallen hym selfe perceyued nat chaunge hath made euery man wel perceyue hym selfe whan chaunged worde perceyued well worde conuerted god turned agayne proued clerely saynte peter e god auerted synfully turned away therfore hathe wylye chaunge euen laste ende hys chapyter hys owne wytnes agaynst owne purpose whole matter peruerted quyte ouer turned ouer throwen hys tryumphant charyotte wordes mery mocke layed matter myre p recapitilacyon tyndalles processe concernynge churche begynnynge hytherto nowe shall good reders vnderstande concernynge hys declaracyon churche hys whole processe endeth wyllynge shulde nowe wene well declared proued v whyche churche nowe begynneth chapiter another newe mater wytte proue comen knowen catholyke churche nat churche therfore sythe ende owne part necessary brefely gather gether consyder thynge hath proued v therein leste proued hathe nothynge thynge hathe tolde v therein begy nynge hytherto remembre fyrste good reders occasyon hys boke answere dyaloge wherein speke churche whiche muste taught enformed shewe comen knowen catholyke churche christen people neyther gone put doctryne churche sure nat erre thynge necessary saluacyon whyche thynge sufficyently proue nowe commeth tyndall teche v churche another churche whiche wyll shewe nat churche tolde yo whether churche sheweth erre nat wyll tell therfore maketh tytle thys boke churche whether may erre nat wherein harken well nowe hathe hytherto taught fyrste tolde v begynnynge thys worde churche hathe dyuers significacyons amonge whyche laste bethought vpon twayne one generall significacyons whiche taken embrace name chryste though theyr faythes noughte thoughe haue faythe nother whiche specially signifyeth onely electes whose harte god hathe wrytten hys lawe holy spiryte gy en felynge faythe mercy christe iesu lorde hys signifycacyons lette passe thynges nat properly pertaynynge present questyon catholyke churche excepte onely whyche hathe also diffined false wytte pertyculer church euery chrysten countrey whiche nat tyndall taketh people towne countrey chrysten hethen open professed heretykes onely suche partes catholyke churche declaracyons signifycacyons hathe ye haue sene fyrste parte thys worke neyther rehersed taken yght almost one hathe rehersed lettynge say remenaunte passe nowe nat pertinent proprely matter reproued myne fyr te parte f worke two laste significacions hathe done hys parte neyther nother hathe shewed lyfte chefe significacyons whervpon matter moste especially dependeth wytte catholyke church christ trewe christen people touchynge fyrste hys two laste wyll say ment catholyke churche say defamed false generall catholyke churche nat nombre embrace name christ whether haue faythe true false faythe none heretykes suche luther zwinglius wyclyffe hym selfe fyrste wylfully leaue forsake catholyke church catholyke faythe therof therfore precyded cut fro cast therof neyther neuer haue bene accompted eyther churche churche thoughe styll call selfe christen men embrace hys name castynge truthe hys faythe fyghtynge agaynste good workes sectes dissoluynge vnyte beynge separate socyetie catholyke churche touchynge seconde signifycacyon onely electes whiche churche wherof abereth worke wolde haue onely taken churche christe milytaunte erthe let v consydre ordrely begyn ynge ende telleth v therof wyse ende laste bryngeth hys purpose aft r defence translacyon fondely defended proue v churche onely nombre electes whose har e god hathe wrytten lawe gyuen felynge faythe mercy christ iesu lorde fyrste moueth ques yon hys owne euysynge whether worde efore churche churche worde though questyon suche wyse benne pu v affyrmed churche word scoffes mo kes concludeth agaynst v worde churche whereof neuer man sayd contrary wrytten worde churche whiche thynge selfe sayd mente whiche e er princypall grounde foundacyon wherof sayd yet say contrary therof chapyter neyther thyng proueth thynge moche speketh chapyter nothynge purpose ouer sythe bryngeth forthe chapyter profe onely electes churche goeth matter well ye wote worde god bothe wrytten vnwrytten may beleued bothe electes nat elected therfore also chapyter nothynge purpose fynally syth speketh lawe wrytten spyryte god harte nowe sythe lawe wrytten rather worde god vnwrytten worde wrytten bokes scrypture haue whiche wordes onely tyndale maketh matter abhorreth euery worde god wolde eyther speke wryte besyde scrypture haue redy chapyter tyndals nat onely nothynge maketh purpose also rather semeth greatly make agaynste goeth forthe chapyter wherein laboreth proue apostels lefte nothynge vnwrytten necessary saluacyon meanynge bounden beleue nothyng onely haue wrytten tyndals mayster martyn luther sayeth euidently plainly wrytten wherin consyder haue answered hym shall truste well perceyue bene better hym haue lefte matter vntouched bothe purpose hys parte vnproued contrary hym proued besyde many place proued sacramentes whiche reproueth wrytten scrypture de howe cor ecteth amendeth therfore doctryne chapiter another chapiter former chapiter c eth bounden beleue nothinge necessyte onely wrytten scrypture yet este shulde thereby concernyng belefe ouer tely rayned euangelycall lybertie bethynketh hym selfe better hys chapyter techeth v nat necessytie bounden beleue neyther beleue promyses may saued well inoughe sayeth beleuynge nat thynges wrytten euen gospell selfe hys doctryne chapyter techeth v churche may erre yet nat erre sauynge sodeynly vnware confesseth euen contrary thanne commeth forthe hys chapyter thys questyon whether churche erre nat fyrste sayeth thys comen knowen catholyke churche bothe may erre dothe erre proueth hys bare worde sheweth hym selfe calleth electe church sayeth whole multytude repentynge synners beleue chryste put theyr truste confydence mercy god felyng theyr harte god christes sake loueth wyll rather mercyfull vnto theym forgyueth theyr synnes whyche repente mocyons vnto synne whiche feare shalbe drawen synne agayne beleue fele withoute respecte owne deseruynge onely respecte goddes trouthe promyse goeth forthe bosteth hyghly thys maner felynge faythe heresyes stede faythe haue myne answere proued therein spendeth vp chapyter yet thoughe thus descrybe electe churche yet dothe nat proue churche whyche muste obeye god hathe commaunded v complayne churche churche obey churche therfore though agreed euery thyng sayeth chapyter yet sythe electes vnknowen proued thereby pece hys pryncypall purpose wytte whiche churche also hys tytle chapyter whyther chyrche maye erre tyndale sayenge catholyke chyrche maye erre whyther electe chyrche whyche hym selfe taketh chyrche maye erre sayth chapyter one worde hys chapyter neyther thynge towarde hys pryncypall purpose yet whyche shame hym thynge conteyneth belongynge mater tytle cometh forth wyth hys chapyter trewe member chrystes chyrche synneth yet synner whiche chapiter besydes fonde rydle nothynge hepe folysshe heresyes haue proued yet also towarde mater wytte whiche churche nothyng purpose moche thoughe sayeth dedely synne yet confesseth may suche horryble dedes muste nedes make taken chyldren deuyll commeth goodly rydle chrysten man nat erre howe may yet erre therein telleth v haue shewed yt electes nat erre ye promyses god errours none sayeth dampnable theym thoughe contrary theyr errour wrytten gospell whiche doctryne hys ye may se errours doctryne maner liuynge tyndale taketh small matter bycause promyses god therfore tyndale nat greatly beleued whan techeth v freres may wedde nonnes bicause promyse god promyse frere nonne nonne frere eche wedded bedded bothe twayne wedded bedded deuyll yet ye se well thys chapyter yf trew false proueth yet thynge whyche chyrche sholde fayste haue proued electes onely chyrch serche whyther erre cometh forth wyth hys chapyter fayth whyche hath descrybed euer foughten wythall electes suche wyse inexpugnable whe one haue ca neuer tyme fayle great conclusyon wherof maketh chapyter ye se well therupon dependeth many greate mater yet doth thys chapyter brynge forth maner thynge profe eyther reason scrypture authoryte onely hys owne bare word telleth v yf tolde v thynge well knowen comenly byleued sholde blame hym tell v suche thynge straunge vnto euery man saue hym selfe inopynable man wold wene lykely trew byd v boldely byleue saue owne bare wurshypfull word tell v cause eyther poynt man authorysed apostle ellys lesse wytted fole fynally cometh forth laste wyth hys chapyter whyche calleth maner order eleccyon therin telleth v concernynge electes order theyr chosyng god doth fyrste chose calleth techeth maketh theym se theyr dapnacyon lawe mercy layed vp hym wyll haue chose god agayn submytte selfe hys lawes walke thynge sayth man doth necessyte bycause wyll none hys wytte muste nedes se thynges god maketh hym se wyll muste nedes agre folow thynge hys wytte eth telleth v mercy god allwaye wayteth vpon electe reason wherof neuer fall yt shall ryse agayne yet sheweth v forther thys electe synketh downe somtyme alleth traunces slepes whyche forgeteth hym selfe doth dyuers horryble abomynable dedes hys slepe yet hys horryble dedes doth dedely synne bycause doth fraylte infyrmyte none purpose wyllyngly wyllyngly bycause lyeth slepe whyle hys fayth neuer fayleth tyme thys proueth v thensamples kynge dauyd saynt peter saynt thomas inde apostle sayth none euer rede scrypture reproued theyr dedes aduoutry manslaughter byleuyn forsakyng forsweryng god euer dedely synne yet faylynge fayth tyme whyle dyd thys nothynge proueth telleth loketh wurshyp hys bare worde sholde byleue tyndals hole tale hath begynnynge hytherto tolde v wherby sholde lerne hym whyche chyrche whyther chyrche maye erre whych loke thorow myne answere therwith shall well perceyue hath hole processe halfe lefe gyther almost halfe lyne without one great foly lest el lye halfe consyder nowe hys electes whyche hys wordes mych perceyue darke intryked purpose wythout dependence order yet ende gathered gyd r aduysed well thys hole somme god choseth certayne lyketh choseth tyndale telleth whyther worlde made selfe borne vnto sendeth forth calleth theym gyueth felynge fayth wherby fele surely shall saued wythout regarde good workes chose hym agayne agre walke lawes theyr felyng fayth neuer one thynke vppon hym endeuour theym selfe goddes good mocyon towarde fayth sayth doth chylde towarde gettynge hys owne father hys mercy wayteth euer vppon theyr fayth doth neuer tyme fayle neuer sinne dedely horryble abominable edes euer syth folke tyndals electes haue wene haue suche felynge fayth therby fele ellys wene fele dampned haue lerned tyndale horryble dedes euer neuer dadely synne also sure repente neuer punyshed hell purgatorye thys lyfe neyther farre sayth tyndale wyth shorte repentaunce longe lyenge synne sayenge one chryste helpe maner sake snesynge fre y may fro nonnes beddes stye euen vp strayght heuen may therfore olde hardy hardly fall workes wyll syth theyr fayth full false heresyes also neuer fayle may make selfe sure se well shall worse parde wurste faythfull harlottes faythfull auo trers faythfull vowbrekers thynge ellys done onely gyuen v two dyffynycyons whyche declared neyther nother suffycyent hys purpose yet secunde mych lesse fyrste fyrste defyneth onely electys whose harte god hath wryten hys lawe heresyes wyll iumpre agre gyther amonge theym selfe fyrste aske tyndale whyther haue one hys baptysme synned purpose wyllyngly sette malycyousely therto maye goddes helpe repente agayne euer dyd reader proue consent olde holy doctours sayntes euery age synnys chrystendome fyrste began vnto frere luther owne dayes vppon parte agaynste haue proued saye thys haue proued nay thys haue say selfe setteth rysshe theym shaketh onys sayth scrypture playn vppon hys syde though saye contrary thys poynt able theym folowe theyr mayster farre fall blasphemynge sayntes take awaye theyr authoryte yet yf thys profe wyll satysfye theym shamelesse saye yet styll olde holy doctours sayntes agaynst v let many tell v one euer costrewed scripture man professynge onys vowed chastyte hys lawfull lybertye iewes turkes make v byleue maye well deceyued byleuynge catholyke chyrche syth crystes day hyther bokes new testamet trew scrypture god iewes theyr talmud turkes theyr alcharon deceyued beleuynge theyr elder frantyke blyndenesse syth amonge crysten men playne bylyef chyrche criste gouerned spyryte god trewth chyrches gouerned deuyll theyr falsed good chrysten people tyndals argument none euen thys chyrches gouerned falsshed deuyll ledeth falsshed iohan maye deceyued erre ergo chyrche gouerned trewth spyryte god ledeth trouth maye deceyued erre lyke wyse syth many false turkes haue cotynued longe false iewes haue thys substancyall reason trowe fyrste inwarde cause fayth theyrs whiche cause arre bytwene v farre vnlyke thenne theyr fayth oures outwarde cause fayth tyndale maketh though none lengthe tyme nomber peple wherin fase sectes passe v surely yf talke wyth eyther turke iewe talke wyth heretykes wolde haue outwarde cause inough laye wherfore catholyke chyrche ought reason byleued theyrs agaynste yet mo good cause haue poynt lay agaynst heretykes agaynste tother tyndale wyll happely saye therin luther answered kynges grace turke wolde laughe reason thys wyse answere surely sholde ashamed euery reason turke wolde laugh laye none suche sure iewes turkes wo allowe must sauyour cryste haue holde hys p ace iewes alowed hys lyke wyse though wolde yet many dyd euyn sholde dowte lyke wyse though reman ut wolde yet cause inough shewed sholde shold haue syth tyndale wyll wyse agre catholyke chyrche coulde lay cause vnto iewes turkes wherfore sholde reason gyue byleue lykelyhed one man catholyke chyrche poynt better ne whole poynt muste nedes tyndale doctryne knowen fyrste thynge wythout whyche nothynge proued remedy sende tyndals electes trewe reason effectuall haue onely ye wote well fyrste shall knowe yes well inough perde yf freres knowe weddynge nonnes well sende luther may sholde laughed bycause alloweth reason saynt austayne knoweth rypture goodly purpose cometh forth ende hys chapyter shewed v god euer olde testament dyd let great multytude erre reseruynge waye lytle floke call backe agayne shewe ryght way meneth god hath sent hym hys mayster holy heretykes teche catholyke chyrche ryght waye haue sayd god hath promysed sende hys holy spyryte thys chyrche teche trouth remayne therwyth hym selfe also perpetually guyde hys chyrche suche fallynge hys catholyke chyrche ryght fayth sholde nede sende coll prophetes heretykes teche hys chyrche fayth appereth well olde holy sayntes euery age syth thapostles dayes wyth whose doctryne theyr bookes proued doctryne catholyke chyrche agaynst heretykes agreeth also whan sent hys prophetes olde wonte alway sende honest men hys erand proued selfe myracles suche rascayle rybauldes call selfe apostle proue iestynge raylynge goddes messenger wonte also teche euery man clennesse honesty bestely felowes teche folke breke theyr vowys freres flye forth wedde nonnes ouer yf trewe flocke alwaye lytle flocke heretykes trewe flocke growen onely greate maynye menne also great shrewde sorte flockes flockyng many countrees chrystendome full faste many place mych harme haue done mych go chaunge bylyefe eyther syde fynally chose folke god wont reserue sende techethe worlde ryghte waye dyd agre theyr doctryne ellys worlde ye w te well wyste whyche folowe hese heretykes almost many sectes men neuer one agreeth wyth yf worlde lerne ryghte waye mater mych lyke yf man walkynge wyldernesse fayne wolde fynde ryghte waye towarde towne enteded sholde mete mayny lewde mockynge knauys whyche poore man hadde prayed tell hym waye wolde gete roundell turnynge theym backe backe speke onys eche tell hym thys waye eche theym poyntynge forthe wyth hys hande waye hys face standeth fynally faythfull folke may well easyly fele false fumblynge heretyke whyche false fumblynge fayth feleth blessed sacrament aultar sacred body sauyour hym selfe sholde haue none honour done taken thynge ellys eyther bare brede starche hath well quytte hym wyth false turkes iewes agaynste trewe catholyke chyrche cryste commeth forth wyth chapyter therin fynall conclusyon hys mater concernynge knowlege chyrche fynall solucyon seconde argument made catholyke chyrche fynall confyrmacyan hys false felynge fayth knytteth vppe hys dyspycyons wyse wordes folow tyndale phow thys worde chyrche hath double interpretacyon thys therfore sure conclusyon paule sayth rom aell aelyt neyther bycause ab ahams seed rahams chyldren onely folowe ayth abra euen none byleue theyr mouthes moued authoryte theyr elder pryncyples chyrche begynnynge falshed amonge trewth good chrysten reders haue geuen whole processe gether vppon hepe wherwyth endeth dyspycyons concernynge knowelege chyrche ended falleth dispycyons preachyng mater tytle boke wyt whyche chyrche vnto two great coclusyons god hath sayth wryten harte electes tone sayth fayth cryste whych knowe god honoured therby fele perceyue well inough wythin theyre owne harte yt sacramentes tyndale sayeth bare sygnes memoryales none effectuall instrumentes grace sacramente auter nothynge brede statche second conclusyon loue theyr neyghbours selfe whyche suffycyently iudge sayeth betwene good euyll ryght wronge goodly vngoodly couersacyon dedes lawes bergaynys couenauntes ordynaunces decree men knoweth offyce euery degree dewe honour euery person ye may well perceyue euer haue lesse knowlege tyndale owne doctryne none electe syth god hath hym self wryte coclusyons fully theyr hertes tyndale nedeth yt semeth make longe sermon though fered yet wyth goodly quyppe agaynste cum patre qui lakkyng exhortacyon ende men sholde therfore pull downe tenterden steple sholde sandwyche hauen amende pull chyrches ye realme sholde nede policy make mery synne though synne chyrche catholike knowen chyrch chyrche telleth v fynall specyall profe worde chyrch h double interpretacyon carnall israel spyrytuall israell euen yt chyrche great hygh secrete mistery man teacheth v selfe haue tolde hym redy mo tymes hande hath fyngers chyrche good badde yet yt chyrch arche noe ryght fygure therof hadde therin clene vnclene menne also electes good noe hys awne sonnes one ye wote well bad genesis owne father accursed hym parable sauyour sygnyfyeth net chyrche matth catcheth kepeth good fyshe bad tyll yt come oute e wauys worlde vnto banke tother nette hys shyppe one thynke alone lo euen begynnynge brought tyndale hym selfe suffycyet mater part agaynst thynge clerely prouynge onely catholyke chyrche trew conterfete false yt pleaseth hym ieste say euen nowe none byleue theyr mouthes moued authoryte theyr elder onely none theym byleue mayster more fayth pope fayth deuyls fayth whyche maye stonde mayster confesseth maner abomynacyons haue ryghte fayth christe chyrche euery man well seeth howe lowde bylyeth foly layeth forth thys lytle space fyrste neuer sayed man byleueth wyth hys mouth whyche though member wyth whych man bounden confesse hys fayth yet member wyth whyche man byleueth thenne h le therfore thys poynte tyndale belyeth onys ouer sayde neuer men byleue moued au horyte theyr elder onely say sauinge credence gyuen authoryte helpeth forth therfore wyllynge wyth hys supernaturall grace towarde inclynacion reason assent obedyence fayth whole catholyke chyrche neuer syke sore synnes besyde yet ledde trouth bylyefe spyryte god thys haue euer sayed therfore tyndale bylyeth twyse sayth fayth whyche may sta de confesse wyth maner abomynacyons ryght fayth cryste hys chyrche sayth pope fayth fayth deuyls ryght fayth onely repente fele lawe good haue lawe god wryten theyr harte fayth oure sauyour iesus euyn spyryte god saye thynge saye fayth alone maye stande wyth abomynable dedes tyndalys owne felynge fayth feleth affermeth sam tyndale sayeth hys electes hauynge hys felynge fayth may frute synne remaynynge theym brekynge oute theyr frayle membres fall ryghte horryble dedes yet theyre faythe standeth stylle therewyth neuer fayleth tyme bycause therof horryble dedes neuer greate abomynacyons yet dedely synne tyndale thus playnely sayth ye haue selfe sene fourth boke playnely foloweth vppon hys tale wyth hys owne felynge fayth maner abomynacyo maye stande howres dayes monethes yeres abyde dwell togyther ye se playnely selfe therfore ye se also playnely syth neuer sayd tyndale reherseth men may byleue wyth theyr mouth neuer comended fayth alone suffycyet tyndale bereth hande makyng fayth alone myne sayd fayth may alone onely wythout vertues stande also abomynable dedes vyce sayd yet fayth alone tyndale sayth hym selfe hys owne felynge fayth alone accompanyed wolde haue seme hope cheryte thynges beyng thus lyketh hym self well weneth iesteth properly camell daunseth callynge fayth pope fayth deuyls fayth euery man wene well marketh mater wyll lykely call hys propre scoffe colde conceyt goffe founde tok vp sottys hoffe say tyndale yet agayne ferforth perteyneth onely nature fayth wyt bare bylyefe alone fayth maye stande wyth maner ahomynacyon ryght fayth trewe saye though bothe ryght trewe yet suffycyent bryng man heuyn yf onely maye also stande wyth kynde abomynable synne bycause lewd luther fayth tindal fayth saye fayth alone fayth coupled abomynable synne fayth alone saye bylyefe alone ryght fayth bylyefe poynt whyche haue redy proued hym mych ofte dare well saye hymselfe hath sayde masse thys moneth therfore wyll laboure mych say trouth thynge playne open selfe sauynge thimportune bablynge heretykes man sholde euer haue neded go aboute profe sholde go proue thyng saynt good wurkes affyrmyng ia dede dede nature fayth dede vnto state saluacyon men whome oure sauyour spake sayth lucae let dede men theyr dede men folowe thou ment suppose men naturally ded dede sholde bere dede corp beryenge ye sayth tyndale yet thys ryght fayth cryste saye yes farre belongeth onely fayth saye onely bylyefe poyntes artycles cryste wyll haue v bounden byleue yet sayth tyndale thys fayth suffycyent saluacyon yf haue bothe hope cheryte nedeth tyndale tell v tale dyd eue say nay yet fayth hope cheryte thre dyuers dystincte vertues saynt poule sayth fayth hope cheryte greter cheryte yet sayth tyndale tho e thre thre systers neuer asuder euer hath one hath playne vntrew yf heresye trew euer fayth thre euer thre euer neded bycause false heresye lest byleueth ryght artycles hystorycall fayth man getteth hym self onely naturall power wurke god soule therfore faith faynt feble soone gone agayne therfore ryght fayth chrysten fayth ryghte fayth wrought wryten alway god hym selfe mane harte therfore neuer withoute hope cheryte wrought wryten within harte togyther fayth therfore felyuge ayth neuer fayle ther n neuer ceace hope well wurke well thys trouth whole somme effect tyndale holy tale wherin dyd somwhat yf wolde onys proue v halfe fyrst denye yt euery historicall faith yt say euery hystorycall bylyefe credece faynt feble soone gone tindale sayth se profe inough wyth many men standeth styll theyr lyfe thynge trewe fal e false story machomet many turkes take trewe wyll withstandyng many suffycyet cause wherfore reason sholde reken false wyll saye yet obstynacy stand styll therin abyde bond slaues chrysten contrees vppon border turkaye ye dyde theron rather byleue contrary saye forther trewe man bylyefe artycles chryste fayth geteth bylyefe hym selfe naturall power wythout helpe god wurkynge wyth hym yet speke bare bylyefe cheryte yet ioyned wyth syth euery man seketh bylyefe endeuoreth hym self therto purposeth therby seke way saluacyon corrupte nature man neuer begyn entre iournaye walke forth one fote therin yf bothe fyrste preuented grace haue walke wyth hym styll iohan sauyour sayth wythout ye nothynge lyke wyse man maye goddes helpe calleth vppon euery man entre towarde bylyefe yet leue agayne ere gete byleue one poynt yet leue maye go forth wyth god poyntes bylyefe yet leue lacke hope maye olso go forth bylyefe hope ye ouer greate hope yet purpose flesshely delyte whyche mynde leue maye leue lacke cheryte though deuyll maye besyde thynges verely knoweth byleue suche artycles wyth preuencyon grace mych beyng perpetually dampned bylyefe furtheraunce towarde saluacion therfore hym mater wurke grace yet man whome faythe goddes ordynaunce prouyded waye toward saluacion tough way two longe lane besyde fayth therfore may leue lystere come ye lanys end wytte hope charyte yet neuer fynde ye enterynge fyrste lane wytte fayth neuer sette forth fote forwarde yt yf god worke wyth wyll sauour sayth man come father drawe hym fallen depe pytte then drawen drawen brynke botome lyke wise god draweth draweth euen begynnynge casteth downe cord grace take holde vpon wheruppon taketh hold holdeth styll god drawen vnto god helpeth hym selfe drawen saynt poule sayth helpe forth wyth god say also god hath wrought wyth mannys wyll called hym preuencyon grace yeres dyscrecyon eyther iudaisme fro gentylyty fyndynge lette man hath baptysme fully infounded fayth wyth hope cheryte put hym state grace whych wrytyng harte euer herde man hauynge nowe fayth alone hope cheryte standynge suche state grace yf deceaced soule sholde forthe flye blysse byfore body colde yet doth infusyon fayth grace thefte auowtry leseth charyte alway custome synne somtyme hope leueth bare fayth say bylyefe alone somtyme false doctrine heretykes leseth aud yet fayth alone good kepte ye peyces fragmentes fayth also meanes whyche man maye easely come remanaunt hath loste lakketh helpe wyth goddes forther helpe kepe man synne though kepe hym man falleth thefte somtyme remembereth yet baptyme beynge deuyll entyced kyll man maketh crosse vppon brest prayeth crist kepe hym aduowtry lyke wyse god good mynde preueteth man grace worketh wyth hys wyll kepynge hym therefro gaue hym good thoughtes offred hym grace yf wold haue taken holde therof kepe hym tother doute yf god left hym one l te god tother deuyll wyth brought god great goodnes begyled hym made hym madde brayne hath vttred hym selfe thynges pene sauyour sayenge hym self yt mouth speketh abudaunce fulnesse herte muste nedes make euery man fele euen fyngers ende tyndale botome hys harte wyth fulsome felynge fayth feleth foule fylthy hepe false sumblynge heresyes yet fayth worse fayth alone whyche calleth deuyls fayth myne saynte iamys sayth deuyls byleue tremble also drede thou sayeth tyndale euery suche tyndale felyng fayth sayth yt great god yt may many horryble dedes wythout dedly synne art worse ye deuyll bycause thou doste drede bysydes syth tyndale teacheth suche felynge fayth fayth sayth saue soule yt teacheth therwyth toward getyng therof man chylde bygettynge owne father say mo e lesse ryght nought doth teachynge teache euery man syt styll go nothynge aboute yt sayth good workes nothynge wyll necessaryly sprynge felyng fayth yet lyke leues rather frut sayth shall neuer haue rewarde heuen b yt damnable thynke euer shold tho gh wold wordes byd men yet doth tale strongly teache contrarye byleueth hym shall leue theym vndone teacheth repentaunce wythout shryft penauce sayth ye shryft inuencyon deuyll could euer haue comen felyng false fayth yf deuyls owne hand fumbled herte passe ouer false fayth sacrametes calling crist blessed body bare cakebrede sterche doctryne lecherye betwene freres nunnes many madde fransyes mo techeth besyde one thynge inough may serue gether teacheth felynge fayth onely serue saluacyon wythout whych sheweth euery mau must nedes go deuyll fayth putteh none sayth frutelesse teachynge therwythall towarde getynge fayth whyche excepte gete muste nedes denyll man thynge good endeuour techeth vayn man labour yt myche pray therfore hys herte onys wyshe yt syth coulde wyth suche thynge helpe thynge towarde yt forsuch desyre thynge nerer syt euen styll let god worke alone yf fele good mynde neuer labour kepe sent kepe yf lyste yf wyll man yf wyll man shall nede nothyng yf wold tornyng towarde god hachette mannys hande though may manys hand wurke vppon tree yet canne yt owne nature thynge helpe selfe moue turne backe towarde man thys tyndalys teachynge thys y hys owne ensample wherby sheweth v canne nothynge turnynge towarde god god doth alone thys dothe tyndale tell v well boldely dare thynge aferde god cryeth contrary mouth salomon sayth turne agayne thou sunamyte turne agayne sayth also canti turne wyll turne wolde prophete wene haue sayd hys hachet zachar sayth also turne ye shall saued lyke man coulde turne wythout god cryste wolde saye wythout ye nothynge yf tother syde man coulde hym tyndale onely techeth v vngracyouse lesson whyche wolde make men loke grace lacke theyr owne endeuoure maye wurthy lese also syth techeth v fayth euery man dampned techeth v also ge tyng therof man nothyng techeth say two thinges togither euery wreched wylfull beste lay weyght wrechednes malyce hys wreched wyll vnto prouydence predestynacyon god syth thys y hygh heresye sore blasphemynge hyghe maiestye god saye tyndalys felynge faythe y yet farre wurse onely bare faythe alone also thenne faythe lesse euyll neuer haue herde god neuer h ue thought hym neyther byleue god bestely blaspheme hym tyndale calleth fayth alone fayth pope deuyll fayth pope hath selfe eyther god shalbe iudge tyndale surely hys owne felynge fayth hym selfe erely declareth double deuelyshe deuyls fayth dede fyrste poynt saynt iamys speketh bycause hys malepert presumpcyon affyrmynge felynge fayth maye myche horryble dedes wythout dedely synne therfore saynt iamys sayeth oute drede god therin worse deuyll whyche bothe beleueth trymbleth also drede secundely hys felynge fayth wurse deuyls deuyll byleueth body cryste blessed sacrament aulter fereth trymbleth gyueth reuerence therto ye vnto image crystes crosse also hath euery ag bene proued sundry place chrystendome dayly appereth yet tyndale calleth blessynge crossyng waggyng folkes fyngers ayre fereth lyke one wolde length wagge hempe wynd mocke myracles say deuyll fleeth fro folkes blessy ge men fle chyldren faynyng selfe aferd lyste sporte playe fereth mocke sacrament blessed body god full lyke stretche hempe call cake brede starche yt clere sonne shynynge trewth goddes wordes dependeth vpon trewth congregacyon syth ye se good reders clere sonne shyuynge man sayde contrarye questyon betwene v whyther goddes worde trewe bycause syth se well say oure questyon thyng maketh goddes worde trew meane men knowe goddes worde trewe meane men know whyche trew word god whether know whyche trew gospell meane teachynge knowen catholyke ye tyndale standeth bakke prompteth hym eare wyse say thou byleuest bycause thou felest yt trew uery well properly answered wyll aske one questyo twayn wherfore byleue good worke shalbe rewarded heuen freres may lawfully wedde nunes blessed sacrament auter nothyng cake brede starche twenty suche questyons mo tyndale teacheth hym thus answere thou wotest feleste yt trewe asketh thow knowest yt trew answere bycause yt wryten thyne herte yf aske wrote yt answere spyryte god yf aske thou camest fyrst yt tell hym whether redynge bokes hearyng yt preached outward instrument inwardly thou waste taught spyryt god yf aske whether thou byleueste yt bycause yt wryten bokes bycause prestes preache answere bycause write thyne herte bycause spyryte god preacheth testyfyeth vnto thy soule saye though begynnyng thou w st moued redynge preachyng samarytanis wordes woman yet thou byleuest yt therfore lenger bycause thou haste h rd yf spyryte god red yt wryten thyne herte lo good reders ye se tyndale hath instructed dyscyple make answere suffycyent euery thynge may asked hym whole e ecte wherof standeth gether two thynges fyrste poyntes fayth byleueth bycause feleth theym wryten hys harte spyryte god seconde though came fyrste vnto writyng preachyng fyrste byleued theym wrytyng redde preachynge herd samarytanys dyd woman wordes yet byleueth hym therfore onely bycause redeth yt wryten spyryte god hys harte mych outwarde meane prechyng redyng fyrst meane whych cam therto meane regardeth hath leger respect hys bylyefe therunto therfore syth nowe comen hygh poynte felynge fayth whyche redeth wryten spyryte god hys harte bookes iiii euangelystes trewe scrypture god byleueth better poynt bycause catholyke chyrche sayth wyll therfore aske thys good scoler tyndale whyther fele wryten hys harte spyryte god hath better fayth perfayte saynt austayne god myracle turned hym fayth wryte agaynst manicheys whose false secte god called hym peradueture questyo wyll somwhat seme strauge dyscyple tyndale bycause none whyche hys mayster hath taught hym make answere yet thynke conclusyo hys mayster wyll aduyse hym saye feleth hym selfe haue perfayt bylyefe saynt austayne suche thynge saynt austayne byleued bothe leste euery man shold fele mayster scoler proue proud fole tother syde yf cofesse fele owne fayth perfayt saynt austayns byleue hys owne mynde saynt austayne trewe poynt bylyefe commune vnto bothe full fayth perfayte wyll aske hym wherfore doth byleue scrypture styll authoryte chyrche well saynt austayne dyd styll wrote hym selfe agaynste manicheys sayd wolde byleue gospell yf authoryte chyrche moued therto byleued authoryte chyrche alwaye styll yet dare saye tyndale suppose dare saye contrary spyryte god hadde well wryten conclusyon hys harte holy harte dyscyple tyndale whome tyndale teacheth answere v contrary thus concernynge knowlege scrypture whyche pryncypall mater tyndals answere chyefe poynte yf proue hys scolers fayth better saynt austayns hys answere techeth hys dyscyple worth rysshe let v artycles aske thys good scoler tyndale syth feleth fyndeth herte wryte spyryte god freres monkes haue vowe forsaken flesshe may lawfully fall fysshe woman flesshe vnder name weddyng make stewed strupettes nonnes feleth also lyke felyng fayth good workes nought worth shall rewarded heuen feleth also false felyng fayth blessed sacrament awter neyther precyouse body bloude chryste onely cake brede wyne starche stede brede shall aske hym saye therfore questyon whyche hys mayster hath bouden hym make answere wyt came fyrst thys fayth saye hystorycall fayth byfore spyryte god wyth wrytynge theym hys harte caused hym bothe rede fele answere thys questyon tyndale sayth scoler tell hym whyther redyng bokes heryng preched uery well syth mayster byddeth hym tell v wolde praye hym tell v whyther prechyng redynge bokes thys wyll wene answere lerned thynges prechynge aske hym whose prechyng came muste fayne saye prechynge hys owne mayster wyllyam tyndale luther lambert huyskyn suinglius suche apostaticall prechers thys shall tell hym agayne syth felyng fayth wryten ye spyryte harte maysters owne tale tyll fyrst byleued thinges hystoricall fayth herynge holy prechers muste thentent maye lede v fayth dyd hym tell v reason byleue seynge neyther men lernynge wytte mych vertue saynt austayn saynt hierom sait basyle saynt cyprian saynt chrysostom saynt grygory warre perysshe loste countrees compelled leue r ceyue language stede therof fayth neu r fayle canne catholyke chyrche agaynste whyche sauyour hath hym selfe promysed heretykes rebelle agaynste tyrauntes vppon erth insourge oppugne whyche two sortes gate hell shall neuer obtayne preuayle lyke wyse deuyls hell wythin hell walkynge thys world bysy aboute gate hell shall neuer able destroye fayth sauyour hath lyke wyse promysed agaynste deuyll went syfte hys chyrche sholde preserued kepte meane hys owne specyall prayour therfore syth grammer laten tong thyng may fayle trewe fayth thynge spyrite god accordynge crystes promyse perpetually taught vnto hys chyrche ioh n therfore canne neuer fayle though bokes worlde sholde fayle therfore hys symylytude gramer lykened vnto fayth lyke apple oyster touchynge olde autentyke storyes speketh whyche sayth chyrche broughte slepe wherwyth sayeth luther tyndale huyskyn suynglius confounde lye wolde fayne one story whyche proueth fastynge prayenge almoyse dedes done fayth hope cheryte noughte worth neuer shall haue rewarde heuen olde story proueth folke shold pray theyr frendes soules old story wyll shew v crysten woman prestes wonte synge masse olde storye make yt good blessed sacrament neyther fleshe bloode onely bare brede wyne olde story new founden make v knowe freres monkes professed olde wonte wedde nunnes well alowed myche commended therin sure poyntes except last shall fynde vnto folke many olde autentyque storyes prouynge theyr heresyes false howe yt laste dede fynde farre remembre olde storyes agaynste yt suppose veryly vntyll frere luther beganne late neuer wreche bestely euer durste shame attepte incestuouse maryage byfore yf yt onely iulianus apostata whyche fell forthwyth fro fayth became false paynym sence theym brynge forth place ouer fynall confusyon poynte ye haue selfe herde fourth boke perpetuall vyrgynyte oure ladye hath hym selfe confessed euer yt taughte muste byleue yt yet yt proued holy maase well ye wote good reders doth hym selfe betwene heretykes chyrche questyon parte wordes scrypture vppon ryght sentence vnderstandynge scripture lay therin agaynste theym olde auncyent doctours whose exposycyons cotemne reward good workes fastynge blessed sacrament vowes chastyte yf wolde stande vnto exposycyons olde holy doctours vppon scrypture neuer auoyde yt scryptures clere parte agaynste ellys haue often sayde let tyndale tell v one many sayntes synnes apostle tyme haue wryten vppon scrypture byfore luther day expowned scrypture wyse yt exposycyon lawefull frere wedde nunne sentence yf tyndale turke borne bycause layeth often turkes parte agay ste v wolde well myghte reken hym proude fole yf wold begynne constre theyr alcharon great necessary poyntes theyr fayth agaynste contynuall fayth fro apostle day vnto theyr owne may myche better call proude presumptuous folys myght turkes teachynge contrary construccyon theyr alcharon besydes ensample iewis wyll helpe hym nother cause olde exposytours theyre scryptures bothe moses prophetes vppon parte cryste apostle consequently catholyque chyrche contynually agaynst false scrybes pharysyes false doctoures synnes suche necessary poyntes vary appereth well dyuers theyr bok whych dayly brought forth allegged men day lerned theyr tonge also substancyall well lerned man lyre hys exposycyon seconde psalme yf tyndale luther huiskyn suingli say yt old holy doctours expositours vpon scrypture dyd euer expoune theyr exposycyon myghte appere scrypture cryste appereth lawfull abhorreth thynge abomynable freres sholde wedde nonnes wyll agre wyth tyndale gyue ouer mater thus ye se good reders concernynge scrypture tyndale techeth dyscyple say alledge elder chyrche thys xiiiic yere syth debate variaunce wordes wherin bothe agre sentece wherin onely comen contynued fayth chrysten nacyos also olde holy doctours sayntes euer synnys scrypture wryte agreeth catholike chyrch agaynst hym hys alledgyng scrypture worth leke therfore dreuen euer vary leue scrypture aske wherfore byleueth eyther thys fayne muste holde hym onely hys felynge fayth tyndale shote ancre techeth hym say byleueth onely bycause feleth wryten hys harte wythout reasonable outwarde cause wherfore fyrste byleued wyth story fayth wherof ye haue herde hys heresyes proue v none syth comen poynt without good outwarde cause muste defende hys fayth hys onely felynge may turkes iewes bothe whome layeth sore agaynst v defende theyr faythes agaynste hym selfe sam ferther saye feleth trew eche theyrs false may eche answere hym fele theyrs trewe hys false thus gone counsayle saynt peter e sholde geue reason hope euery man wyl aske v wherfore hope therfore leuynge saynt peter hys way lette euery man folowe tyndale byleue lyste saye feleth wryten hys owne harte wyth goddes owne hande men saye whyche hath bene onys hierusalem may lye authoryte bycause shall sure seldome mete man hath whome hys tale myghte controlled tyndale hath lye without controllement wyth lesse labour sought shorter waye hym selfe thynketh surer goeth onys dore therfore saye lyste tell v feleth trewe fyndeth wryten wythin hys harte hym wryte false spyryte god hym selfe weneth hym selfe surer yf wente twyse hierusalem twyse farre beyonde yet myghte fortune fynde man hadde waye walked farre founden tyndalys tale false sayeth feleth wryten wythin hys owne harte weneth hym selfe sure thynketh veryly ther canne man loke controlle hym se whyther lye yet wyly inuencyon tyndale y therin begyled god hath gone beyonde hym made hys wyly foly founden playnely late appered came controllement selfe wyly foly rycharde webbe thys webbe whyle chauncelloure kynges hyghnesse dyuers heretykes detectyd vnto solde vsed contynually sell many heretykes bookes forboden kynges gracyouse proclamacyon brought realme ferther good honeste men enfourmed brystowe dwelled pestylent bookes throwen strete lefte mennys dores nyght durste offer theyr poysen sell wolde theyr attached lyke mater whyche hadde receyued docer bookes webbe afterwarde abiured hys heresyes gaue commyssyon certayne good wurshypfull folke brystowe attache rycharde webbe wheruppon suertyes fouden appere byfore went large commynge vppe london daye came gate hym saynte catheryns robert necton vttered hys bokes fell secrete agrement wyth hym eche sholde saye therin examyned therof whan webbe thought made mater saufe sure came boldely shrewdely bygyled yet ere came necton ferynge webbe myghte happe tell treuth thoughte wolde hym self hym sent worde greate haste webbys beynge wyth hym communycacyon hadde ben bytwene theym webbe vnware therof beynge examyned morow fyrst dyuers thynges answered othe many false answere well perceyued sauynge salue hys remembraunce euer parte referred restraynyd hys remembraunce done saw found fawte nothynge obiected agaynst answer vsed selfe though byleued beganne loke pytuously vpon sayd euer herd hys examynacyon trew playne vnto ben alwaye wont fynde good fauorable sayd cause hym selfe shewed euer hys stomake playnely knewe hym selfe vpon hys fayth hys remembrauce wherupon shewed hym yf founde hym trew sholde fynde fauourable fered answerys trew syr quod yf ye fynde one false neuer good lord vnto neuer trust whyle ye lyue say thought hys many lye assay hym one asked hym agayne one syr nycholas answered neuer sold suche bookes preste holy sayntes xv hundred yere space chrysten people besyde good man crystendome feleth fyndeth wryten goddes hande hys owne herte tyndale feleth fowle fylthy heresye wryten herte hande god yf fele yt catholyque chyrche hystoricall fayth thynge aught yt full heresyes besyde therfore yt chyrch heretyques sayd ende goodly solucyon fyrste argument therfore yt go sayth chyrche syth hym chyrche muste definycyon chirch nedes electes haue owne definycyon also felynge fayth wryten theyr hertes goddes owne hande demaunde aske tyndale therfore yt happeneth holy electes faythfull felynge folke gone fro catholyque chyrche fele one fayth great necessarye poyntes fayth fele eche contrarye fayth eche theym feleth eche calleth false fumblynge heretykes though false shrewes conspyre agree gether agaynste trew catholyke chyrche yet theyre contrary sectes vary betwene selfe lutheranys anabaptystes huyskyns swynglianis wyth many sectes mo wolde one byte nothers nose complayne heretyques punyshed yet one secte punysheth kylleth noher among selfe thus good reders ye may easely se yt theyr felyng faythes dissonaunt amonge selfe contraryouse repugnaunte wryten theyr harte tyndale sayth hande god whose spyryte inspyrer vnyte concorde peace tolde byfore brethed blowen brothel brestes spyryt dyscorde debate dyssencyon deuyll yet better perceyuynge tyndale doctryne concernynge fayth consyder one agayne good reders yt putteth two kyndes fayth hystoricall fayth felyng faith euery person hath faith yt tyndale one two kynd eyther hystorycall fayth felynge fayth hystoricall fayth artycles fayth putteth byleuynge necessary trewth atteyned goten outwarde meane herynge thynge preached redynge yt wryten fayth calleth faynte feble vnable eyther laste endure worke well conclusyon deuylles fayth tother kynde fayth wyt felyng fayth sayth fayth god wryteth hym self mannes herte therfore felyng fayth hath yt herte goddes owne wrytynge hath yt yt neuer w shed oute must necessite dwell abyde hym neuer fayle shall fele yt herte felynge therof shall necessyte make hym loue god euer euer worke well neuer dedely sy ne though neuer many deuylyshe dedes thorow frute synne remaynynge fleshe brekynge oute frayle member good reders let v begyn storye fayth syth sayth ca neyther endure worke well wold wyt hym whether yf man dye forth wyth sone hath yt wyth good purpose baptysed worke well yf lyued therto suche mynde many martyres dyed byfore theyr cristendome shold saued wyth hystorycall fayth wythout ferther felynge fayth shall may ye historycall fayth suf ycyet saluacion ye though yt faynt yt yt may fayle yet may per ase laste longe fayle man maye wyth yt worke prayour fastynge almouse dede well leste wyse cornelius centurio paynym dyd wythout yt yf suche place could baptysed lakke mynyster dyed wyth repentaunce synne suche hystorycall fayth workynge wythout farther felynge sholde saued tyndale say yes sayth somwhat hystorycall fayth stande wordes byfore yf saye naye syth man parte byleue well well felynge fayth tyndale speketh must god infounded towarde getynge wherof man hym selfe sayth tyndale chyl e bygetynge owne father trow tyndale shall haue man well cosydereth great good nature god geue credence poynte yf tyndale saye suche case god dothe vnto hym byleueth onys wyth story fayth infounde felynge fayth thereto except man haue parte let impedyment synne say therby confesseth mannys endeuour inclynyng vnderstannyng seruice hystoricall fayth hath yet lest wise somwhat done toward getynge felynge fayth whyche onely fayth tyndale calleth ryght fayth chyld getynge owne father lyeth tyndale tale duste say also yt sholde seme farther tyndale hystorycall fayth one goten god shold let good congruence infounde felynge fayth hym wystandynge synnes whyche man goynge caryed forth frayltye rage concupiscence reygnynge rulyng weke sykly member letteth kepe styll wythout faylynge tyme felynge fayth onys haue yt wythstandyng horryble abomynable edes euer shold yt appere gete one hystorycall fayth hath alwaye forthwith felyng fayth also though way towarde doynge ye though doynge dede neuer great horryble myschyefe fall therto frayltye shall lakke felynge faythfull wreches ye shall fynde inough say also yf hystoricall fayth goten man wyth good cyrcumstaunces man possybylyte may put vnto yt god doth euer adde infounde felynge fayth hym selfe supplyenge congruence owne goodnesse inbecyllyte lakke power vppon mannys parte towarde atteynynge owne saluacyon beynge great hyghe gyfte god farre aboue proporcyon mannys naturall state saye loste destroyed effecte tyndale deuysyon betwene hystoricall fayth felynge fayth euery man onys hath well tone sure tother wythout whiche hys good workes toward rewarde wrought vayne whiche thyng lyberall goodnes god coulde cogruence lacke vpon hys owne parte suffre thus ye tone halfe dyuysyon wyt hystorycall fayth ye se good reders poynt tyndale brought cosyder speke hystorycall fayth fayth necessary poyntes bylyefe atteyned goten man outward meany onely thynke myn owne selfe hystoricall fayth attayned without inwarde wurkyng god bycause tyndale putteth therfore thus reasone thentent ye sholde therby se thynge trouth wolde wurke vppon tyndals vntrewe posycyon haue also forborne whyle speke thyng sacrament baptysme bycause tyndale hys mater fayth bothe hystoricall fayth felyng fayth neuer maketh mencyon therof though sacrament parte thys playe whyche obstynate sylece men may wel perceyue meneth though spake yet make hym somwhat saye therin shall seconde parte hys dyuysyon wytte consyderynge hys felynge fayth lytell appose hym therin aske hym therfore tyme begynnynge tourned togyther fayth two thre thousande onys dyd prechynge saynt peter appereth seconde chapyter actes u theruppon chrystened toke theyr baptysme hadde therby bysyde hystorycall fayth goten prechynge new kynde fayth new felyng theyr formar fayth infounded god theyr baptysme yf towchynge fayth bylyefe hystorycall faith goten outward meane good full fayth god infounded inwardly truste tyndale doth thynke hadde suche fayth able serue saluacyon truely turned yf forth wyth vpon theyr baptysme deceaced yf tyndale take tother parte answere yt baptysme felynge fayth infounded foloweth saye euery man age dyscrecyon whiche dewly cometh baptysme hath felynge fayth syth hath baptysme ryghte fayth fayth suffycyent saluacyon whyche tyndale none felynge fayth therby come dewly baptysme tyndals tale electes euerychone yet semeth ferther tyndals tale mayster martin added vnto yt yf come baptysme vndewly wyt walkyng outwarde yet waye toward aduowtry sacrylege murder bringe bylyef baptysme perfyteth tyndals grauntynge god infoundeth snffycyent perfeccyon fayth baptysme affermyng perfayt fayth hauer therof may horryble dedes neuer fayle perfayt felynge fayth canne sayd consyderyng tyndals tale horryble dedes perfayt felynge fayth maye abyde gyther perceyue se dedes beyng yet ye course towarde doyng sholde let ye perfeccyon fayth god infounded shold let kepte preserued specyally syth tyndals owne wurshypfull mayster marten luther sayth expressely chrysten man dapned yf wyll byleue nothynge sayth dampne hym onely vnbylyefe synnys sayth supped vp swalowed onys bylyefe therfor come baptysme onely bare bylyef synnes luther calleth hys horryble dedes tindale calleth frayltye hy flesshe baptysme cometh h fro fonte nothyng lette perfeccyon god infounded hys baptysme syth yt perfec yo mu te tyndale eyther felyng fayth el felyng faythe whyle hym none faythe suffycyent foloweth euery man whyche hystorycall fayth cometh baptisme sure ye feling faith many synnys euer ab nte feblenes rayl ye comytte yf tindale wyll make styckyng tell age discrecyon come vnto baptisme say may som lette vppon theyr parte reason may synne wyllyngly eyther purpose malyce lette v consyder waye well thys mater come baptysme wythout maner lette chyldren baptysed whyche kynde fayth haue hystorycall fayth felynge fayth fayth haue muste ellys canne neuer stande goddes fauoure saued wytnessynge saynte poule wythout fayth impossyble please god therfore trouth faith haue though come baptysme receyued font fayth theyr father hole chyrch offereth yet ye baptysme god infouded grate habyt fayth hope cheryte wherwith made forth perfayte mebres hys mystycall body catholyke chyrch erth therby made iheritable vnto yt blesse heue aske therfore tyndale kynde fayth hystorycall fayth felyng f yth hystoricall trow ye chyldren haue yet neyther redde herd many storyes wherfore must nedes tyndals tale felyng fayth mo kyndes faith putteth twayne none suffycyent saluacyon onely one suffycyent muste fayth chylde receyueth baptysme ellys chylde neuer rather saued case dyed many chyldren chrysome cloth cradle peraduenture tindale gessyng wher go wyll say baptysme god infoudeth felyng fayth say hys onely electes theyr harte writeth infoudeth reprobate wyll happely say agred doctours chyrch god gyueth ye baptysme lyke grace euery chylde vnto thys answere though baptysme eyther goodnes instat prayour ye father godfather hylde cause seene vnto hyghe wysdom gyue one greter grace yet gyueth one kynde grace one kinde fayth though dyffer degree man hath lytle stature hath great pygmey geaunt tyndale sayth hym selfe answere vnto dyaloge wurkes muste perfayt wurk cryst hym selfe fayth sayth suffycyent though neuer lytell besyde thys sayed god gyueth vnto e ery chylde baptysme haby e hat fayth suffycyent saluacyon th sayth ty dale n ne felynge fayth ergo tyndale felynge fayth wherof habyt god infoundeth euery chylde baptysme yet syth haue proued yf chylde haue fayth hath tyndals tale felyng fayth ow wyll tyndale peraduenture saye habyte ayth fayth bycause actuall fayth whych hath lacke vse reason want whero e thynke vppon actually consent vnto poynte faythe vnto thys answere maye reason saye chylde hath reasonable soule bycause thynke vpon reasonynge therfore lacketh specyficall kyndely dyfference dyuydeth kynde man kyndes vnreasonable brutyshe bestes chylde man cal e also yf habituall fayth fayth chyld baptysme styll oute state grace ellys muste tyndale say saynt poule sayed vntrew hebrae tha tolde hebrues wythout fayth impossyble please god besydes thys yf habytuall fayth fayth lacke actuall thynkynge theruppon dyeth euery man fayth happeth dye hys slepe neuer good greate actuall ayth went bedde man shall saued fayth onys fayth hath whyche h dyeth therfore trouth habytuall bylyefe chylde bylyefe though actuall byleuyng thynkynge vppon fayth habytuall reason chylde reason though actuall reasonynge makynge yllogysmys thenne saye story ayth therfore tyndals tale none felynge fayth syth putteth mo kyndes fayth none ayth su ycyent goddes wurke perfyte infoundeth baptysme none suffycyent fayth though thys trouth habytuall fayth fayth infounded god wyth sacrament baptysme euery chyld euery chyld hath therby felyng faith yf tindale tell v trew yet put argument shall shortely strayne tyndale graut farther thynge ellys forsake mayster ye shall vnderstande though chyrche tea heth habytull fayth chyldren suffycyent yet cometh tyndale mayster martyn luther boke make h agaynst anabaptistes teacheth longe processe yonge chyldren ha e founded actuall fayth dede therfore tyndale scoler maye denye crystened chyldren haue fayth syth hystorycall lakke redynge storyes muste nedes whyle hildren yt neuer sinne dedely theyr liues though neuer many horryble dedes bycause tyndale sayth felynge fayth euery one hath yt borne god hath seed hym may well horryble dedes neuer dedely synne doth mych mysse rayle ieste vpo ye wote well tyndale neuer gete net whyle leueth whyche folyshe false felynge fayth hath wrapped hym yf refuse onely doctryne catholyke chyrche cryste owne hym selfe clerely cotayned gospell hys chyrche neuer brought dampnable errour yf myghte suerty neyther doctryne scrypture selfe tother syde yf sholde graunte doctryne catholyke chyrche trewe theyr tyndale one whose chyrche ye haue harde redy secunde shall frere baro whose chyrche wyll som shewe fynysshe thys worke thus endeth vii boke pthe viii boke whyche confuted doctour baron chyrche frere baron maketh tytle hys processe concernynge chyrch thys wyse holy chyrche therof wherby men maye knowe tytle hys processe begynneth playe tyndalys parte fyrste flyttynge poynt wyt whole catholyke chyrche vnto clergye alone lyke maner raylyng surely notwithstandynge man myghte wen tyndale suche fonde scoffynge perelesse yet doth frere baron farre outrune hym ylynge draggeth behynd hym reasonyng wherin wyth tyndale baron hold fote downright tindale halteth therin frere baron lashethe agaynste theym pryde pompe theyr lyues spent whoredome though good preste catholyke chyrche tyll leue putteth chyrche cumpany onely suche neuer synne dedely therfore neuer chyrche calleth theym waye repentauntes yet sheweth somtyme repente caryed forth theyr synne long ere repent neyther agreeth wyth hyther haue hys euangelycall doctryne accepted kynge openly receyued realme whyche sore hath trauayled regender agayne vnto god trew fayth bu menes false scrybes pharas y reiected rebuked sauynge kynges saufe conduc sholde haue standen parell burned hys bok wyth hym whyche saufe conducte bycause graunted vi weekes thenne almost passed whyche cause chaunged hys notable monstrouse apparayle came
