thus good christen reders tha shame se barn answereth wordes cry whyche playnely proue chyrche cryste knowen chyrche auoydynge wherof barn tryfle suche fasshyon boldely carelesse semeth reken euer shall rede wyser almoste euyn wylde goose yf euer thoughte man sholde rede shold haue wytte hys hed man wolde wene haue bene full sore ashamed handle thys mater chrystes owne holy wordes suche tryflynge maner doth yet sayth barn thys knowen catholyke chyrche chyrch bycause persecuted chyrch sayth barn inuenteth none way heuen foloweth chryste onely sufferynge oppressyons persecucyos blasphemynges thynges may layed vnto hyr whyche saynte austayne sayth lerned mayster cryste holy mother chyrche thorow worlde scatered farre longe trew hedde chryste iesus taught hath lerned fere contumely crosse yet deth y strengthed resystynge sufferynge wordes euery man seeth well touch clergye onely yet maketh barn ment mo meneth hym selfe hys holy felowes chyrch bycause runne awaye fere persecucyon saynt austayne sayth chyrche strengthed sufferynge persecucyon holdynge fals heresyes techynge men bounden faste lente maye eate flesshe good frydaye people bounden come goddes seruyce whytsondaye vpon shroue tuysdaye whyche daye though boundeu leue vndone thinges many men vse yet specyally bounden spende day dyuyne seruyse tother barn bablyng vpon abiuracyon chyrche dyd suffer persecucyon techyng frerys may wedde none breke theyr vowys runne apostasyand set nought periury rayle agaynst order holy relygyouse lyuyng thynges saynte austayne bryngeth hym full whole agaynste persecucyon uffered catholyke chyrche suffyseth men mynde gladly suffer whan necessyte sufferauce shall happen paynyms infydel ceace crystes chyrche yf suffer heretykes aryse remayne amonge selfe fy ste wyth false doctryne contende inquyete wyth rebellyon bete robbe spoyle kyll saynt poule sayth put away euyll man fro amonge selfe saynt austayne bryngeth hym dyd good longe delyberacyon playnely wryte thys poynt agaynst hym appereth expressely many hys pystles wryten bothe vnto secular power exhorted agaynste heretykes represse theym amende force also dyuerse heretykes selfe wherin declareth wherfore yet besyde thys chyrche doth dede abyde endure shamefull contumelyes wreched heretykes ashamed contumelyes crosse though blasphemouse wreches rayle agaynst ye crosse call idolatrye crepe kylle crosse place forbere caste fylthy myre vppon crosse yet ferther partes almayne thys knowe chyrche cryste hath many tymes suffered yet suffereth lytell persecucyon martyrdome bothe theyr goodes landes theyr bodyes yet sayth barn thys knowen chyrche wyse chyrche cryste bycause persecuteth heretykes profe therof alledgeth wordes saynt hylary wryten agaynst arryans whyche baron chyrche doth threten wyth banyshementes presonmentes compelleth men byleue whyche exiled caste preson nowe hangeth dyghyte felowshyppe whyche consecrated thretenynges persecuters causeth prestes flye encreaced chasyng away prestes gloryeth loued world whyche coulde neuer chrystes excepte worlde dyd hate c thynke lordes thynges layed arryans charge owne frendes ye owne conscyence muste nedes accuse thynges yet wyll u called chrystes child saye nothynge holy doctours laye vnto consyder well saynt hylaryes wordes shall fynd therin sorest thynge lyghtely could haue ben brought forth agaynst frere baron wordes appereth catholyke chyrche dyd neuer persecute heretykes temporall payne secular power vntyll heretykes began suche vyolence selfe yet saynte hylaryes dayes trewe catholyke chyrche dyd arrianes heretikes ye perceyue saynte hillary wordes hadde corrupted goten theyr secte great prynces vsed theyr authoryte agaynst catholikes bannishemetes prysonamet myche cruell handelynge whych good catholyque people suffred vsed none defence sauyng sworde word god cesuris chirch whyche holy clergy pronouced declared agaynste arrius adherentes holy counsayl holde nece afterwarde secte goodnes god abated right fayth well fully restored concorde reste quyete growen amonge chrysten people yet agayne heretikes beganne rayse new brabelynge good prynces remembryng great harme vnrestefulnesse growne heretykes brought vppe sectes scysmes chyrch cryste byfore dyd theyr good myndes preseruacyon peace prohybyte forbyd heresyes vpon certayne paynes lyke wyse comaunded bokes heretyques burned good men holy doctours wold haue ben gladde treate vse heretyques tenderly sholde haue hadde bodely harme myche holy saint austayne fyrst mynde hym selfe yet afterwarde consyderynge mater betser perceyued cotrary mych better mych harme growynge good men dyspleasure god yf yt shold contynue letted writyng confesse ouersyght reuoke fyrst opynyon onely cotente suche obstynate heretykes trouble good quyete people dysturbynge catholyque fayth wyth parell many pore symple soules wolde styrre suche scysmes heresyes sholde fere refrayned byforce repressed payne punyshed also requyred owne wrytyng seculare power ther thought benefyt heretyques self reduced theyr errours ryght fayth rather fayre payn temporall perseuere theyr heresy fall ye fyre perpetuall many fere force begynne good thynge trouble aduersyte fall grace encreased loue ye goodnes whyche theyr wanton welth hated vexacyon geueth vnderstandynge begynnynge wysedome feare god matth whyche bode apostle fere hym myght onely kyll ye bodye caste also soule hell stayne saynte austayne poynte declareth mynde playnly concernynge repressynge heretyques temporall punisheme pystles adressed vnto noble seculare men requyred therto also wrytynges wherin playnely declareth vnto heretyques selfes cause wherfore yt well done whych saue length wolde set saynte austayne mynde alone saynt hierome many holy men also vnto haue spyryte god weale crystedome crysten nacyons full whole agreed haue ben importune malyce heretyques raysynge rebellyons dyuerse regyons dreuen necessyte set sundry tymes sorer sorer punyshement therunto yet ye se strong deuyll theyr obstynate harte scantely suffyse yet layeth barn nother reason proue chyrche cryste knowen chyrche wyse sayth byleue chyrch cryst fayth yt artycle oure fayth therfore yt knowen chyrche knowen chyrche yt muste nedes chyrche vnknowen onely holy people pure clene wythout spotte wryncle chyrche muste nedes suche holy company pure clene without spot wrincle proueth thus barn marke saynt paules wordes crist hath geue hym self might make gloryouse clennesse thys holy chyrche mercy god towarde thorow chryste whose sake layeth nothynge charge ye yf person wold redy geue clennesse lette fayth clayme ryght hys purenesse owne betweyne theym comen betweyne man wyfe yf chyrche loke owne merytes workes full synne muste nedes saye dimitte mihi debita whyche neded saye yf hadde none yf referre selfe vnto merytes blessed husbande cryste iesus clennesse hath blood wythout spot reason stycketh fayth faste vnto husbande chryste doth abyde confessyon synne requyreth mercy theym therfore nothynge layed charge thynge y geuen therfore sayeth saynt paule y damnacyon vnto cryste iesu haue good reders somwhat touched wordes byfore ye se sayth chyrche hath alway synne alway spottes wryncles yet bycause stykketh faste vnto husbande chryste fayth abydeth confessyon synne requyreth mercy therfore nothynge layed vnto charge thynge forgeuen therfore hath neyther spot wryncle lefte proueth ye se saynte paule sayenge dampnacyon vnto cryste iesu haue sayde vnto barn byfore yet say agayn yt though crist hath saynt paule saith vnto ephesies gyuen hym self er myght make gloryouse yet ment saynt oule euery man criste hath geuen hym selfe make hym gloryouse shall dede gloryouse wyll forwardely refuse made gloryouse company yt shalbe gloryouse shall yet gloryouse world shall world gracyouse may nother worlde gloryouse yet euery tyme gracyouse world neyther tyme fall frowardely neglygetly grace stande longe suche vngracyouse state yet thorow goddes callyng tourne agayne wyllyngly grace vnto grace passe laste thorowe grace glory may crystes chyrch many yeres erth happely neyther gracyouse gloryouse yet may knowledge synyes aske mercy byleue euery artycle ryght fayth trust saued yet wylfull purpose cotynuynge horrible synnes stand styll dampnable state yt may shall amende saued may yt wyll neuer amende shall therfore fynally dampned yet though one cristes electes yet member mystycall body catholyque chyrche erth may byleue hym truste hym knowledge synne aske mercye lacke good purpose may mysse mercy baron make men wene onely fayth suffycyent saluacyon accordynge pestylent heresy whych dyd one forswere forsweryng hym selfe holdeth defendeth agayne telleth v gay tale gloryouse chyrch hath synnes forgeue styckynge spouse onely fayth wyth knowledgynge synnes aud askynge mercy man may bolde yf thus synne neuer fast purpose neuer litle amende layeth v falsely forth saynt poule telleth v saynt poule sayth damnacy criste iesu holy saynt paule holy chryste iesu yt good crysten reders ryght heuy herynge euer suche man shold herde speke among crysten peple holyly bryngeth wordes blessed apostle though ment make men loue cryst iesu malycyousely pulleth away wordis wherin weyght hangeth make men wene stycke god fayth alone wyth false hope saluacyon onely knowledgyng theyr synne askynge mercye su ycyent saue theyr soules doyng could neuer dampned though dyd howe euer purpose perseuer theyr synne besyde saynte poule reproue baron false doctryne sayth reherseth hym damnacyon cryste iesu sayth da nacyon cryste iesu walke fleshe declarynge playnely though cryste iesu suche maner beynge hym baron descrybeth v yet yf walke fleshe shall damned saynt poule sayth playnly yf ye lyue fleshe ye shall dye fleshe may walke fleshe may lyue yet frere barn sayth wordes chyrche doth speketh holy wordes nothynge leuynge synnefull wayes fleshe purpose eyther make men wene suche thynge neded onely byleue trust knowledge synne ke mercy byleue onely truste surely lyue styll lyste faith alone sticke crist barn wold haue seme synfull euer yet wythout synne clene pure cristes purenesse sayth thynges comune sayth among frendes therfore dapnacyon wyse cryst iesu euer lyue euer thus may ye se good chrysten people shamefully thys euyll chrysten man false yeth saynt poules wordes ye deceyte vnlerned folke dampnacyon good symple soulys worlde se laboreth cary reder away perceyuynge therof yet hath god made barn hym self blynd ye blynd goth make reder stumbleth vnware vppon trouth taketh vp bryngeth forth also sheweth hys owne shame folysshely neuer saw lyke lyfe lo wordes forth wyth vppon tother barn thys may playner wyll brynge saynt austayns wordes whych vexed donatystes wyth reason layd agaynst wordes whole chirch sayth forgyue v synnes wherfore hath spottes wryncles knowledgynge spottes weshed awaye chyrche abydeth prayour myghte clensed knowledgynge synnes longe lyue standeth shall departe body thynges forgyuen euery man wherfore thys meane chyrche god treasurer god withoute spotte wryncles therfore lyue without synne shal asse hence without synne c good chrysten reader haue herde frere barn saye wolde parte away make seme playner hys purpose therfore entent may make hys false handelyng saynt austayn fals entent therin appere playnely vnto haue redy made appere vnto lyke handelynge hys lyke entent handelynge saynte poule shall reherse saint austayns wordes lytell fully truely frere baron hath done begynnynge barn begynneth endyng endeth endeth wote nere maketh two lynys hys owne endeth wyth c shed hys bloud v ye faythfull people knowe wytnesse ye beare vnto bloud whych ye haue receyued trueth ye saye amen ye knowe thynge bloud hed many remissio synnys marke lo chyrche made wythout spotte wryncle streched strecher tenter hokys crosse chyrch well wesshed clensed may euer thys thynge doynge lorde doth exhybyte present vnto hym selfe gloryouse chyrch spotte wryncle goth aboute thys thynge doyng euyn exhybyteth man sayth let v haue neyther spot wryncle great goth goth aboute well cunnyngest wurke man strecheth v vpon crosse maketh v smoth wythout wryncle weshed made clene without spotte yt came wythout spot wrincle stretched vpon strecher ye tenter hokys yt sake hym self make v wythout spot wryncle let v therfore pray make v whe hath done tha bryng v ye shoppys lay v vp shalbe pressyng strecchyng thou spakest thus art thou without spot wricle dost thou chyrche whyche sayth forgyue v synnys confesseth hath styll synnys forgyuen confesse foloweth therfore haue synnes bycause amonge turkes sarasyns chrysten men longe chrysten whych agre knowen chyrche chrysten contynued nacyons fayth folke thys knowen chyrche also ouer whan euer contreys vnchrystened nowe shall truste onys catholyque chyrche vnknowen chyrch onely good folke pure clene eyther spotte wryncle maner synne wolde make v wene saynte austayne therfore wrote word agaynst ye donatistes proue agaynst chyrche erth vnknowen chyrche onely suche holy sayntes wythoute synne proue frere barn maketh v ly poynt ye shall vnderstande good reders saynt austayne spake wordes agaynst donatistes agaynste sectes heretyques synne goeth saynt austayne farther sayth suche chyrche therfore lyue wyhoute synne gete forgeuenes knoweledgynge theyr synne askynge mercy prayour fayth co trycyon hert vnfayned terys flowynge fro man lyueth clene long lyueth spotteth hym selfe agayn caccheth euer wryncles lyueth neuer wythout longe necessyte nature peraduenture thorow wylfull fraylty neglygence sheweth farther yet synnes wythout whyche man lyueth meaneth abomynable dedely synnes maslaughter aduoutry suche horryble dedely synnes sle soule one stroke suche synnes crysten men sayth haue good fayth good hope wyll commytte uecessarye trouth full hope wytte great stronge truste cryste saued criste yet good fayth able make man good bycause yt barn fayth witte onely fayth without well workynge charyte good hope bycause saynt austayne meaneth none otherwyse declare hym ye may well perceyue yf ye well aduyse wordes whych haue truely traslated yet bycause ye shall lesse doute therof saint austayn shall self declare truely declare place playn wordes nother place xxxii sermon wordes apostle augustinus de verbis apost serm lo thus sayth man ought doute wyth prayours chyrch wyth holsome sacryfyce wyth almoyse geuen soules departed holpe mercyfully delt wyth lorde theyr synnes haue deserued thynge tradycyon olde father whole catholyque chyrche obserueth y wyt tyme deceaced communyon blood cryste tyme sacryfyce theyre place order remebraunce made pray ur shold made onely also specyall rehersall shold made sacryfyce offerd vp workes mercy done commendacyon fauoure theym doute holpen therwyth syth prayour made vnto god frutelesse wyse dowted thynges succour releue deceaced onely suche men saye haue lyued theyr deth thynges maye theym good theyr deth relyefe departed body wythout fayth workynge wyth cheryte nd wythout sacramentes suche deades deuocyon vayne vsed pledge erneste peny whyche deuocyon lacked whyle lyued ether bycause wold receyue grace god bycause receyued vayne treasurynge layenge vp selues mercy wrath wherfore whe good worke done deceaced theyr louers frendes meryte newe thynges gyuen rewarde thynges consequent well folowynge vppon theyr merytes whyche deserued whyle lyued sayd thynges shold helpe onely whyle lyue deade therfore euery man endeth thys lyfe thynge receyue onely whyche hath deserued beynge lyue another place sayth thus thyng euer venyall synnys redemed v must purged wyth fyre august serm de aia u de u rum whyche apostle sayth worke shall appere fyre yf mannes wurke burne shall suffer losse eyther whyle lyue thys worlde labour selfe wyth penaunce ellys truely bycause god wyll suffereth punysshed wyth many trybulacyons synnys yf gyue thankes vnto god delyuered whyche thynge thys wyse yf oure husbande oure wyfe oure sonne dye yf substauce whyche loue shold taken v though loue chryste aboue substaunce yf nede wolde rather l se substaunce denye chryste yet bycause haue afore sayd yf loue substaunce shold whyle lyue dye lese wythout greate sorowe yet yf lese gyue thankes good chyldren vnto god whych mercyfull father suffereth substauce taken fro v yf wyth humylyte confesse suffer lesse punyshment haue deserued synnys suche wyse purged thys worlde worlde come fyre purgatory fynde eyther thynge ryght lytell burn yf neyther thanke god trybulacyon bye synnys good workes shal longe abyde fyre purgatory tyll venyall synnys aboue named consumed vp wode hey stubblys man wyll saye force longe abyde maye last go euerlastyng lyfe let man say thus moste welbeloued bretherne fyre purgatory sharpe payne yt thys worlde sene thought felt c lo good chrysten reders ye maye clerely se saynt austayns wordes mente deny purgatory affermeth playnely syth sayeth dowt prayour almoyse dede oblacyon holy sacryfyce offred masse maketh soulys departed mercyfully delt wythall theyr paynes releued whyche fewe wordes saynt austayn wytnesseth agaynst mo theyr esyes one onely affermeth purgatory agaynst yong father fryth affermeth also almoyse dede prayour maye releue soulys therin ouer techeth v agaynst newe sectes good wurkes merytoryouse onely hym selfe doth also folke yet ouer techeth v maye meryte deserue thys lyfe yt folkes good dedes may meryte v serue v whan dede foloweth also syth maye praye soules haue nede maye also praye v whyche haue yet nede present peyne te porall auoydynge perpetuall syth soynt iamys sayth iac bi orate pro inuicem vt sal emini saynte austayne affermeth also blessed body bloude cryste masse sacryfyce oblacyon god agaynst luther hys adherentes fynally techth v tradycyon father comune obseruaunce custume catholyke chyrche certyfycacyon trouth sure vndowted authoryte good chrysten reders yf ye lyke take myche labour rede saynt austayns wordes agayne wyse barn reherseth hys boke co pare wyth hys wordes dede haue trewly translated ye shall merueyle mych se wylynesse hath vsed therin yet lacke wyt therwith barn hath ye maye se taken pecys saynt austayne pached theym gyther wyth worde twayne hys owne bytwene thoughe wordes laye gyther text reherseth leueth waye chyefe poynte whyche saynt austayne excepteth forgyuenesse theyr deth haue ded ly synne saye yt dye therin barn leueth come poynt le sholde se whyche forgyuen clene theyr deth muste vse suche wayes therto euery man suffycyently vseth soone clene forgyuen yet dyeth state grace shall layd vp last pure gold treasure god shall furnace fyre purgatory purely fyned fyrst also saynt austayne hauynge hys whole wordes well vnderstanden sayth euery suche man chyrche dyeth dedely synne wyth helpe god vertue crystes passyon faythfull prayour cont ycyon great heuynesse harte wyth dylygence vsed auoydynge synne doynge good vertuouse workes hys lyfe shall hys deth fully forgyuen layed vp pure golde treasure god frere barn reherseth wordes wise though saynt austayne sayed euery man chyrche wythout excepcyon sholde passe hense pure clene forthwyth go god though man thys chyrch coulde dye dedely synne wherof saynt austayne wordes quae talia habebat vt dimiterentur declareth playnely contrary barn also concludeth wherfore thys meane chyrche god treasure god without spotte wryncle whyche wordes wha redde sowned vnto myne vnderstandyng haue many know haue redde chyrche treasure goddes foreknowledge predestynacyon alwaye pure clene saynte austayne sayth meneth many chyrch forgyuen thoughe many forgyuen bycause lette theyr forgyuenesse self lacke dew desyrynge yet shall whan layed vp pure golde goddes treasory one good shoppys shall neuer tryall pressynge strechynge put vnto barn leueth also wordes saynte austayne god moste cunnynge wu keman goth aboute clensynge spottes stretchyng wryncles dylygently yet thys world course oure lyfe alwaye doynge hath fully done tyll parte hense deth wordes saynt austayne whyche baron leueth purposely leueth ere come theym playne full agre wyth exposycyon gaue thys boke agaynst barn saynt po lys wordes barn brought hym men loue wiues cryste loued chyrche hath gyuen hym selfe myghte sanctyfye clense fou tayne water thorow word lyfe make hym selfe wythout spotte wryncle thyng myghte holy wythout blame uppon whyche wordes barn sayth haue lo trewe chyrche cryst pure clene neyther hath spotte wryncle wordes saynt poule partely told hym proue thynge hys purpose saynt poule sayeth cryste gaue hym selfe make sayth shall make euery parte saue heue hath sanctyfyed baptysme lyke wyse though god wolde euery man saued whych wyt yf euery man wolde hym selfe yet bycause many men theyr owne frowardnesse wyll walke dapnacyon god wyll wrestle wyth saue spyght theyr teth bycause consydereth hym selfe able lyue wythout though haue gyuen hym selfe hys chyrch make gloryouse wythout spotte wryncle wolde haue euery man come part hys chyrch saued hym lerne trouth wolde sayth thapostle euery man sholde saued come knowledge trouth thimot yet many men wyll neuer come iewys turkes sarasyns many haue come haue agayne gone fro haue luther huyskyn suinglius lamkert huchyn baron many great herety ues mo many man abydeth tyll dyenge day byleueth trewe doctryne yet bycause wyll byleue yt well workynge folowe yt wyll wythout dew repentaunce dye dedely synne departeth deth vncurable roten member easte conclusyon vppon dyuyls dounghyll hell member chyrche wyll worke well remayne wyth frere baron fayth alone god shall make theym gloryouse wythoute spot wryncle saynte austayne sayth though theyr instante prayour goth styll aboute yt alway pray therfore doyng yt alway washyng alway stretchyng yet parte intermyssyon theyr prayeng part theyre contynuall new bespottynge wrynclynge neuer endeth yt byfore theyr dyeng day chyrch erth euen beste men therof pure clene alway wythout eyther spotte wryncle agaynste say te austaynes wordes barn bosteth hym selfe proue wordes apostle though clerely proued yt ayth haue lo trew chyrch crist pure clene yt neyther hath spot wryncle yt world se barn boste place endeth saynte anstaynes wordes wyth clene contrary sentence agaynste owne parte concludeth whole mater quyte agaynst hym selfe vtterly destroyeth owne chyrche wenynge pullynge downe settynge vp bosteth myche therof ende lo thus sayth therfore e lyue wythout synne shall passe hense wythout synne c lo wordes baron owne wryten thought saynt austaynes wyth c bryngeth vppon owne c wordes folowyng haue clerely chyrche god clensed puryfyed cryste knowledgyng synnes lettynge passe saynte austayne sayth whole chyrche cryste passeth se withoute synne euery man one chyrch shall chyrche heuen let v take frere baron owne wordes though wolde haue seme wordes saynt austayne hym selfe none wyse ment neyther saynt austayne barn wolde haue theym taken let v se fyrste sayth frere baron sayth saynt frere austayne barn fyrst frere baron bosteth sayth haue clerely chyrche god clen ed puryfyed cryste knowledgynge synnes aske frere barn whych chyrch questyon chyrch cryst erth chyrche cryste heuen frere barn muste nedes graunte mater chyrch betwene hym v chyrche criste erthe wyll aske hym whyther mater men lyuynge men dyenge syth speke chyrch doctryne chyrche suppose frere barn wyll graunt speketh chyrch men lyuyng quycke quethynge whyle may speke talke confesse byleue meaneth speke theym onely whyle lye dyenge spechelesse geuynge vp goost well ye perceyue nowe frere baron sayth whyche chyrche bos eth sayth se clerely god clenseth purifyeth chyrch knowledging synnes whyche chyrche yt sayth clene pure wythout spot wryncle se meaneth chyrch erth lyuynge good helth whyche men haue trew doctryne bycause ye chyrch yt sayth erre syth se sayth frere barn let v se sayth frere saynt austayne barn sayth ye wote wel ye chyrch shal passe hense wythout synne yt treasours god wythout spot wryncle sayth yt lyueth wythoute synne lo good crysten reders sawe euer man geue self fowle fal frere barn hath done whyche goynge proue v chyrch cryst lyuynge erth company holy pure clene without spot wryncle synne bryngeth saint austayne whose wordes altered framed frere baron owne fashyon playnely declare shew chyrch cryst whyle yt lyueth erth lyueth withoute synne therfore neuer pure clene wythoute spottes wryncles synne thus barn sayd ye begynnyng wold bryng saynt austayne proue purpose playn semeth rather brynge saynte austayne wyth playn wordes proue frere barn fole specyally syth seeth yet fowle fall hath whyle lyeth myre tumbled dyrte holdeth vppe fowle sleue bosteth clenly cote hath pure clene wythout spot wryncle saynte peter could fynd one droppe durte theron hath shamfully loste chyrch onely good holy people vnknowen clene pure wyth spot wryncle yet chyrche muste nedes vnknowen chyrche onely good holy men leste though somwhat wryncled vtterly spottelesse wyse knowen chyrch wyll frere barn weneth well substancially proue though proue owne promyseth yet wyll proue yt oures neyther ware therfore sayth barn suche chyrch muste nedes though carnall yie se fleshely reason iudge wherfore byleue artycle fayth holy chyrche communyon felyshyppe holy men knowe yt seynge felynge felyshyppe draper mercer yt none artycle fayth nowe let v argue lyke false iew myght haue sayd crystes dayes whyle preached hierusalem byleue cryste must artycle fayth ergo cryste must person vnknowen perceyued carnall yie onely byleued fayth seyng felyng men know draper mercer thus myghte dayes false iew haue argued cryste hadde ben cryste bycause knowen person argument maner made false iewes dede sayde iohn knowe man whense cryste cometh man shall know whense yt myght haue answered criste fayth byleued yet also syght felyng knowe well wyse knowe draper mercer eyther false iewes knew hym tone meane onely trew discyples knew hym saynt thomas inde hadde sene hym felt hym dyd syght felynge know manhed iohan therewyth fayth byleued godhed euen know chyrche syghte herynge felynge know draper mercer byleue spyryt god abydynge therwyth ledynge yt trouthe han cryste chyefe hedde therof assystyng yt preseruyng yt faylynge agaynste gate hell matth byleue yt one chyrche professyon baptysme holyly dedecated vnto god seuered openly knowe manyfold open sectes heretyques comen crede sayth dayly songe masse byleue one holy apostolyke chyrche whyche worde apostolyque wherfore yt putte frere baron wyll hym selfe yt semeth lette confesse though tyndale wyll agree yt byleue communyon felyshyp suche folke halowed dedycated vnto god euer worlde agreynge gether knowe catholyque bylyefe bothe knowen beleued holy catholyque chyrche cryste also byleue communyon sayntes nother maner besydes wyt byleue lyue chyrche chyrch also dye catholyque fayth state grace shall thys lyfe haue communyon felyshyp sayntes byfore departed heuen lyued tyme knowen catholyque chyrche dyed knowen catholyque fayth yf frere baron aske proue seme sette mych hym lo therfore wordes saynte austayne augus sermone vigilia penthecostes ye must knowe ought byleue chyrch byleue chyrche chyrche god house god catholyque chyrch calleth chyrch spred abrode thorowe hole worlde chyrches heretyques whych dyuerse called catholyke vnyuersall chyrches conteyned euery secte proper place owne prouynce catholyque chyrche spred abrode wyth shynyng lyght one fayth rysyuge vppe sonne goyng downe greater rychesse greater treasure greater honour greater substauce thys world catholyke fayth whych saueth synfull men gyueth blynde theyr syght agayne healeth syke whych also chrysteneth new come chrysten relygyon iustyfyeth faythfull repayreth penitentes increaceth ryghteouse folke crowneth martyr giueth order ye clergy cosecrateth prestes prepareth v kyngdome heuyn maketh v felowes coparteners holy angel euerlastynge inherytaunce euer maner man euer chrysten man yt chyrche cryst truely onely chyrch whyche lord gladly receyueth sacryfyce onely maye wythout dystrust herd make intercessyo wandered way whyche cause also lorde comaunded sacryfyce pascall lambe sayeng ye shall eate one house onely ye shall beare part flesshe forth dores matth lambe eaten one house bycause trew hoost redemar offred vp one catholyke chyrch onely whose flesh god comaunded forbade part shold borne ye dores forbydeth v gyue holy thyng dogges thys chyrch onely good worke frutefully done therfore none receyued reward peny onely yt labored within vyne yerde matth onely kepeth strong bonde cheryte kepe selfe within thys cause truely water noyes flode caryed arke vp ye hyghar place destroyed many foud wythout arke onely chyrch whych maye veryly byholde heuenly mysteryes therfore sayth lord moyses haue place thou shalt stand vpon rocke exodi soone shall take away hand thou shalt se backe halfe bycause trewth perceyued sene onely catholyke chyrch therfore sayth lorde hath place may sene moyses set vpo rocke byholde goddes fygure except holde kepe sure faste grounde fayth dyscerne knowe dyuyne presence dysseuer sayth saynt cypryan sonne beame frome whole body sonne vnyte lyghte receyueth dyuysyon breke braunche tree soone one broke budde cut awaye ryuer heed anone dryeth vp wordes cypryan perceyue lyght receyueth dyuisyo holy men predestynate vnto kyngdome god whyche maner wyse dyuyded chyrch hat braunche broken tree lenger budde vnderstande buddyng euerlastynge lyfe dryeng vp ryuer cut cundytte heed wyse vnderstand voyde empty holy goste deuyded vnyte felowshyp sayntes say let v holde selfe comunyon felowshyp hope wyth sayntes whych deceaced thys fayth whyche haue receyued therfore yf wyll haue felowshyppe wyth sayntes euerlastyng lyfe let v thynke vpon folowyng must recognyse fynde v theyr vertues thentent may voucesaufe pray v vnto lord yf beare tormentes whyche sayntes suffred euyn death yet leste wyse lette v theyr prayour interce syos fyghte agaynst concupyscences neyther abraam isaac iacob put death yet merites fayth iustyce deserued chy fly honoured amonge patryarkes whose feast gathered euery man founde faythfull ryghteouse laudable therfore derest bretherne though suffer suche thynge bondes strypes presonment none bodyly tormetes persecucyon men ryghteousnes sake yet maye able obteyne felowshyp sayntes yf labour chastyce body make subiect yf accustome seluys pray vnto lord humble spyryte cotryte soule yf endeuour selfe take wyth peaceable mynde spyghtes done vnto v neyghbour yf cotende stryue wyth selfe loue hate v v wrong good pray gladly theyr lyfe well fare wyth vertue pacyence frutes good workes garnysshed made gaye yf conuersacyo yf also accordyng sayeng apostle exhibyte bodyes lyuely hoost holy pleasau vnto god shal gyfted wyth heuely honour may one glory rewarded wyth yt lordes sake gaue theyr mebres deth lyke wyse theyr deth precyouse syghte lorde let lyfe shall worthy also entre place cytye aboue amonge companyes blessed martyr render vnto oure redemer vowys thankes lo haue ye herde good chrysten reders saynte austayn vnderstandeth expowneth sanctam ecclaesia catholicam holy catholyke chyrche also sanct rum communionem comunyon felesshyppe sayntes wherby frere barn maye se yf byleue saynt austayn wold seme tha owne fonde imagynacyo quayled whyche divyneth hys dyuynite wordes sanctorum communione sharpely prycke ye clergye sayth place thys maner barn chyrche erre onely vniuersall chyrche whych called communyon felyshyppe sayntes whyche addycyon made holy father saynt cyprianes tyme mencyo lykelyhed declare presumpcyon certayne men certayne congregacyons rekened selfe holy chyrch wherfore lordes se well leste holy goste haue prycked thys addycyon haue alwayes made selfe holy chyrche ye without holynesse hath neuer bene holynesse whole spyrytualtye holy father barn sayth added crede sanctorum comunione holy carnall father well baron sake dare saye none suche father father frere luther father frere huyskyn byget chyldren nonnes thys suffyseth agaynst frere barn ye perceyue saynt austayn frere barn fonde inuencyon fayled wordes saynt austayne ye se also frere barn hys gay bable wherwyth wolde make men leue chyrche chyrche yf suffre persecucyon man myghte come heuen trewe chrysten man yf persecuted lo good reders besydes greate persecucyon vnto chyrche ryghte greate gryefe heuynesse se many membres waxe roten fall away body incurable canker false fe tered heresyes also sore persecuted bothe body goodes false heretyques dyuers partes almayne yet se ferther fore rehersed wordes thynge tolde persecucyon suffyseth suffre wha necessyte put vnto men neyther bounden go seke suffer euyl folke amonge selfe contagyon maye corrupte great many whyche growen onys great nomber may fall vnto rebellyon persecute cuntrey saynt austayn sheweth well clerely persecucyon yf haue wolde god plentuousely parte haue good cherytable wurkes wyth catholyke fayth hym selfe reherseth may good chrysten men membres onely chyrche erth whyche maye communyon fayth though good wurkes want also ye chyrche heuen ouer good chrysten reader ye se saynt austayne wordes doth playnely shew sayntes whyche redy heuen praye v erthe whyche thynge heretyques wyll wyse agre se also wordes sanctam ecclaesiam catholica whyche frere barn wolde make v wene holy catholyke chyrche secrete vnknowen chyrche scatered worlde sayn austayn well playnely declareth yf consyder well hys wordes must nedes thys comune knowen catholyke chyrche haue playnely confuted frere baron saynte austayne hym selfe whose order rule frere barn professed whose wordes often alledgeth hys purpose alwaye prouynge agaynste hys purpose wyll frere barn ferther wurshyp confute hym selfe place saynt austayne whyche hym selfe bryngeth forth hys specyall profe hys vnknowe holy chyrch proue company vnknowen faythfull folke beynge holy theyr onely fayth wherof ar frere barn wordes barn thys well preued owne law de con di c prima igitur whose wordes therfore chyrche holy bycause byleueth ryghtuousely god frere barn goth forth glose vpon wordes sayth heare cause wherfore chyrche holy bycause byleueth ryghtuousely god byleueth nothynge hym byleueth heareth worde hys mayster cryste bereth wytnesse shepe heare voyce nother mannys voyce knowe baron holdeth olde crafte furnyshyng owne gloses wyth falsefyenge scrypture god ye shall vnderstande good crysten reders saynt iohn euangelyste io oute whose gospell baron hath taken wordes sauyoure cryste reherseth theym suche wyse barn doth wyt shepe cryste know voyce man sayth ye shepe cryst folow straunger fle hym bycause know voyce strau gers cometh baron telleth v cryst sayde shepe knowe voyce man though chyrch sholde refuse wordes onely criste spake owne person cryste sayde sholde none sholde heare straungers men whome estewe fle thus ye se good reader fere barn false fyeth wronge interpreteth wordes cryste gospell saynte iohn let v retourne consyder wordes lawe baron hath rehersed whyche haue ben ye se lytle letted eyther spot wryncle ow yt though saynt bernarde shold proue ba ons chyrche yet wolde frere baron hat saynt bernard old proue chyrch lest vnknowe chyrch onely good folke proue knowe catholyque chyrche chyrch arns trouthe felowes myghte dysproue destroy chyrche care greatly akynge nother yet wolde frere baron farther saynte bernarde sholde seme dyspyse set nought holy ornamen nd call harlottes deckyng eanes dyspyse holy ceremon e chyrche ut shall shew good reders yrst saynt ber proueth nothynge frere barn agaynste owen cathol u chyrche though wo de ere arns reherseth shew ba n playth saynt bernard ye haue sene hym play wyth saynt austayn wyth saynt poule saynt iohn euangelyst wytte reherse hym false chaun e wordes kepe wordes away make mate swete fynally shall shew ye saynt bernarde thys heresy onely cocernynge quest whych chyrche also frere barn heresyes specyall enemy wyll make n ende fyrste poynt yf saynt bernarde sa frere barn reherseth hym yet ayde frere barn concernynge chyrch wo de amo euery kynd chyrch nought den eth tha sayth also suche serue chryste chryste sayth nay th euyll folke rue god well dothe euery man agre th euyll chrysten peple theyr dedely synnes ser th deuyll frere baron wyll thynge proue v bernarde muste shewe saynte berna de th suche euyll chyrche sheweth v suche worde myghte bernarde many holy man aye word yet meane suche thynge th rby saye sermon monke b eketh y hys vowes neyther monk man mych wurse iew mean th lenger monke dede member monastery wolde saye wo n keth obedy ce husband wyf husband therfore dyscharged may take wyfe sayth dronk n woman sowe meaneth therby perd chyldren shalbe pyggys prophete speketh person selfe wurme man yet ment deny dede vyle maner hadeled passyon thou man vile wurme man giueth meate drynke w stelth seruyc th ster ye secretely somtyme agayns therfore ou sauy ur sayd maysters ayd man yf haue twayne whyle serueth tone shall leue tother vnserued therfore though saynt bernarde saye serue antechryste serue deuyll yf sayed also therfore seruautes cryste chrysten menne chrystes enemyes antechrystes yet ment thys yt thys oute chyrche none whyle agayn whan ame ded agayn soone synned agayne thus playe lyke docke netle man sholde wyt whan whan knowe whych chyrche thus haue shewed good reders though saynt bernard sayd dede barn falsely reherseth ye somwhat yet ued barn secunde poynt ye shall vnderstand baron hath vntruely translated saynt bernardes wordes lettynge passe peces hath lefte myddes cause ca se yf lacke lernynge lettynge passe suche also hath mysse translated ignoraunce wyll shewe one place twayne whyche hath wyth one word twayne chaunged malyce hath turned sentence hys purpose clene agaynste mynde saynte bernarde wrote euyn fyrst begynnynge saynt bernarde sayth thus ministri christi sunt seruiunt antichristo mynystres cryste serue antichryst barn hath translated thus call selfe mynistres cryst serue antichrist saynte bernard sayth though serue antichryste yet mynystres cryst hys chyrche frere barn turneth way maketh though saynt bernarde sayd sayd onely call selfe lyke wyse ende saint bernard sayth pro huiusmodi volut esse sunt ecclesiaru ppositi thynges wyll ruler chyrches deanys archdekyns c barn hath translated thus thinges wyll ruler chyrch dekyns archdekyns c wordes leueth though sait bernard sayd ruler chyrch onely sayth yt wold whan hath suche wyse falsely translated saynt bernarde make hym seme saye lyeth alowd sayth vnto hym selfe lo saynt bernarde saith neyther chyrche chyrch wherof ye se saynt bernarde sayeth playne wordes contrary whych playne wordes saynt berua de frere barn hath ye playnely se playne pure malyce manyfestely falsely chauged euer yt lerned rede ye sermo saynt bernard shall euydentely se saynt bernarde calleth chyrche cryst comune knowe catholyke chyrche none vnknowen chyrche lamenteth estate chyrche whyche calleth also body cryste wherby ye maye se speketh chyrche cryste erthe sheweth thys chyrche hath bene dyuerse tymes dyuersely vexed fyrste paynyms neuer secundely heretykes whyche went thyrdely noughty folke euyl ruler styll go whome sayth wordes baron hathe falsely translated fourthly good men therof also whyche abydynge therin beynge also styll therof yet somtyme begyled subtyll slayght ye wyly deuyll vnder colour goynge farre better thynge thys processe iiii vexacyons chyrche saynt bernarde bryngeth vppon wordes prophete tim n c urno sagitte volantis die negocio perambulantis tenebris ab incursu et demonio meridiano assygnynge euery one iiii vexacyons one foure kyndes deuyls whyche whole processe together lerned rede shall se barn heresye concernynge chyrch full playne ouerthrowen shall playnely se saynt bernarde barn bryngeth proue euyll folke none chyrche cryst onely good holy folke declare expressely chyrche cryste whyche calleth body cryste whole nomber good bad dyuers lyuynge yet one bylyefe whych one chyrch chyrches heretykes departed barn also sayth saynt bernarde calleth holy ornamentes harlattes deckyng game player dysguysynge though saynt barnarde dyd hym selfe doth ocke scorne halowynge copy vestymentes chalyces ornamentes vsed ye chyrch dyuyne seruyce whych kynd halowed thynges frere barn mockage scorne accompteth amonge prophane thynges ioyneth gyther lefe hys boke nexte bokes belly candels chalyces oyle crysme holy water wyth horse howndes goodly ge e hym make though saynt bernarde sayd ye thyng abomynable whych cause thentent ye maye clerely know farre saynt bernard fauorynge frere baron heresyes shall gyue playne sample twayne saynt bernard lykeneth apostatas vnto traytour iudas serm super ersu ter psalm wolde frere baron spyed brought v forthe place lykeneth vnto iudas onely apostatas cast theyr habytes ronne rouers frere barn doth iudas dyd ye maudy also relygiouse folke yt apostatas theyr mynde yet byde styll theyr habyte theyr cloyster bycause runne theyr cloyster cast theyr habyte fere worldly shame whyche wordes saynt bernard ye maye good reders perceyue suche apostasy wrechyd dayes wyth mych people lytell estemed saynt bernardes tyme amonge chrysten people thynge shamefull abomynable whyche el wolde fayne haue rune relygyon thought selfe fyre almoste ye whyle therin yet durste rune shame sholde haue hadde loke man face sa nt bernarde also detestynge suche apostasy pestylent heresyes whyche apostatas comely falle wryteth vnto hildefonsus erle tolowse agaynste one henry apostata runne relygyon corruptynge cuntrey wyth many suche poysened heresyes apostatas thentet ye may better fully perceyue goodnes saint bernarde thys mater hys frutefull labour payne taken honour god profyte chrysten people god agaynewarde wyth many great open myracles alowed approued agaynst sayd henry frere barn double brother wytte well heresye apostasy shall reherse somwhat mater story vertuouse holy man tyme thynge done wryten lyfe saynt bernard partes tolouse one whose name henry tyme moke lewd apostata vngracious lyuynge pernycyouse doctryne persuasyble wordes hadde tourned wauerynge people countrey thapostell foresayde certayne folke lyued hypocrysye lyed made merchaundyse false fayned wordes manyfeste enymy chyrche derogatynge vnreueretly bothe holy sacramentes mynysters hadde preuayled myche malyce reuerent father saint bernard wrytyng hym prynce tolouse amonges thynges sayeth euery almoste went men myght fynde chyrches wythout people people wythout prestes prestes wythoute dewe reuerence fynally chrysten men wythout cryste lyfe cryst shyt fro baby cryste folke whyle grace baptysme denyed prayours mocke oblacyons mennys soules prayenge sayntes sentece excomunycacyon pylgrimage faythfull folke byeldynge chyrches sparynge bodely worke holy dayes consecratynge holy creme oyle fynally maner ordinaunces chyrche set nought necessyte holy man often therunto instantely requyred cryste folke countrey laste toke iournay persuaded brought therunto reuerente father god albericus byshoppe hostyens legate see apostolyque came thyther receyued people wyth incredyble deuocyon though angell comen downe vnto theym heuen longe myght tary wyth man able kepe bakke thronge people hym great multytude theym came hym dayly nyghtly callyng vppon hym blessynge helpe yet preached certayne dayes cytye tolouse suche place wreche haunted moste greuousely hadde infected many symple soule fayth place saynte bernarde instructed strengthed wauerynge reuokynge theym erred settynge vppe agayne ouerthrowen ouer throwynge kepynge vnder anthoryte subuerters obstynate whome ouerthrewe repressed suche wyse neyther durste resyste myche appere shewe selfe yt though heretyke fled hadde hyd hym selfe yet way suche wyse stopped patthes byset scant coulde lurke sure place last taken faste bounde brought byshoppe iourney saynt bernarde god said seruaut gloryfyed many myracles whyle called bak harte theyr wycked errours also cured dyuerse disease theyr bodyes place countrey called sarlate sermon fynyshed brought many louis brede seruaunt god custome euery halowed whyche louys brede lyft vppe hande name god blessed theym wyth sygne crosse sayde vnto people shall ye knowe thynges whych tell trew thynges whyche heretyques tell false yf ye se syke folke haue tasted brede cured reuerent father byshoppe carnotenses great famouse man byshoppe galfryde ther present nexte man god somwhat ferenge leste myracle curynge shold fall vpon euery syke man sholde eate brede sayde vnto peple syke folke shall fynde helpe eate brede good fayth saint bernard nothyng doutynge powre lorde answered thynge wolde haue sayde veryly euer taste therof shall cured thentent may therby know trewe trewe messangers god great nomber syke people tastynge brede recouered tydynges thereof publyshed prouynce holy man retournynge place nere aboute intolerable concurse people fayne turne waye tered go thyther good crysten reders may ye perceue holy saynte bernard wyth whose wordes frere baron though saynt bernard specyall patrone proudly maketh ende peuyshe processe full open playne agaynst hym whole heresyes man wolde meruayle frere barn wytte brought hym fyrste haue sene wordes saynt bernarde whyche barn bryngeth newe framed hym selfe falsely forged owne auauntage playnly make agaynst purpose bryngeth ye se farther saynt bernarde also enymy baron heresyes onely dyd preache agaynst selfe heresyes baron nowe setteth forth dyd also proue false fayth catholyque chyrch trew manyfolde open myracles fynally baron reproueth chyrch persecutyng heretykes ye se holy saynt bernarde whome barn specyally bryngeth parte dyd playnely pursew theym laboured theyr punyshement hym selfe farther haue shewed saynt bernard selfe processe whych frere barn hath pycked falsefyeth wordes bryngeth doth playnely frere baron confusyon pryncypall purpose chyrche declare make open trew chyrche cryste mystycall bodye erth secrete vnknowen chyrche frere baron goth aboute make yt seme oute questyon one comen well knowen catholyke chyrche crysten nacyons byfore haue specyfyed left gether stocke vnite knowen catholyque fayth dystyncte dyuyded manyfolde wythered braunches many soundry scysmys sectes begynnyng vnto wreched dayes haue wyth obstynate malyce wylfully fallen therfro wyse good crysten reders ende thys boke agaynste frere baron euyll vncrysten processe wherwyth agaynste promyse cryste matth deuyll labour vayne pull downe crystes chyrche thus endeth viii boke
